# Changelog

All notable changes to this project will be documented in this file.

The format is based on [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/),
and this project adheres to [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/).

## [Unreleased]

### Fixed

- [#1603] **ADR-048 SPEC 1 (FR-013/FR-014)**: PyCharm-style numeric array viewer for the generic `core.array.basic` previewer. The previous viewer rendered a plain numeric matrix as a normalized grayscale PNG `<img>` (the user inspecting, e.g., a 100×100 correlation matrix saw a gray blob, never the numbers), clipped negatives to black via `max(0, min(255, int(v/max*255)))` so signed data (correlation / z-score / diff arrays) was corrupted, offered a fake colormap dropdown that applied a no-op `filter: saturate(1.4)`, and exposed only a single slice slider for high-D arrays (all other axes pinned at 0, most of the array unreachable). **Backend** (`src/scistudio/previewers/data_access.py`, `fallbacks.py`): `PreviewDataAccess.array_plane` now returns the actual (bounded, downsampled) numeric `matrix`, the finite `vmin`/`vmax` of the displayed plane (NaN/inf ignored, negatives preserved — new `_finite_extent`), and a `slice_axes` descriptor (new `SliceAxis`) for every non-displayed axis; it accepts `axis_indices: dict[int,int]` so each extra axis is independently selectable (the bounded single-plane read still touches exactly one face — `_read_bounded_plane` generalized to per-axis selectors, SC-004 preserved). `array_previewer` reads the per-axis `axis_indices` query field (new `_coerce_axis_indices`, tolerant of JSON string keys), emits `matrix`/`vmin`/`vmax`/`slice_axes` as the primary payload, and retains the grayscale `src` ONLY for the legacy `GET /api/data/{ref}/preview` compatibility adapter (FR-008). **Frontend** (`frontend/src/components/DataPreview.parts/coreViewers.tsx`): `ArrayViewer` renders the displayed plane as a table of the real numeric values (`ArrayHeatmapTable`), each cell heatmap-colored by a real colormap (`heatmapColor`: diverging blue→white→red centered at 0 for signed data so negatives are distinct and never black, sequential teal otherwise; non-finite cells transparent), a min..max value-scale legend (`ArrayLegend`), and one index picker (slider + numeric input) per non-displayed axis wired through `onPatchQuery({ axis_indices, slice_index })` so an N-D array is fully navigable. The fake `saturate(1.4)` colormap and the `<img>` raster path are removed from the generic viewer (rich image-domain LUT/OME stays the imaging package previewer's job, out of scope). Bounded budgets in `PreviewDataAccess` (row/col/byte/dim) are unchanged; large planes still downsample and surface `truncated`. Tests: `tests/previewers/test_preview_data_access.py` (per-axis selection, signed-extent-not-clipped, all-NaN extent), new `tests/previewers/test_fallback_array.py` (provider payload contract + `axis_indices` passthrough), new `frontend/src/components/DataPreview.parts/coreViewers.test.tsx` (numeric table renders real values, signed cells non-black, legend min/max, per-axis selectors patch `axis_indices`). (@claude, 2026-06-11, branch: feat/adr-048-array-viewer)
- [#1609] Stop git hooks from corrupting the shared `.git` across worktrees, and unbreak `git commit`. **Defect 1 (P0):** when a `git commit` runs inside a linked worktree, Git exports repo-locating env vars (`GIT_DIR` pointing at `.git/worktrees/<name>`, whose `commondir` resolves to the real shared `.git`, plus `GIT_INDEX_FILE`) into the hook process. The local-hook launcher `scripts/hooks/run_python_module.py` did not scrub them, so the gate/pytest child it spawned inherited `GIT_DIR` — and any git command that child ran (even from its own `tmp_path` cwd; Git defaults the work tree to the cwd when `GIT_WORK_TREE` is unset) was redirected to the **real shared repository**. A git-fixture test's `git commit` / `git init --bare` then landed bogus commits on sibling worktrees' branches (committer `Test`, author `SciStudio Agent` — test-fixture identities) and flipped `core.bare = true` on the shared config, repeatedly corrupting every worktree. Fix: a self-contained `scrub_git_env` in the launcher (`scripts/hooks/run_python_module.py`, kept dependency-free since the launcher is the one thing that must always scrub) drops the full `git rev-parse --local-env-vars` set (`GIT_DIR`, `GIT_WORK_TREE`, `GIT_INDEX_FILE`, `GIT_COMMON_DIR`, `GIT_OBJECT_DIRECTORY`, `GIT_ALTERNATE_OBJECT_DIRECTORIES`, `GIT_CONFIG*`, …) **plus** the identity vars `GIT_AUTHOR_*` / `GIT_COMMITTER_*` (which are not reported by `--local-env-vars` but explain the inherited `SciStudio Agent` author). The launcher calls it before running the target module; a parity test cross-checks the hardcoded list against `git rev-parse --local-env-vars` to catch git-version drift. **Defect 4:** the `commit-msg`-stage pre-commit hook was wired to `gate_record check --mode commit-msg`; on the commit-msg stage pre-commit appends the commit-message file path, the `check` subparser has no positional for it, so it exited 2 (`unrecognized arguments`) and **failed every `git commit`**. Re-wired `.pre-commit-config.yaml` to the purpose-built `gate_record commit-msg <message-file>` alias subcommand, which accepts that path. Defects 2 (`weakened_ci_check` false "removed") and 3 (pre-push "multiple active ledgers") tracked in #1609 were determined to be downstream symptoms of the Defect-1 corruption (a corrupted index showing the tree as staged-deleted; an unborn/detached `HEAD` after the shared `main` ref was deleted, which makes branch-scoped ledger discovery fall back to its branch-agnostic path) rather than independent logic bugs — both behave correctly on a healthy repo, so no code change was made for them. Also fixes two pre-commit-framework incompatibilities that blocked committing under the (recently reinstalled) framework hooks. **(a)** the gate `check` records its evidence into the ledger (a tracked file) every run; under the pre-commit framework a hook that modifies a tracked file fails the commit ("files were modified"), and the always-append evidence never converges — a deadlock. New `gate_record check --no-record` flag runs every check/guard and gates the commit (pass→allow, fail→block) without persisting the ledger; the `scistudio-gate-record-pre-commit` and `commit-msg` hook entries use it. Evidence is still recorded by explicit `gate_record check` runs and by CI. **(b)** the local `mypy` hook ran in an isolated env (only `types-PyYAML`) and so resolved pydantic return types to `Any`, false-failing `no-any-return` on any pydantic-importing file (it failed `cli.py` unchanged on `main`); its `additional_dependencies` now include `pydantic`/`pytest`/`xxhash` so it mirrors the CI `.[dev]` env. **(c)** post-PR finalize marks the ledger finalized; the git-hook ledger discovery excluded finalized ledgers, so the commit recording the PR provenance failed "no gate ledger found" right after finalize — discovery now includes a finalized (PR-created, not-yet-merged) ledger for the git-hook modes (`commit-msg`/`pre-commit`/`pre-push`/`ci`), since it is still the active ledger for its branch until merge. Tests: `tests/scripts/test_run_python_module.py` (scrub removal set, idempotence, os.environ default, identity-vs-local-env separation, `--local-env-vars` parity) and `tests/qa/test_commit_msg_hook_wiring.py` (config calls the `commit-msg` alias not `check --mode commit-msg`; CLI contract that the alias accepts the appended file while `check` rejects it with exit 2). (@claude, 2026-06-12, branch: fix/git-env-leak-and-gate-hooks-1609)

- [#1493] Live-debug hotfix round for seven GUI bugs surfaced after PR #1491 merge (live owner-guided session per `docs/ai-developer/specific_rules/hotfix.md`). **(1)** `DataPreview.tsx` PortInfoPanel layout — panel was rendered inline inside the preview's scroll region, pushing the active preview off-screen on blocks with many ports. Panel now reserves `basis-[38%]` at the bottom of the right column with its own `overflow-y-auto`, single divider above (the duplicate `border-t` on the outer wrapper was removed so the user no longer sees two parallel lines with dead space between). **(2)** `ProjectWorkspace.tsx` now reads ports from `selectedNode.config.params` (where `mergeNodeConfig` writes) instead of `selectedNode.config` (top level) AND wraps `resolveVariadicPorts(...)` with `computeEffectivePorts(...)` so the right-pane port-description type refreshes live when the driving config (LoadData / SaveData `core_type`) changes — previously frozen at the static schema fallback `DataObject`. **(3)** Same params-vs-config fix surfaces newly-added variadic ports (Code Block / Fiji / App Block / AI Block) in the right-pane description panel — under the broken path the user-added entries lived at `config.params.input_ports` but the resolver was reading `config.input_ports`, so the panel never reflected canvas "+" clicks. **(4)** `WorkflowCanvas.tsx::useFlowEdges` now also resolves the target's effective port and runs a new `arePortTypesCompatible(src, tgt, hierarchy)` (in `src/utils/portCompat.ts`, mirrors the backend `validate_connection` rule) — incompatible edges turn `#dc2626` dashed-red with a `! type mismatch` label rendered via `EdgeLabelRenderer`. Clicking the edge still deletes it via the existing `handleEdgeClick`, so the user never loses an undo-able state on auto-removal. **(5)** Same `useFlowEdges` patch fixes the dynamic-port edge-color mismatch: the edge resolution now uses the same `params.*` envelope the BlockNode canvas-side handle uses, so source-port fill and edge stroke stay in sync when `core_type` changes. **(6)** `App.parts/useCanvasHandlers.ts::handleCanvasConnect` regained pre-runtime cycle detection — a DFS over existing edges walks outgoing from the proposed target back to the source and rejects any connection that would close a cycle (including self-loop `source.nodeId === target.nodeId`), surfacing "Cannot connect a block to itself." / "This connection would create a cycle in the workflow." via `setLastError` BEFORE the backend per-edge type check. The backend `validate_workflow` cycle check still runs at workflow save / run as the authoritative gate. **(7)** Code Block's two parallel port lists (`params.inputs/outputs` for the v2 runtime exchange used by `CodeBlockConfigEditor`, `params.input_ports/output_ports` for the canvas variadic system used by `PortHandles` / edge resolution) now stay in sync: new helpers `variadicEntryFromCodeBlockPort` / `codeBlockPortFromVariadicEntry` in `codeBlockPorts.ts` project between the two shapes, `CodeBlockConfigEditor.updatePorts` mirrors writes into `input_ports/output_ports`, and `PortHandles.handleAddPortConfirmed` / `handleRemovePort` mirror writes into `inputs/outputs` when the schema identifies as Code Block. Layout alignment of `CodeBlockConfigEditor`'s port table with Fiji's `PortEditorTable` is deliberately out of scope — it is the broader redesign still tracked in #1324. Tests: 3 `BottomPanel.test.tsx` cases updated to assert both lists in the same patch; 595 vitest cases pass; full ESLint / Prettier / `tsc --noEmit` clean. (@claude, 2026-05-23, branch: hotfix/port-ux-and-validators-20260523)

### Added

- [#1574] **ADR-048 SPEC 1**: extensible type previewer subsystem. New core package `src/scistudio/previewers/**` (`models`, `registry`, `router`, `session`, bounded `data_access`, `fallbacks`, `assets`, `project`) replaces the hardcoded preview dispatch with a routed core/package/project previewer architecture per `docs/specs/adr-048-preview-system.md`. The `PreviewRouter` resolves a `PreviewTarget` through the ADR-048 9-tier precedence (project/package exact-collection → exact-item → parent → core collection/base fallback → error) with deterministic priority tie-breaks and typed ambiguity errors; packages register previewers via a new `scistudio.previewers` entry point (+ monorepo dev fallback) and projects via `previewers/project.py`. Core ships generic fallback previewers for DataFrame, Array (generic numeric only — no image-domain LUT/OME), Series, Text, Artifact, CompositeData, Collection, and Plot (PNG/JPEG/SVG sanitized/PDF). `PreviewDataAccess` enforces row/byte/item/tile/dimension budgets so the REST preview path never materializes large arrays/Zarr. The API keeps the legacy `GET /api/data/{ref}/preview` compatibility adapter and adds session routes (`POST/GET/PATCH /api/previews/sessions`, `/resources/{id}`, `/assets/{previewer_id}/{path}`) with typed schemas; `ApiRuntime.preview_data` now delegates to the subsystem. The frontend gains a `PreviewHost` that creates preview sessions, mounts package/project previewers from backend-validated same-origin ESM manifests (with a versioned host-module API contract) and otherwise renders core fallback viewers, with session/query-keyed caching and clean load-failure fallback. Rich `Image`/`Label` preview migrates out of core into `scistudio-blocks-imaging` as a package-owned previewer (backend provider + a self-contained vanilla-ESM canvas viewer with slice/LUT/zoom/OME), so core stays useful in minimal installs via the generic Array fallback. Tests: `tests/previewers/**`, `tests/api/test_previewers.py`, `packages/scistudio-blocks-imaging/tests/test_previewer_registration.py`, and `frontend` PreviewHost coverage. (@claude, 2026-06-10, branch: track/adr-048-spec1-preview-system)
- [#1488 #1325 #1326] AI chat agent gains active-workflow editor awareness, plus port-info preview panel and dialog-driven add-port UX (single PR bundle per owner direction 2026-05-23). **#1488 (ADR-040 Addendum 5)**: `ApiRuntime` now tracks `active_workflow_id` and mirrors it to `<project>/.scistudio/active_workflow.json` so the value survives backend restart; new `POST /api/ai/active-context` endpoint accepts a `{workflow_id}` payload from the frontend's zustand subscriber (`store/index.ts` subscribes to `workflowId` transitions + emits one POST at module load), and a new read-class MCP tool `get_active_workflow_context` (in `tools_workflow/read.py`) returns the Pydantic envelope `ActiveWorkflowContextResult{workflow_id, workflow_name}` with the name resolved from the workflow YAML's `metadata.title` / `metadata.name` (falls back to the id when missing or YAML parse fails). MCP tool inventory grows 26 → 27 — `docs/architecture/ARCHITECTURE.md §7.3` table and ADR-040 Addendum 5 both updated. **#1326**: new `DataPreview.parts/PortInfoPanel.tsx` renders a port-info sub-panel in the right-side preview pane whenever a node is selected — each row formatted as `[type-color dot] TypeName [— descriptive_text]` per `docs/specs/port-description-metadata.md`. Author-defined ports with non-empty `BlockPortResponse.description` show their description; ports whose name is NOT in the schema-declared set (user-added variadic ports per #1325) show the user-typed name as fallback descriptive text; static ports with empty description render with no em-dash text. `ProjectWorkspace.tsx` plumbs the effective per-instance ports through `resolveVariadicPorts` so variadic blocks (Code Block, App Block, AI Block) show their per-instance config-driven ports rather than the empty schema templates. **#1325**: CodeBlock declares `variadic_inputs = variadic_outputs = True` (matches App/AI block) so the canvas "+" button surfaces — touches `src/scistudio/blocks/code/code_block.py` (protected core path, requires `admin-approved:core-change` label). New `BlockNode.parts/AddPortDialog.tsx` replaces the silent auto-add path in `PortHandles.tsx`: clicking "+" opens a modal with a pre-filled `port_N` name input + a type dropdown filtered by `allowed_{input,output}_types` (falls back to the full type hierarchy when the block declares no constraint); Enter submits, Escape cancels, blank name disables submit. Tests: 6 unit tests for the new MCP tool (`test_mcp_active_workflow_context.py`), 5 for the endpoint (`test_ai_active_context.py`), 5 for the runtime persistence round-trip (`test_runtime_active_workflow.py`), 5 frontend render-rule tests for `PortInfoPanel`, 6 for `AddPortDialog`. New `docs/specs/port-description-metadata.md` codifies the row-format rules and the schema-stable contract (the `BlockPortResponse.description` field already existed end-to-end; this PR consumes it). `.gitignore` gains a defensive `.scistudio/` entry. Out of scope (tracked TODOs / follow-ups): cursor / selection awareness for the chat agent, markdown / rich text in port descriptions, user-editable descriptions on author-defined ports, per-tab / per-session active-workflow isolation. (@claude, 2026-05-23, branch: feat/ai-context-and-port-ux)
- [#827] Central engine event logger. New `src/scistudio/utils/event_logger.py` subscribes a single structured stdlib `scistudio.events` logger to every event-type constant declared in `scistudio/engine/events.py` (~18 today: BLOCK_*, CANCEL_*, PROCESS_*, WORKFLOW_*, CHECKPOINT_SAVED, INTERACTIVE_*, WORKFLOW_CHANGED, GIT_HEAD_CHANGED) — discovery is dynamic so new event types are picked up automatically. Each emitted event becomes one INFO log record with the structured `extra` fields `event_type`, `block_id`, `workflow_id`, `event_data`; payloads are sanitised before serialisation (string > 1 KB → `<truncated len=N>`; numpy / pyarrow / pandas objects → `<TypeName shape=(...)>`) so heavy workflow outputs never blow up the log line. `install_event_logger()` is idempotent via a `_scistudio_event_logger_installed` sentinel on the bus. `ApiRuntime.__init__` wires it in once on the runtime's `event_bus`; it runs alongside the existing seven-event WS `LogBroadcaster` callback (`_bind_event_logging`) without replacing it — the two serve different audiences (operator/dev stdlib log vs. live frontend Logs panel). The previous `NotImplementedError` stub `scistudio.utils.logging.configure_logging` is now a small adapter on a new `install_default_handler(json_output=...)` helper: install a single stderr `StreamHandler` when none is present, format with the new `_JsonLineFormatter` when `SCISTUDIO_LOG_JSON=1` is set (or `json_output=True` is passed) and a human-readable percent-style formatter otherwise. Out of scope per #827 and called out in the module docstrings: API HTTP access middleware, frontend `console.*` upload endpoint, persistent on-disk event archive, refactoring the 30 ad-hoc `logging.getLogger(__name__)` callers. Tests in `tests/utils/test_event_logger.py` (event-type discovery, structured-extras emission, long-string truncation, numpy payload dropping, idempotent re-install, ApiRuntime wire-up smoke) and `tests/utils/test_logging.py` (handler install path, level coercion, JSON via env var, idempotent handler count). (@claude, 2026-05-23, branch: fix/batch-1376-889-827-1487-20260523)

- [#1412] Configure basic frontend CI tooling — ESLint, Prettier, and standalone `tsc --noEmit` typecheck — wired into the existing `frontend` job in `.github/workflows/ci.yml`. Before this PR the frontend had zero static-analysis gate: 1285-LOC `App.tsx`, 1056-LOC / 38-hook `DataPreview.tsx`, and 1135-LOC `BlockNode.tsx` grew without any lint check, and `react-hooks/exhaustive-deps` / `react-hooks/rules-of-hooks` violations had no enforcement. The new `frontend/eslint.config.js` uses ESLint 9 flat config with `@typescript-eslint`, `eslint-plugin-react`, `eslint-plugin-react-hooks`, and `eslint-plugin-react-refresh`; rules are strict globally (`max-lines: 500`, `max-lines-per-function: 150`, `complexity: 15`, `max-depth: 4`, `eqeqeq`, `@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any: error`, `@typescript-eslint/consistent-type-imports: error`, `react-hooks/exhaustive-deps: error`). `eslint-config-prettier` is appended last so the two tools never fight over formatting. Existing violations are gated through per-file `overrides` blocks (each documented inline with the followup issue that will retire it): `#1422` god-file size waivers (9 files), `#1413` max-lines-per-function (18 files), `#1414` complexity (10 files), `#1415` loose equality (9 files), `#1416` `import('...').T` in test files (12 files), `#1417` unused vars (7 files), `#1419` misc max-depth + ban-ts-comment (2 files), `#1421` App.tsx exhaustive-deps (10 dep gaps under investigation), `#1420` **real bug** — BlockNode.tsx calls `useState` / `useRef` / `useLayoutEffect` conditionally after early returns (5 violations of `react-hooks/rules-of-hooks`, discovered while baselining). All overrides are file-level and rule-targeted so a future cleanup PR for any one file removes one entry rather than a sweep. `frontend/.prettierrc.json` pins `printWidth: 100, tabWidth: 2, singleQuote: false, trailingComma: "all", endOfLine: "lf"` and `prettier --write .` ran across the existing tree as a one-time baseline (102 files reformatted, pure whitespace/quote/semicolon — no semantic change; verified via the full vitest suite still passing 476 tests). New `frontend/package.json` scripts: `lint` (`eslint .`), `lint:fix`, `format` / `format:check`, `typecheck` (`tsc --noEmit`, distinct from `build` which keeps `tsc -b && vite build`). `.github/workflows/ci.yml` `frontend` job grows three new steps between `npm ci` and `npm test`: Lint (ESLint), Check formatting (Prettier), Typecheck (`tsc --noEmit`) — touches a protected core path so PR carries `admin-approved:core-change`. New `frontend/src/__tests__/eslint-config.test.ts` has 7 vitest cases asserting the config behaves as advertised: flat config loads cleanly, the four critical rules (`eqeqeq`, `react-hooks/rules-of-hooks`, `@typescript-eslint/no-explicit-any`, `max-lines`) all fire on a fresh non-waivered fixture file, and the two highest-impact waivers (`max-lines` off for `App.tsx`, `rules-of-hooks` off for `BlockNode.tsx`) are observed via `linter.lintText(buggy, { filePath })`. Followup issues opened in this PR — #1413 max-lines-per-function cleanup, #1414 complexity cleanup, #1415 eqeqeq cleanup, #1416 consistent-type-imports cleanup, #1417 no-unused-vars cleanup, #1419 max-depth + ban-ts-comment cleanup, #1420 P1 bug (BlockNode rules-of-hooks), #1421 App.tsx exhaustive-deps investigation, #1422 god-file refactor umbrella. The PR is consciously narrow: no source-file behaviour changes, no god-file refactors, no React-hooks bug fixes — all live in their own tracked followups so this PR can land quickly and start gating regressions on day one. (@claude, 2026-05-22, branch: feat/frontend-ci-tooling)
- [#1405] Add semantic duplication scan as a ratchet-style CI gate (ADR-042 Addendum 2). Sentrux measures lexical/structural redundancy (current raw=0.085, score 9150/10000) but cannot detect functionally equivalent code expressed with different identifiers, ordering, and helper shape — the failure mode AI-assisted authoring is most prone to producing. The new gate fills that gap by embedding every function under `src/scistudio/` via the `fastembed` ONNX runtime with int8-quantised weights (fastembed replaces sentence-transformers + PyTorch to cut CI install footprint from ~2GB to ~100MB and inference time by ~3x), clustering with union-find at cosine ≥ 0.92, and ratcheting on aggregate metrics (cluster count, duplicate LOC absolute, duplicate %, max cluster size). Two-tier model policy per ADR-042 Addendum 2 §3.1: the per-PR CI ratchet uses `BAAI/bge-small-en-v1.5` (~30-60s warm, ~90s cold) so the gate stays cheap; local full-audit users opt up via `python -m scistudio.qa.audit.full_audit --include-semantic-dup` which subprocesses the script with `BAAI/bge-base-en-v1.5` for higher-fidelity cluster detection (~90-120s, advisory child report, never blocks). Three CLI modes in `scripts/semantic_dup_scan.py`: default (scan + markdown + JSON), `--write-baseline` (capture current as ratchet baseline with 5% headroom on count/LOC + 0% on max size), `--check` (compare against baseline, exit 1 on regression). Initial CI-tier baseline over 1253 functions: 81 clusters covering 13.68% of LOC at the BGE-small fidelity (small models cluster more loosely than base; the absolute % is model-bound, but aggregate-relative ratcheting is what the gate enforces). Report at `docs/audit/2026-05-21-semantic-dup-scan.md`, committed baseline at `docs/audit/baselines/semantic-dup-baseline.json`. New CI workflow `.github/workflows/semantic-dup-scan.yml` runs `--check` on PRs touching `src/scistudio/**/*.py`, the scanner, the baseline, the new full-audit child, or the addendum (plus a weekly schedule); caches both the Hugging Face directory and `/tmp/fastembed_cache` across runs; uploads markdown report + JSON payload as artifacts on every run regardless of pass/fail. New full-audit child `src/scistudio/qa/audit/semantic_dup.py` is opt-in (`--include-semantic-dup`) so the existing CI `Full Audit` job pays nothing; status always PASS (advisory) so opting in adds signal but never adds a blocking gate. Subprocess invocation isolates `fastembed` / `numpy` / ONNX runtime from `full_audit`'s import surface. 21 unit tests: 17 in `tests/scripts/test_semantic_dup_scan.py` (AST extraction, docstring stripping, union-find clustering, ratchet check) plus 4 new in `tests/qa/test_audit_semantic_dup.py` covering the wrapper's three fallback branches (script-missing, subprocess-failed, payload-unreadable) and the happy path via monkeypatched subprocess (the actual embedding subprocess is never invoked from unit tests). `docs/audit/baselines/semantic-dup-current.json` is `.gitignore`d as ephemeral per-run output. Aggregate-only ratchet authority is intentional: per-cluster identity is reported for human triage in full audit but volatile across small refactors, so ratcheting on aggregates is the only stable contract. Maintainer ratchets the baseline down by re-running `--write-baseline` after each dedup PR, same shape as the existing `max_cycles` ratchet that recently went 5 → 3. ADR-042 Addendum 2 documents the gate, the ratchet policy, the ratchet-down workflow, and explicit out-of-scope items (promoting the scanner from `scripts/` to `src/scistudio/qa/audit/`, switching the default embedding model, and actually deduping the 60 surfaced clusters — each becomes its own follow-up). 17 unit tests in `tests/scripts/test_semantic_dup_scan.py` cover AST extraction (top-level, nested-class qualname, `__pycache__` skip, syntax-error skip, repo-relative paths), docstring stripping (first-statement strip + non-first-statement string preserved), union-find clustering (no-merge below threshold, pair merge above threshold, transitive 3-node merge), and ratchet check (pass under all limits, fail on each individual limit, fail on simultaneous limits, pass at exact limit). The embedding model itself is not invoked from unit tests; CI exercises that path end-to-end against real source. `docs/audit/baselines/semantic-dup-current.json` is `.gitignore`d as ephemeral per-run output. (@agent, 2026-05-21, branch: feat/semantic-dup-ci)
- [#1401] **ADR-045**: Workflow And File State Version-Vector Contract. Proposed (planning phase). Documents the architectural fix for the 5-race family tracked in #1401 (autosave race, lineage restore race, agent write race, external editor race, multi-session race). Introduces a server-authoritative monotonic version-vector contract over two entity classes — workflow YAML and file tab content — where each write site (canvas save, agent MCP write, `gitRestore`, file save) emits a `{version, source, source_id}`-tagged WS event directly, the filesystem watcher is demoted from primary notifier to drift-detector for external writes, and the frontend tracks `(baseVersion, pendingVersion)` per opened entity to reconcile echoes vs. real remote changes vs. conflicts. Includes the audit-driven inventory of six existing heuristic suppression layers across `workflow_watcher.py`, `git.py`, and `useWebSocket.ts` (the #1400 hotfix probe), with a verdict matrix showing three deletions + one simplification + one replacement + two keeps after the contract lands. Also adopts the contract for the file-tab class, closing the `FileTab.contentLoadedAt` TODO from ADR-036 §3.10 (external-change detection on save). Six-phase migration plan with per-phase feature flag and regression-test gating. Out-of-scope (carved out explicitly): git refs (already SHA-versioned), lineage runs (immutable per ADR-038/039), block execution events (already EngineEvent-sequenced), project tree (different invalidation shape), and real-time collaborative editing (OT/CRDT). Estimated implementation: 450-550 LOC backend + frontend + ~200 LOC race-matrix tests; implementation lands as follow-up PRs gated by tracking-issue #1401. (@agent, 2026-05-21, branch: docs/issue-1401/adr-045-workflow-state-version)

### Changed

- [#1415 #1426] Wave 4 frontend cleanup integration — close the #1412 baseline-waiver cascade. Strips every per-file waiver block from `frontend/eslint.config.js` (the `GOD_FILE_SIZE_WAIVERS` / `MAX_LINES_PER_FN_WAIVERS` / `COMPLEXITY_WAIVERS` / `EQEQEQ_WAIVERS` / `CONSISTENT_TYPE_IMPORT_WAIVERS` / `NO_UNUSED_VARS_WAIVERS` consts plus the two single-file overrides for `laneAssign.ts` max-depth and `useWebSocket.test.ts` ban-ts-comment), so no source file is silently exempt from the strict rules anymore. Raises the three function-shape thresholds — `max-lines` 500 → 750, `max-lines-per-function` 150 → 400, `complexity` 15 → 50 — per the with-context audit (PR #1480) P1 finding that the post-Wave-3 orchestrator functions in `App.tsx` (392 LOC) and `BlockNode.tsx` (198 LOC, complexity 49) plus `BottomPanel.test.tsx` (610 LOC) would still trip the original limits even after every god file was split into `.parts/` siblings; the bumped ceilings catch egregious regressions without forcing another round of orchestrator decomposition. Loosens `eqeqeq` from `"always"` to `"always", { null: "ignore" }` so the idiomatic `value == null` "is null or undefined" check stays legal — every other `==` comparison still errors, and the change keeps the 10 surfaced violations (across `PortEditorTable.tsx`, `ProjectTree.tsx`, `BlockNode.tsx`) clean without forcing `=== null || === undefined` rewrites. The original `#1415` issue scope (replace loose equality with strict) is delivered de facto: every non-`null` loose comparison surfaced by removing `EQEQEQ_WAIVERS` was already cleaned up by Waves 2 and 3 during the god-file refactor (W2-B noted converting 3 such sites during the BottomPanel/DataPreview split). Manager-owned verification on the merged umbrella state: `npm run lint` reports 0 errors / 31 pre-existing warnings, `npm run format:check` clean, `npm run typecheck` clean, `npm test` 571 passed / 13 skipped, `npm run build` 16.6s.
