- [#1100] ADR-042/043/044 — QA Infrastructure Overhaul cascade (Draft). Three-ADR design package establishing a unified quality regime to address documentation/code drift caused by AI-agent-driven development at ~30 KLOC / 41 ADRs / ~680 public symbols scale. **ADR-042 (primary, ~3694 LOC)**: frontmatter schema (`extra="forbid"` Pydantic v2 on every ADR/spec, mandatory `governs`/`contracts`/`files`/`excludes`/`amends`/`status`/`agent_editable`/`phase`/`is_code_implementation`), drift classification (a/b/c1/c2/c3/d), Fact Substitution Registry (§10, `{{ facts.X }}` Jinja2), bidirectional MAINTAINERS ↔ governs closure, AGENTS.md hierarchy (root canonical + CLAUDE.md symlink + path-scoped rules + skills + hooks), git trailer conventions (`Assisted-by:` / `Fixes:` / `ADR:` / `Loosening-Approved:` / `Errata-Only:` / `Backfill-Test:` / `Governance-Modification-Approved-By:`), Real-Behavior-Proof gate, docs-agent active fixer (PR-only, no direct push), `committer.py` hard tooling, required-skill cross-runtime installer, Workflow v2 (7 stages), libCST codemod discipline, Sphinx+autoapi+autodoc_pydantic+nitpicky docs build with linkcheck builder, DeepL translation pipeline, human-developer exemption tiers, seven-step phased rollout (Phase 0/1/1.5/2/3/4/5 with 6-agent parallel Phase 1 DAG 1A-H), zero-tolerance terminal state via ratchet wrapper (GitHub Checks API `conclusion=neutral`), Amendment records protocol (§27.5, `amends:` field + auto-generated `consolidate_cascade.md`), self-iteration mechanism, M1-M11 meta-compliance gates. **ADR-043 (Addendum A, ~1849 LOC)**: implementation tracker, phase gate validator, 5-layer rule-modification hard blocks (`governance_mod_guard` local + `governance_mod_pr_check` CI), test-quality enforcement (mutmut + hypothesis + AST anti-pattern detection), AGENTS.md layered design refinement (mechanism-types: hook / path-scoped rule / skill), 2026 convention adoptions (data classification, assessment rubric, three-tier path boundary, weakened-CI block). M12-M15. **ADR-044 (Addendum B, ~1401 LOC)**: unified documentation set across 4 audiences (docs/contributing/, docs/user/, docs/prod-agent/, docs/doc-guide/) with 2-letter-page source-based length cap (120 line / 600 word), skill-as-pointer convention (procedural / tool-wrapping / bootstrap-meta), auto-generated user-facing reference (API via autoapi, CLI via typer introspection, blocks via custom `scistudio_block_catalog` directive, schemas via `scistudio_runner_catalog` + `scistudio_ai_block_catalog`, OpenAPI via FastAPI, `llms.txt`), four entry points (AGENTS.md / onboarding.md / configuring-your-agent.md / quickstart.md). Appendix A clarifies ADR-040 = four-layer production-environment agent reliability stack with 6 deliverables (NOT just FastMCP migration). M16-M19. **Process**: drafted via 7 audit iterations (3 targeted + 4 no-context independent) plus 2 external audits (tool-reality + phase-plan) plus 1 anti-hallucination verification (reversed planned removal of `InstructionsLoaded` Claude hook after live-fetch confirmed it exists). All critical and warning findings addressed; remaining info-level findings deferred to Phase 1 where real CI tooling becomes ground truth. **Scope**: design only — no tooling, no enforcement, no behavior change in this PR. Self-exempt from doc_drift/fact_drift/closure checks per ADR-042 §3.0 bootstrap exemption window. (@claude, 2026-05-17, branch: feat/issue-1100/adr-042-044-qa-infrastructure, session: 20260517-234226-adr-042-043-044-qa-infrastructure-overha)

### Fixed

- [#1241] Fix all accepted ADR-043 Codex auto-review findings: scalar capability iterables are rejected, SimpleIO requires a single path, legacy registry lookup preserves extension-only ordering and falls back past broken capability classes, frontend placeholder capability selection clears to `null`, AppBlock treats null output `capability_id` as unset, and boundary output validation now matches AppBlock's first-runtime-type behavior. (@agent, 2026-05-19, branch: fix/issue-1241/adr043-codex-audit, session: 20260519-193810-fix-adr-043-codex-auto-review-findings)

- [#1214] Fix ADR-043 fact-audit fallout without editing locked ADR/spec frontmatter: add machine-readable ADR-042 governance addendum support, append ADR-041/ADR-043/spec addenda for materialisation/API capability surfaces, and refresh generated facts. (@agent, 2026-05-19, branch: track/adr-043/capability-registry, session: 20260519-172415-adr-043-implementation-cascade-managemen)

- [#1200] Fix Lineage run status finalization so workflows with block-level `ERROR` now persist `runs.status="failed"` instead of `completed`; cancelled block states persist `cancelled`, and all-success runs remain `completed`. Adds regression coverage for the scheduler-normal-completion/block-error path that previously made the Lineage tab show failed runs as complete. (@agent, 2026-05-19, branch: hotfix/lineage-error-status, session: 20260519-152650-fix-lineage-run-status-for-block-errors)

- [#1196] Restore the repository tree to PR #1099 as the rollback baseline, then re-apply the selected post-rollback IO/materialisation fixes from PRs #1104, #1105, #1106, #1107 (transitive dependency required by #1112/#1116), #1108, #1112, and #1116 so `supported_extensions`, registry query dispatch, file materialisation, and AppBlock typed reconstruction remain available on the rollback branch. Also restore the current ADR-042 branch documents (`docs/adr/ADR-042.md` plus the ADR-042 spec companions) onto the rollback PR, and relax the typed-reconstruction regression test to accept plugin subtypes (for example `PeakTable <: DataFrame`) while still forbidding silent downgrade to `Artifact`. (@agent, 2026-05-19, branch: fix/issue-1196/rollback-pr1099-selected-fixes, session: 20260519-121322-rollback-main-to-pr1099-with-selected-po)

- [#1079] Rewrite `AppBlock._bin_outputs_by_extension` to call `scistudio.engine.materialisation.reconstruct_from_file` for typed port outputs (ADR-028 §D8). Pre-fix the binner silently downgraded every non-`Artifact` declared port type to `Artifact` and emitted a `"declared type ... not constructible from a file path"` warning, breaking the FijiBlock → SaveImage edge where the user declares `accepted_types=[Image]` and downstream rejects the resulting `Artifact`. New per-port semantics: declared concrete type with a registered loader → typed `DataObject`; declared `Artifact` (or subclass) with no loader → `Artifact` fallback (intentional, no warning, preserves #690 homogeneity); declared concrete non-`Artifact` type with no loader → `LookupError` propagates from `reconstruct_from_file` so the run fails fast instead of silently violating the declared contract. The pre-#1079 warning is removed because the Artifact fallback inside `reconstruct_from_file` is the new intentional path. `DataObject` declared as the port target type (the wildcard root) maps to `Artifact` before the call so legacy wildcard-port behavior survives. `Collection.item_type` is now computed from the actual constructed item class (or the declared target type for empty optional ports), keeping the #690 homogeneity guarantee under the new fallback path. 4 new tests in `tests/blocks/app/test_appblock_bin_outputs.py` (typed `DataFrame` reconstruction via `LoadData` on `.csv`, no-warning assertion, legacy `Artifact` port, missing-loader `LookupError`); `test_binner_falls_back_to_artifact_for_non_constructible_type` replaced by `test_binner_raises_lookup_error_for_non_constructible_type` to match the new contract. 50 non-Fiji app-block tests pass. (@claude, 2026-05-18, branch: fix/issue-1079/appblock-bin-outputs-typed-reconstruction, session: 20260518-032442-fix-1079-appblock-bin-outputs-by-extensi)
- [hotfix][#1097] **P0 information-disclosure**: production MCP `search_docs` / `get_doc` no longer expose SciStudio developer source-tree paths. Pre-fix `_docs_root()` in `src/scistudio/ai/agent/mcp/tools_qa.py` unconditionally walked `__file__.parents` looking for any `docs/` directory when the active project had none. With SciStudio installed editable from a developer checkout (the common e2e setup at `C:\temp\scistudio-e2e-adr-040\...`), the walk landed on `C:\Users\<dev>\workspace\SciStudio\docs` and let the embedded Codex/Claude agent search and read SciStudio ADRs / specs / planning docs — violating ADR-040 §2.1 dev/prod boundary and leaking absolute developer-machine paths through MCP responses. **Fix**: `_docs_root()` resolves only `ctx.project_dir/docs`; the parents-walk is removed entirely. **No env-var backdoor** — an interim draft gated the fallback behind `SCISTUDIO_DEV=1` mirroring the monorepo-scan convention, but was rejected because any env-var-controlled escape into "dev mode" is a soft attack surface (compromised shell init, malicious launcher, supply-chain dep could silently re-open the leak). `search_docs` now returns `[]` when no docs are available; `get_doc` keeps fail-closed with `FileNotFoundError`. `GetDocResult.path` is now relative to the docs root (POSIX-style), closing the secondary absolute-path leak. Regression tests in `tests/ai/test_mcp_fastmcp.py` cover (a) no project docs → empty/404, (b) `SCISTUDIO_DEV=1` MUST NOT re-open the parents-walk, (c) `GetDocResult.path` is relative. Follow-up #1098 (P1) tracks injecting a packaged user-facing docs corpus so production agents have a non-empty docs surface without re-opening the leak. (@claude, 2026-05-17, branch: hotfix/issue-1097-mcp-docs-leak-dev-paths, session: 20260517-233930-fix-1097-mcp-docs-tools-no-longer-leak-d)
- [hotfix] ADR-040 Phase 4 user-directive #40 — Codex hook parity (config-level; upstream runtime gap on Windows documented). Reverses §3.10's "Codex hook coverage deferred" gap per explicit user override ("codex和claude必须一视同仁" / "Codex and Claude must be treated identically"). Codex 0.130's hook surface (https://developers.openai.com/codex/config-reference) ships PreToolUse/PostToolUse hooks with the same stdin-JSON contract Claude Code uses — `tool_name`, `tool_input`, exit code 2 + stderr blocks the call. `agent_provisioning/codex_config.py` now appends `features.hooks = true` plus 3 PreToolUse + 3 PostToolUse matcher groups after the existing `[mcp_servers.scistudio]` block; each hook command points at the same Python scripts under `<project>/.claude/hooks/` Claude already uses (cross-provider DRY, no Codex-specific script tree). Matchers handle Codex tool-name variants: `^Bash$` for the shell tool, `^(Edit|Write|MultiEdit|apply_patch)$` for the edit/write surface (Codex routes some edits through `apply_patch`), MCP tool names unchanged. The MCP block stays byte-identical to `_render_codex_block()`'s output (ADR §3.7/§3.9 unification contract — `scistudio install --target codex` still produces the same bytes). New regression test `test_codex_config_emits_six_hooks` covers matcher count + feature flag + cross-provider script-path invariant. ADR-040 Addendum 4 documents the matcher-table mapping AND the upstream Codex 0.130 Windows-runtime gap discovered during e2e: a trivial debug hook with a wildcard matcher never fires under any combination of (inline TOML vs hooks.json) × (project-scope vs user-scope) × (with vs without `--dangerously-bypass-approvals-and-sandbox`); the same hook scripts work correctly when invoked directly. SciStudio ships the correct hook declarations regardless — when Codex resolves the Windows runtime, our config "just works" with no SciStudio-side change required. (@claude, 2026-05-17, branch: track/adr-040, session: phase-4-hotfix-codex-hook-parity)
- [hotfix] ADR-040 Phase 4 e2e bugfix #33 — MCP server now silently drops JSON-RPC notifications instead of returning `-32601 "unknown method 'notifications/initialized'"`. Codex 2026 (vcodex-cli 0.130.0) treated the bogus error envelope on the MCP-mandatory `notifications/initialized` notification as fatal and tore down the transport, surfaced in Phase 4 e2e as `MCP client for "scistudio" failed to start: MCP startup failed: Transport closed` and ZERO scistudio tools in the Codex tab. JSON-RPC 2.0 §4.1 forbids responding to notifications. Fix: `MCPServer.dispatch` returns `None` for any frame without an `id`; the connection loop skips writing. Claude Code v2.1.143 had silently tolerated the spec violation, so this is purely a Codex-side ship-blocker that the strict transport surfaced. Regression test in `tests/ai/test_mcp_fastmcp.py::test_dispatch_silently_drops_notifications`. ADR-040 Addendum 3. (@claude, 2026-05-17, branch: track/adr-040, session: phase-4-hotfix-mcp-notifications)
- [hotfix] ADR-040 Phase 4 e2e bugfix #28 + #31. **#28 (P1)** — Skill install paths flattened from `<root>/skills/scistudio/<name>/SKILL.md` (nested) to `<root>/skills/<name>/SKILL.md` (flat). Phase 4 e2e on `track/adr-040` surfaced `Skill(scistudio-write-block) -> Unknown skill` because Claude Code's skill registry walks one level under `<root>/.claude/skills/` and never recursed into the `scistudio/` namespace directory. Same constraint on Codex (`<root>/.agents/skills/`). Fix: `agent_provisioning/skills.py::_DEST_TREES`, `agent_provisioning/_orchestrate.py` idempotency enumeration, `tests/agent_provisioning/test_skills.py`. ADR-040 amended with Addendum 1. The dev-side `scistudio install --skill` cross-install path (ADR §3.9) still writes to nested layout and is tracked separately. **#31 (P2)** — Provisioned `<project>/CLAUDE.md`/`AGENTS.md` template gained a "Git commits" section teaching the `[agent] <subject>` prefix + `Co-Authored-By: <provider>` trailer convention; original template shipped no commit-message guidance. Fix: `agent_provisioning/templates/claude_agents_md.md`. ADR-040 amended with Addendum 2. (@claude, 2026-05-17, branch: track/adr-040, session: phase-4-hotfix-skills-discovery)
- [#1084] F40-integration: ADR-040 Phase 3.6 — 6 consensus P1/P2 findings from A1 + A3 Phase 3 audits. (F1) Rewrite `src/scistudio/agent_provisioning/templates/hook_enforce_concrete_port_types.py` to scan the live `InputPort/OutputPort(accepted_types=[...])` API; the pre-fix hook AST-greped for `PortSpec(type='DataObject')` — a legacy shape that no longer exists in `src/scistudio/blocks/base/ports.py`, so every real block escaped the dead-code "safety net". New hook flags `DataObject` elements, empty `accepted_types=[]`, and missing `accepted_types` kwargs; handles Name/Attribute/Constant forms. (F2) Fix `_SCAFFOLD_TEMPLATE` in `tools_authoring.py` to emit the 2-arg `run(self, inputs, config)` signature matching `Block.run` ABC and `InputPort(name=..., accepted_types=[Type], required=True)` matching the live `Port` dataclass; pre-fix the template emitted 1-arg `run(self, inputs)` + legacy `type=` kwarg that raised `TypeError` at `reload_blocks`. (F3) `scistudio-build-workflow/SKILL.md` §6 "When a run fails" now teaches the live `GetRunStatusResult(progress.block_states, errors: list[BlockErrorEntry])` envelope; pre-fix it taught the legacy flat `{state, block_states, error}` shape. (F4) `agent_provisioning/templates/claude_agents_md.md` adds a top-level "Hook safety net — Claude Code only" section + parenthetical Claude/Codex distinction on each rule; pre-fix the template promised hooks would block violations unconditionally, which is FALSE on Codex per ADR §3.10 (Codex hook coverage deferred — #1015). (F5) `scistudio-write-block` frontmatter tightened to name the file target (`blocks/<name>.py`) and explicitly reject "ADDING AN EXISTING BLOCK TYPE AS A NODE in a workflow YAML" (which is `scistudio-build-workflow`); resolves the A3 §B.2.2 discoverability ambiguity. (F6) Base `_skills/scistudio/SKILL.md` gains static fallback content between `<!-- tool_catalog:begin -->` / `<!-- tool_catalog:end -->` markers; `compose_system_prompt._splice` replaces ALL content between markers, so the static fallback only manifests on Codex (which reads the file verbatim, no splice). Enumerates 4 categories × 26 tools. 8 new regression tests added across `tests/agent_provisioning/test_hooks.py`, `tests/agent_provisioning/test_claude_agents_md.py`, `tests/ai/test_mcp_fastmcp.py`, `tests/packaging/test_wheel_skills.py`. 79/79 affected tests pass locally. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: feat/issue-1084/adr-040-f40-integration-p1-fixes, session: 20260516-211635-f40-integration-adr-040-phase-3-6-p1-fix)

- [#1057] Codex P1/P2 reconcile follow-up (orphaned after #1059 squash). Three findings from Codex auto-review on the merged PR landed AFTER squash-merge into `track/adr-040`; cherry-picked onto a follow-up branch per the same pattern used for #1037/#1058. **P1** (`scistudio-write-block`): `mcp__scistudio__run_block_tests` takes `type_name: str` (registered block name; resolves test file at `tests/blocks/test_<lower>.py`), not `block_path`. Updated the worked-example tool-call sequence + mandatory rule. **P2** (`scistudio-build-workflow`): `validate_workflow` returns `ValidateWorkflowResult(valid: bool, errors: list[str])` per `tools_workflow.py:251` — no `ok`, no `next_step` (read-class tool). Rewrote §5 'When validation fails' against the real envelope and noted `write_workflow`'s `next_step` as the canonical follow-up. **P2** (`scistudio-debug-run`): `GetRunStatusResult` (`tools_workflow.py:300`) is `{run_id, state, progress.block_states, errors: list[BlockErrorEntry]}` with states `queued/running/succeeded/failed/cancelled/unknown` (no `pending`); per-block state lives at `progress.block_states`, not the top level. Updated §2 envelope shape and worked example. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: fix/issue-1057/codex-reconcile-orphaned, session: 20260516-195227-i40b-adr-040-skill-content)
- [#1037] F40-impl-1053: Codex P1/P2 reconcile on I40a — (P1) `_render_tool_catalog` no longer deadlocks when `compose_system_prompt` is called from inside a running event loop (e.g. the ai_pty websocket); switched from `run_coroutine_threadsafe(coro, current_loop)` (which schedules onto the very loop the caller is blocking) to running `asyncio.run` on a dedicated worker thread via `ThreadPoolExecutor`. (P1) `_preview_dataframe` no longer loads the full Parquet/CSV table before slicing — switched to `pq.ParquetFile.iter_batches` and `pcsv.open_csv().read_next_batch()` streaming readers so the 8 MiB preview cap is honoured on multi-GB datasets. (P2) `search_docs` no longer breaks the traversal loop at the first 20 hits before sorting; it now scores every matching doc in the corpus then sorts + caps, so the top-N reflects the highest-scoring documents rather than alphabetical traversal order. 4 new regression tests (1 async-context test for the deadlock fix, 2 streaming-preview tests with 5000-row fixtures, 1 sorted-corpus test with 25 docs of split scoring). (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: feat/issue-1037/adr-040-i40a-fastmcp-impl, session: 20260516-195013-f40-impl-1053-codex-p1-p2-fixes-on-i40a)
- [#1050] Preview panel UX hotfix round (CLAUDE.md §11.5 hotfix mode): (1) drop the redundant **Start Here** and **Cancel** buttons from the right Data Preview panel header — both actions are already exposed on each block node's header (▶ / ↻) and on the workflow toolbar (Stop); the panel now reads "PREVIEW / <block name>" with no duplicate controls. (2) DataFrame preview becomes a real server-paginated table: ``GET /api/data/{ref}/preview`` gains ``page`` (1-based, server-clamped) / ``page_size`` (capped at 200) / ``sort_by`` / ``sort_dir`` (``asc``/``desc``); response carries ``total_rows`` / ``page`` / ``page_size`` / ``total_pages`` / ``sort_by`` / ``sort_dir``, with the old ``row_count`` field preserved as a backward-compat alias for the (now correct) total. Frontend ``TableViewer`` rewritten with 3-state click-to-sort headers (unsorted → asc → desc → unsorted), prev/next/first/last buttons, and a jump-to-page input — only the active page is fetched, ``key={dataRef}`` remount prevents state bleed across selections, ``readTablePayload`` tolerates old single-page responses for graceful degradation. (3) Wide-table sort no longer "卡一下": small process-local LRU keyed by ``(path, mtime, sort_by, sort_dir)`` parses + sorts each file once. Sort-variant misses reuse the unsorted base from the same cache, so flipping columns / directions only costs an in-memory ``pyarrow.sort_by`` (no IO). mtime-keyed → auto-invalidates when the producing block re-runs. ~25 MB cap on 16 entries. Backend 15/15 (``tests/api/test_data.py`` adds pagination, sort, cache-invariant, and mtime-invalidation tests); frontend 8/8. Backend wire shape live-probed through the running worktree stack via JS fetch — page 1 returns ``total_rows=137 / total_pages=3``, page 3 with ``sort_by=score&sort_dir=desc`` returns ``last_row_score=1``. Also answered (informational, no code): current image preview loading mode = server-side downsample → base64 PNG data URI per slice (Array's first non-(y,x) axis becomes the slider; LUT / zoom / pan are pure frontend canvas). (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/ux-session-20260516, session: 20260516-192735-preview-panel-ux-hotfix-drop-redundant-b)
- [#1015] Wire backend-supplied per-block ``inputs`` / ``outputs`` through the frontend adapter. ``adaptBlockExecution`` (``frontend/src/lib/api.ts``) hardcoded ``inputs: []`` / ``outputs: []`` with a stale "future enhancement" comment from the D38-2.4c skeleton. #996 inlined the join server-side, so ``GET /api/runs/{id}`` already carried the data — but the frontend dropped it on the floor, and the Lineage block cards rendered "0 inputs / 0 outputs" even though the Methods export (which reads the recorder's joined SQL directly) showed the same DataObjects correctly. New ``adaptDataObjectRef`` maps each backend row's ``{direction, port_name, position, object_id, type_name, backend, storage_path, produced_by_execution}`` shape to the frontend's leaner ``LineageDataObjectRef`` (drops ``direction`` because the server-side bucket assignment already separated inputs from outputs, drops ``backend`` and ``produced_by_execution`` because the v1 card UI doesn't display them). 36/36 Lineage frontend tests pass. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/issue-1004/graph-row-virtualization-spacer, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#1014] Add missing ``src/scistudio/__main__.py`` so ``python -m scistudio`` dispatches to the Typer CLI. The 2026-05-14 hotfix to ``scistudio.cli.install._scistudio_command_for_env`` changed every project's ``.scistudio/mcp.json`` from ``scistudio.EXE mcp-bridge`` (PATH-shadowed, foot-gun under multi-install dev boxes) to ``{sys.executable} -m scistudio mcp-bridge`` so the bridge always runs from the same interpreter that emitted the manifest. But ``python -m <pkg>`` requires a ``__main__.py`` next to ``__init__.py`` — without one the interpreter raises ``No module named scistudio.__main__`` and exits 1. The MCP client (Claude Code subprocess in an AI Block, Codex, ``claude mcp`` listing, etc.) then reports "scistudio MCP server failed: connection closed" with no useful diagnostic; the underlying error never reaches a log because the bridge subprocess died before writing any frames. Surfaced live during Phase 4 e2e when the user reopened ``scistudio gui`` and the AI Block agent's MCP tool list showed ``scistudio: failed``. New ``__main__.py`` re-exports ``cli.main.app`` and is two non-comment lines. Regression test ``tests/cli/test_dunder_main.py`` runs ``python -m scistudio --help`` in a subprocess and asserts exit 0 + expected subcommands. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/issue-1004/graph-row-virtualization-spacer, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#1013] Lane recycler holds the slot until the fork-back edge's true endpoint, not the chain's last commit. **Root cause**: when a DFS chain breaks (the parent is already on another branch), the edge router still draws a fork-back edge from `curIdx` (this branch's last commit) down to `parentIdx` (the parent on the OTHER branch). With #1012's elbow geometry that edge has a vertical segment on THIS branch's lane spanning `curIdx → parentIdx`. Pre-#1013 the lane assigner marked the slot "available" at `curIdx`, so a freshly-allocated branch could claim the same lane starting at `curIdx + 1` — and its vertical edges visually overlapped with the still-rendering fork-back tail from the previous branch. Users saw a single vertical line whose colour flipped mid-segment with no dot at the transition. **Fix**: at chain-break, set `availableColours[branch.colour] = parentIdx` instead of `curIdx`. The lane stays held until the fork-back edge actually ends. Twin code path for fold-in chains (`startParentP > 0`) gets the same treatment. 26/26 GitGraph tests still pass — small fixtures don't exercise chain-break-then-recycle. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/issue-1004/graph-row-virtualization-spacer, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#1012] Graph elbow corner moved from mid-row to dot-row so dots hide the corner. **Root cause**: #1005's elbow placed the corner at `midY` (halfway between child's row and parent's row — i.e. the empty space between two dots). The horizontal cross-cut at that mid-row coordinate then OVERLAPPED main's vertical edge AND other lanes' vertical edges at a y-value where no dot existed to anchor it, so the corner read as "a line floating above main with no endpoint". User report: "每个端点引线都是必须有个90拐角出来 ... 一个拐角和main路重叠了". **Fix**: split the elbow into two cases by lane direction. (1) **Fork-out** (`parent_lane > child_lane`, e.g. merge fold-in branching out of trunk): corner at **child's y**, so the child dot draws on top of the corner; horizontal segment extends right from the child dot, then vertical drops to the parent. (2) **Fork-back** (`child_lane > parent_lane`, e.g. side branch terminating into trunk): corner at **parent's y**, parent dot hides the corner; vertical drop on child's lane, then horizontal across to parent. Both cases align the corner with a dot's row so the dot visually closes the bend. Same idiom as vscode-git-graph / GitLens. Fixture B updated (C3→C2b: `M 12 11 L 28 11 L 28 55`; C2b→C1: `M 28 55 L 28 77 L 12 77`). 26/26 GitGraph tests pass. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/issue-1004/graph-row-virtualization-spacer, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#1011] Graph: render ref chips (local / remote / tag) next to each commit and surface them from the backend. **Backend** (`git_engine.py::log`): `for-each-ref` scan extended from `refs/heads/` only to also include `refs/remotes/` and `refs/tags/`; synthetic `origin/HEAD` symbolic ref is skipped to avoid a duplicate chip. Pre-fix, a commit kept alive purely by a remote-tracking ref or a tag (e.g. `6b37e84` = tip of `origin/docs/issue-819/metadata-spec`, no children in local history) returned `branches: []`, leaving the frontend with nothing to anchor the orphan tip. **Frontend** (`GraphSVG.tsx`): per-row label now renders small colour-coded chips for every ref in `commit.branches` — blue for local branches, grey for remote-tracking, amber for tags. Closes the "断头" visual where an orphan merge dot floated with no incoming line and no name attached. New `test_log_endpoint_includes_remote_and_tag_refs` in `tests/api/test_git_endpoints.py` exercises tag + remote-tracking ref round-trip. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/issue-1004/graph-row-virtualization-spacer, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#1004 #1005 #1006 #1007 #1008 #1009 #1010] Graph rendering hotfix batch (live-debug round per CLAUDE.md §11.5, dev-repo `.git` copy stress test). **(#1004)** `GraphSVG.tsx` row virtualisation — visible LIs were flow-laid-out from `y=0` even when `visibleStart > 0`, so deep histories had the LI column shifted up relative to the absolutely-positioned SVG dots; add a top spacer LI sized `visibleStart * ROW_HEIGHT` so the slice aligns. **(#1005)** swap cubic bezier S-curve for 90° elbow path in `edgeRouter.ts` — at the 16px lane pitch / 22px row pitch the curves were visually twisted ("两端弯曲方向不相同"); 3 straight segments match vscode-git-graph / GitLens. **(#1006)** `laneAssign.ts` trunk-swap pins the "true main" to lane 0 by walking merge-parent continuations when HEAD's first-parent chain ends mid-log (e.g. `git checkout feat; git merge main` makes the merge's first parent the feature tip, not main, so the DFS chain follows feature back to its origin shallow root and stops); refined on a second commit from the initial `candidateRows` heuristic which didn't fire on real dev repos. **(#1007)** diff modal width — `min-w-0` on the flex-1 inner div so long unified-diff lines produce a horizontal scrollbar instead of bursting the modal beyond `max-w-5xl`. **(#1008)** merge commits (`parents.length > 1`) render as a double-ring (filled outer disc + white-filled inner disc) so they visually pop next to linear commits — standard vscode-git-graph / GitLens / GitKraken idiom. **(#1009)** `/api/git/log` default `limit` `500 → None` — the 500 cap silently truncated dev histories (SciStudio's own ~570-commit repo cut off at "fix572" with no error); row virtualisation (#1004) handles deep render so the cap is no longer load-bearing. **(#1010)** decouple branch stroke colour from lane index in `laneAssign.ts` — each new `Branch` records `colorIndex = colorSeq++ % PALETTE.length` at allocation time instead of `lane % PALETTE.length`; PR-merge-heavy ladders no longer collapse onto a wall of identical-color lines when the lane allocator recycles a slot. `edgeRouter.ts` looks up per-branch `color_index` from the outer-lane endpoint's assignment instead of recomputing from the lane number. 26/26 GitGraph tests pass — small fixtures don't exercise recycling so colour outputs match either rule; the visual change shows up on long histories with many concurrent feature branches. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/issue-1004/graph-row-virtualization-spacer, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#994] Git graph edge color rule: every edge inherits `max(child_lane, parent_lane)` (= side-branch color). #990's "always child_lane" rule fixed single-fork mismatch but broke octopus/stash/merge where child is on trunk and parents fan out to side lanes — edges took trunk color while landing on side-branch-colored dots, recreating the same mismatch under a different topology. `max()` always picks the side-branch color; linear (same lane) is a no-op; fork preserves #990; merge/octopus/stash now matches the side-branch dot. Matches IntelliJ's `PrintElementPresentationManagerImpl.getColorId` "larger layoutIndex wins". 13/13 GitGraph tests pass (Fixture B/F/G updated; new Fixture H for octopus). (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/batch-994-1000, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#995] `_extract_type_name` in `core/lineage/recorder.py` now handles Collection wire wrappers. Pre-fix every block output stored as `Collection[T]` landed in `data_objects.type_name = "DataObject"` (the fallback) because the wrapper has shape `{kind: "collection", item_type: "T", items: [<T-wire>...]}` and the root-level metadata is absent — per-item type_chain lives at `items[i].metadata.type_chain`. Methods MD rendered every Image/Mask output as `Type | DataObject`. The helper now probes the Collection wrapper first (returns `item_type` or recurses into `items[0]`), falls through to existing root-level type_chain logic for non-Collection outputs. 4 new tests in `TestExtractTypeNameCollection`. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/batch-994-1000, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#996] `GET /api/runs/{id}` now inlines per-block I/O DataObjects as `block_executions[i].inputs / .outputs` arrays. ADR-038 §3.7 Q4b "Per-block I/O DataObjects?" SQL was never wired into the route — D38-2.4c left a "clients fetch on demand" placeholder but no such endpoint shipped, so the Lineage tab block cards always rendered "0 inputs / 0 outputs" (Phase 4a finding). New `LineageStore.list_block_io_with_objects(run_id)` runs one batched SELECT joining `block_io ↔ block_executions ↔ data_objects`; route buckets the rows into each `block_execution` as `.inputs` / `.outputs`. Each entry: direction, port_name, position, object_id, type_name, backend, storage_path, produced_by_execution. `wire_payload` excluded — KB-scale per-object JSON would balloon the response. `test_inlines_block_io_inputs_outputs` asserts the seeded DataFrame output renders with port_name + object_id + type_name + storage_path. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/batch-994-1000, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#997] "Restore this run's workflow" (Lineage tab) made reliable. Pre-fix: repeat clicks on a dirty tree accumulated `auto-stash before restore` entries (rendered as commit nodes in the graph) and the user got no feedback when the click was effectively a no-op. Two surgical changes: (1) `git_engine.py::restore` adds a skip-if-unchanged short-circuit — when `files=[<path>]` and the target file's content at the requested commit is byte-identical to the worktree (`git diff --quiet <commit> -- <files>` returns 0), skip BOTH the auto-stash and the `git checkout`; whole-tree variant keeps original semantics. (2) Frontend `runRestoreWorkflow` now returns the `{status, stash_id?}` payload; when status is "stashed" the button renders an amber `role="status"` hint "Your unsaved changes were stashed as <id> — recover via Git tab → Stashes." `test_restore_skips_when_file_unchanged` pins the no-op contract. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/batch-994-1000, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#998] RunsList row's primary visual is now a colored status pill (`bg-emerald-600` / `bg-rose-600` / `bg-amber-500` / `bg-slate-500` + white text). Timestamp moves to the right as a small grey label. Replaces the glyph-icon + small text pattern. Pill text is directly visible to screen readers (no sr-only fallback needed). `runs-list-row-{id}-status-pill` testid added; 36/36 Lineage frontend tests pass. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/batch-994-1000, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#999] RunDetail header metadata `<dl>` switches from `grid-cols-2` (one dt/dd pair per row → ~7 rows) to `grid-cols-[auto_1fr_auto_1fr]` (two pairs per row → ~3-4 rows). Saves ~80px of vertical space so the Blocks list — the primary content per ADR-038 §3.8 — keeps most of the panel height. Blocks section already had `flex-1 overflow-y-auto`; saved space flows there. py-3 → py-2, gap-y-1 → gap-y-0.5, leading-tight on the heading. No data-testid changes. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/batch-994-1000, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#1000] Git tab default view = Graph (was List). Graph button moved LEFT of List in the view-toggle so the default is visually anchored first. Per Phase 4a user feedback: "graph is the primary affordance, list is fallback". One-line `useState("graph")` default flip + JSX reorder; no behavioral change beyond. (@claude, 2026-05-16, branch: hotfix/batch-994-1000, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#992] `/api/workflows/{id}/execute-from` now stamps `runs.parent_run_id` on the new partial-rerun's row to point at the most-recent completed run of that workflow. Per ADR-038 §3.6a the new run's `parent_run_id` "points at the historical run whose outputs are reused"; pre-fix the route called `start_workflow(execute_from=...)` without forwarding a `parent_run_id`, leaving the column NULL and breaking the re-run chain linkage that §3.8 Lineage tab UI depends on (Phase 4a e2e exposed this: the partial-rerun banner rendered correctly but the parent-run-link was empty). The route now resolves `parent_run_id` via `lineage_store.list_runs(workflow_id, limit=1)[0]` and threads it through `runtime.start_workflow`. Lookup failure is logged + non-fatal (the re-run still proceeds with `parent_run_id=NULL`, the pre-fix default). Discovered live during Phase 4b ADR-039 e2e Test 6 follow-up + Phase 4a Lineage tab verification. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/issue-992/execute-from-parent-run-id, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#990] Git graph fork-edge color now follows the **child** lane (the side branch), not the parent lane (the trunk it forks off). Pre-fix, a side-branch dot rendered in its lane color (e.g. green) but the slant edge connecting back to the common-ancestor parent suddenly switched to the main lane's color (blue) mid-stroke — visual discontinuity at every fork point that broke "one branch is one color end-to-end". Cross-implementation survey (mhutchie/vscode-git-graph, IntelliJ Platform, GitLens) all use child-lane color for every edge regardless of primary/merge; only legacy gitk uses parent-lane (which SciStudio's old rule matched). Drop the primary-vs-merge split in `edgeRouter.ts` — `colorBase = childLane` always. ADR-039 §3.5b addendum documents the industry-standard evidence. Fixture B / F updated; new Fixture G synthesizes a V-shaped fork (SIDE/MAIN sharing BASE parent) to pin the contract. 23/23 GitGraph tests pass. Discovered during Phase 4b ADR-039 e2e graph rendering verification. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/issue-990/git-graph-fork-edge-color, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#988] Tree-mutating git endpoints (`/api/git/branch/switch`, `/api/git/restore`, `/api/git/merge`, `/api/git/cherry-pick`, `/api/git/merge/complete`, `/api/git/merge/abort`, `/api/git/stash/apply`) now actively emit `workflow.changed` events per modified workflow YAML, instead of relying on the filesystem watcher. ADR-039 §3.8 originally treated the watcher as the single source of truth for "YAML changed on disk → reload canvas", but watchdog coalesces / drops events when git rewrites many files inside a single debounce window — e2e Test 3 confirmed: branch switch left the canvas showing the previous branch's workflow until manual reload. The endpoints now snapshot SHA-256 of every `workflows/**/*.yaml` before the engine op, diff after, and emit one event per (created / deleted / modified) file with `changed_by="git"` (vs `"watcher"` for the existing filesystem watcher path). The frontend's existing `useWebSocket.ts` `workflow.changed` handler — which already supports the three kinds correctly — reloads the canvas without any new frontend code. ADR-039 §3.8 grew an addendum documenting the decision. Discovered live during Phase 4b ADR-039 e2e Test 3 (branch checkout canvas sync). (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/issue-983/git-utf8-decode, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#983] Pin git subprocess stdout/stderr decode to UTF-8 (with `errors="replace"`) in `GitBinary.run`. On Chinese Windows the default locale is GBK/cp936, and Python's `text=True` auto-decodes subprocess output via that locale. Git always emits UTF-8 (commit messages, author names, paths) regardless of the `LANG=C` / `LC_ALL=C` env we already inject — those localize git's own error strings but not repo data. Any non-GBK byte (em dash in auto-generated commit messages, Chinese chars, emoji) crashed the reader thread with `UnicodeDecodeError`, leaving stdout empty and the frontend rendering "No commits yet" on a healthy repo. Discovered live during Phase 4b ADR-039 e2e Test 1. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/issue-983/git-utf8-decode, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#984] `gitSlice.invalidateHistory` now re-fetches `loadBranches`/`loadStatus`/`loadLog` instead of merely clearing the cache and trusting "the next consumer render" to dispatch fresh fetches. Several state flows (branch switch, post-commit refresh) call it without an associated render, so the cache stayed null and the History panel + BranchPicker showed empty. Companion fix in `BranchPicker.tsx`: a Radix `onOpenChange` handler now dispatches `loadBranches` whenever the dropdown opens with `branches === null`, covering the residual mid-session invalidation window before sibling state flows refetch. Both discovered live during Phase 4b ADR-039 e2e Test 1 + Test 3. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/issue-983/git-utf8-decode, session: n/a-hotfix-mode-§11.5)
- [#981] UX hotfix — bottom panel default size 30% → 45% (so Git tab history list isn't clipped on a 1080p canvas column); Git tab tab-bar icon swapped from the U+1F500 shuffle emoji to Lucide `GitBranch` SVG for consistent rendering across OS font sets and clearer semantic. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/bottom-panel-size-git-icon, session: 20260515-204710-hotfix-bottom-panel-size-gitbranch-icon)

- [#975] MergeFlow modal now mounted at App.tsx level so its mid-conflict close-guard survives BOTH bottom-tab switches AND project switch/close. PR #974 had moved the mount up to `BottomPanel.tsx` to fix the tab-switch unmount (Codex round-1 P1), but `BottomPanel` only renders when `currentProject != null` (the App.tsx `{currentProject ? (...)}` conditional), so closing or switching the active project mid-merge still unmounted the modal and bypassed its Mark Resolved / Complete / Abort guard (Codex round-2 P1 on PR #974, agent-cap deferred per `feedback_wait_for_agent_done_before_merge.md` ONE-Codex-round rule). New `AppLevelMergeFlow` wrapper in App.tsx subscribes to gitSlice so App itself does not re-render on every modal-state change. Vitest 356/356 pass, build clean. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/issue-975/mergeflow-app-level, session: 20260515-194650-hotfix-issue-975-mergeflow-app-level-mou)

- [#978] Phase 3.5 — integrate ADR-038 + ADR-039 tracks and apply the 5 P1 + 5 P2 audit fixes from `docs/audit/2026-05-15-adr-038-039-integration-audit.md` in a single integration PR against `main`. Merge of `track/adr-038/lineage-db` + `track/adr-039/git-versioning` on top of hotfix #977 resolves 11 conflicts. **(P1-1 set_pending_git_commit ordering)** the captured pre-run-auto-commit SHA is now threaded through `_build_lineage_recorder` into the `RunRecord` constructor so the `runs` row carries `workflow_git_commit` at INSERT time — the previous design called `lineage_store.set_pending_git_commit(workflow_id, sha)` from `start_workflow` BEFORE `_build_lineage_recorder` had inserted the row, which silently stamped the SHA on the previous run; the call site is removed. **(P1-2 workflow_dirty plumbing)** the same `_build_lineage_recorder` signature now also accepts `workflow_dirty: bool`; `start_workflow` sets it to `True` when the dirty-tree auto-commit failed so the `runs.workflow_dirty=1` safety net documented in ADR-038 §3.1 + ADR-039 §3.4 is finally live. **(P1-3 delete_project union)** `ApiRuntime.delete_project` now closes the lineage `LineageStore` SQLite handle AND calls `_rmtree_force` (handles read-only `.git/` refs/packs on Windows) — the dead `MetadataStore.get_metadata_store()` shim block from the 039 source is dropped (D38-2.3 collapsed `MetadataStore` to a deprecation shim). **(P1-4 H-D1 RunDetail.tsx add/add)** keeps the ADR-038 full UI body (header dl, BlockExecutionCard list, Re-run, Export methods, parent-run + partial-rerun affordances) and overlays ADR-039's named exports (`RestoreWorkflowButton`, `runRestoreWorkflow`, `workflowYamlPathForRun`, `RunRecordForRestore`); the Restore button is mounted in the action footer next to Re-run / Export methods so reviewers can click straight through the three primary affordances on a single row. **(P1-5)** resolved by P1-4 (no separate code). **(P2-1)** added `tests/api/test_open_project_degraded_modes.py` exercising the 2×2 of (lineage init fails / git init fails) — both subsystems are independently best-effort and the project still opens in any failure mode. **(P2-2)** `/api/git/branch/switch` now calls `runtime.refresh_block_registry()` after `engine.branch_switch` succeeds so per-project custom blocks under `<project>/blocks/` (ADR-039 §3.5b "blocks alongside git") pick up the new branch's source files; refresh failure is non-fatal. **(P2-3)** `RunDetail.test.tsx` split — ADR-038 tests stay in `RunDetail.test.tsx`, ADR-039 Restore helpers move to a new `RunDetail.restore.test.tsx`. **(P2-4)** suppress D38-2.3 `scistudio.core.metadata_store` `DeprecationWarning` at the MCP-tool import boundary (`tools_inspection.py::inspect_data` + `get_lineage`, `tools_qa.py::get_project_info`) so the agent PTY stderr stream stays clean. **(P2-5)** Codex reply-on-comment drift on PRs #926/#927/#960 — posted retroactively on PR open. **Conflicts**: `BottomPanel.tsx` keeps hotfix #977's flat container (no inner card frame, `px-2 py-2`) AND adds both `lineage` and `git` tabs; the legacy `jobs` placeholder is dropped per ADR-038 §3.8 (Lineage subsumes the run-history surface). `store/index.ts` rehydrate-coerce guard normalises stale persisted tab values to `"lineage"`. `store/types.ts` intersection chain ends in `& LineageSlice & GitSlice`. `api.ts` union keeps both `lineage.*` and `git.*` namespaces. `app.py` registers both `runs.router` and `git_routes.router`. `frontend/tsconfig.tsbuildinfo` now ignored by `.gitignore` (was a merge conflict source on every track sync). - [#929] D38-2.3 follow-up — Codex P1 on PR #931: when a `LineageRecorder` is bound, the scheduler's `_persist_output_metadata` is now a no-op so the recorder's `BLOCK_DONE` handler is the authoritative writer of `data_objects` rows and stamps `produced_by_execution = block_execution_id` (the recorder's own allocation). Pre-fix the scheduler pre-upserted with `produced_by_execution=None`, and the recorder's later `INSERT OR IGNORE` was a no-op — leaving the producer FK permanently NULL and breaking ADR-038 §3.7 Q4b joins for normal (non-test) runs. Scheduler-side persist is retained as a fallback for runners that bypass the recorder (CLI / direct tests) where the row's `produced_by_execution` is legitimately NULL because no `block_executions` row exists. Regression test `tests/engine/test_lineage_data_objects_propagation.py` now asserts the FK is stamped end-to-end. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: fix/issue-929/codex-p1-produced-by-execution, session: n/a-codex-followup-no-gate)

- [#976] GUI UX hotfix bundle (4 fixes from a live-debugging round per CLAUDE.md §11.5). **(1) BottomPanel** — delete the redundant `rounded-[1.8rem] bg-white/80 p-4` inner-frame wrapper around tab content and shrink the outer scroll padding from `px-4 py-4` to `px-2 py-2`; the wrapper was a pure visual artefact and was causing horizontal overflow when the panel was narrow. **(2) Resize handle** — switch `ui/resizable.tsx` CSS override from `[data-orientation=*]` (never matched in react-resizable-panels v4) to `[aria-orientation=horizontal]`, so the bottom-panel handle renders as a full-width horizontal strip with a centred grip instead of a 12×24px vertical pill stuck at the canvas's left edge. **(3a) Minimap** — add `initialWidth`/`initialHeight` to each flowNode (280×180 for blocks, 200×80 for annotations, mirrored from `style` for groups) so the MiniMap's `nodeHasDimensions` check passes; without these the minimap was rendering no node rectangles because `onNodesChange` intentionally drops dimension changes. **(3b) Auto-collapse + pin** — bottom panel now collapses on canvas-pane click (unless pinned), re-expands on tab click / node select / error click; a new pin button in the tab strip toggles `bottomPanelPinned` (UISlice) and is implemented via `react-resizable-panels` v4 imperative ref (`panelRef` + `.collapse()` / `.expand()`); `collapsedSize` bumped 3% → 8% to fully show the tab strip; the existing `bottomPanelCollapsed` zustand state is intentionally untouched per parallel debugging. **(4) Block port placement** — move port handles from below the inline-config strip up to `configSection.offsetTop + 14` so port row 1 visually aligns with the first config row, recovering vertical space; variadic blocks' `+` / `×` buttons inherit the new origin automatically. The banner is suppressed for full runs. Upstream-skipped blocks have no `block_executions` row per ADR §3.6a so the blocks list is intentionally partial — the canvas DAG grey-out treatment described in §3.6a is the canvas renderer's responsibility and remains out of scope for the run-detail panel. - [#939] D38-2.4c — frontend Lineage tab IMPL (ADR-038 §6 Phase 3 frontend impl). Fills every skeleton body from PR #937 and wires the slice + components to the backend REST endpoints from PR #936. `frontend/src/store/lineageSlice.ts` replaces all TODO-throwing actions with real implementations: `fetchRuns` calls `api.lineage.getRuns` and on failure preserves prior runs while surfacing the error string; `fetchRunDetail` caches by `run_id`, maps `ApiError(status=404)` to `"Run not found"`, and keeps stale detail visible on subsequent failures; `selectRun` only fires `fetchRunDetail` on cache miss; `toggleBlockExecutionExpanded` flips set membership immutably; `openMethodsDialog` / `openRerunDialog` set the dialog id and ensure detail is cached; `clearLineage` resets every field to its initial value. `frontend/src/lib/api.ts` replaces the five `api.lineage.*` TODO stubs with real fetch calls. Because the merged backend (#936) returns raw SQLite-row shapes that don't match the frontend's `LineageRunSummary` / `LineageBlockExecution` / `LineageRunDetail` types, new adapter helpers (`adaptRunSummary` / `adaptBlockExecution` / `parseJsonObject` / `parseJsonRawObject` / `computeDurationMs`) coerce `workflow_dirty 0|1 → boolean`, parse the `environment_snapshot` + `block_config_resolved` JSON columns, and compute `duration_ms` from `started_at`/`finished_at` when the server doesn't surface it. `getRunMethods` uses raw `fetch` + `.text()` because the backend serves `text/markdown` rather than JSON; `rerunRun` returns `{new_run_id: ""}` as a placeholder since the backend's `POST /api/runs/{id}/rerun` doesn't surface the new run id (RerunDialog refreshes the list after success so the new row appears at the top). `validateRerun` returns an empty `{input_warnings: [], env_warnings: []}` stub — the backend route was deferred from D38-2.4a, so v1 renders the "no drift detected" clean banner; the IMPL contract from the skeleton is preserved so the wiring lights up once the route ships. Backend `block_io` ↔ `data_objects` join is not yet surfaced through the routes, so `LineageBlockExecution.inputs` / `outputs` default to `[]` for v1; the BlockExecutionCard renders the "(none)" placeholder correctly. `frontend/src/components/Lineage/LineageTab.tsx` implements the two-pane root with header (run count + refresh spinner), dismissible error banner with Retry button, `useEffect`-driven mount fetch, `useRef`-guarded auto-refresh that re-fetches when `isRunning` falls from true → false (no new event-bus type needed — reuses the existing `executionSlice.isRunning` flag), keyboard shortcuts (`m` opens methods, `r` opens rerun) that respect `activeElement` to avoid stealing input focus, and project-switch cache invalidation via a `currentProject.id` ref comparison (honors the slice contract without touching the out-of-scope `projectSlice.ts`). `frontend/src/components/Lineage/RunsList.tsx` renders the reverse-chronological list as `role="listbox"` + `role="option"` with `aria-selected`, formatted timestamps via `Intl.DateTimeFormat` (today/yesterday/this-year/older buckets), duration formatter (`Xms` / `X.Ys` / `Xm Ys`), accessible status icons with `aria-hidden` glyph + `sr-only` text label, re-run marker for `parent_run_id`, and a 1Hz live duration counter that only ticks when at least one run is `status="running"` (no wasted re-renders on completed-only lists). `frontend/src/components/Lineage/RunDetail.tsx` renders the four lifecycle cases (empty / loading / error / happy path) with a `<dl>` metadata grid, an ordered `<BlockExecutionCard>` list, and the Re-run / Export methods action footer; `aria-disabled` + `disabled` on Re-run while the run is `status="running"`. `frontend/src/components/Lineage/BlockExecutionCard.tsx` renders the expandable card with `aria-expanded` + `aria-controls`, resolved-params `<pre>`, Inputs / Outputs lists (each row `<code>port[pos]</code> + type + short-id + storage_path`), and a rose-tinted error section when `termination === "error"` and a detail is present. `frontend/src/components/Lineage/MethodsExportDialog.tsx` implements the modal: in-mount fetch via `api.lineage.getRunMethods`, Copy button that uses `navigator.clipboard.writeText` with a 2-second "Copied ✓" flash and falls back to "Could not copy. Try Download." on rejection, Download .md via a `Blob` + synthetic `<a download>` click + `URL.revokeObjectURL` cleanup; Esc closes via a window-scoped `keydown` listener; backdrop click closes. `frontend/src/components/Lineage/RerunDialog.tsx` implements the modal: fires `api.lineage.validateRerun` on mount (advisory; failure falls back to empty warnings, never blocks), renders the green clean banner when warnings are empty or the amber input/env-drift cards when they're not, `handleConfirm` calls `rerunRun` then `fetchRuns()` then `onClose()`, submit error surfaced inline with `aria-live="polite"`. Tests: `frontend/src/store/__tests__/lineageSlice.test.ts` flips all 7 skeleton skip-docs to real assertions (initial state, fetchRuns happy + failure-preserves-prior-runs, fetchRunDetail caching, 404 → "Run not found", selectRun cache-miss-only behaviour, toggleBlockExecutionExpanded idempotency, openMethodsDialog auto-fetch, closeMethodsDialog clears id, clearLineage full reset) — 10 tests passing. `frontend/src/components/Lineage/__tests__/{LineageTab,RunsList,RunDetail}.test.tsx` flip the existing skip-docs to real `render` + `fireEvent` cases against the global `useAppStore` with mocked `api.lineage.*` — 22 tests passing. `cd frontend && vitest run` 230 passed / 13 skipped (the 13 skips are pre-existing unrelated TODOs in other components); `npm run build` (tsc -b + vite) clean with zero TypeScript errors. - [#933] D38-2.4a — backend REST + AIBlock rename (ADR-038 §6 Phase 3 backend). `src/scistudio/api/routes/runs.py` rewritten from the D38-2.2 health-only placeholder to the four ADR-038 §3.7/§3.8 endpoints: `GET /api/runs` (reverse-chrono list with optional `workflow_id` filter + `offset`/`limit` pagination, returns `{runs, offset, limit, has_more}`), `GET /api/runs/{run_id}` (joined run + `block_executions` rows), `GET /api/runs/{run_id}/methods` (markdown body served as `text/markdown; charset=utf-8`), and `POST /api/runs/{run_id}/rerun` (body `{execute_from_block_id?: str}` delegates to `ApiRuntime.start_workflow` so the new run is recorded by the existing LineageRecorder path — surfaces `ValueError` as 400 / `FileNotFoundError` as 404 / unknown run as 404). The `/_health` route is preserved and now declared before `/{run_id}` so the literal segment matches first. New `src/scistudio/core/lineage/methods_export.py::render_methods_markdown` renders the four user questions per ADR-038 §3.7: run identity + git commit + dirty marker (Q1), environment snapshot JSON code-fence (Q1), workflow YAML literal in a yaml code-fence (Q2), per-block `### {block_id}` subsections with config JSON + I/O markdown tables joining `block_io` ↔ `data_objects` (Q3/Q4). Renderer is read-only against `LineageStore`; missing-run returns a "Run not found" body rather than raising. `src/scistudio/blocks/ai/run_dir.py` renames `RunDir.run_id` Python attribute and `__init__(project_dir, run_id)` parameter to `block_execution_id` per ADR-038 §5.2 (path component renamed in lockstep: `<project>/.scistudio/ai-block-runs/<block_execution_id>/`). The agent-facing manifest JSON key `block.run_id` and the engine-surface `PtyTabSpec.block_run_id` field are intentionally kept under their legacy spellings — they are external contracts (ADR-035 §3.4 + ADR-034 freeze respectively); only internal identifiers were renamed. `src/scistudio/blocks/ai/ai_block.py` renames `run_id` local + `_make_run_id` helper to `block_execution_id` + `_make_block_execution_id`; adds an inline ADR-035/ADR-038 cross-reference docstring documenting the rename rationale. `tests/api/test_runs_routes.py` (NEW, 20 tests): TestListRuns (seeded runs / workflow_id filter / pagination / negative offset / excessive limit / no-active-project), TestGetRun (joined detail / 404 / trailing slash / `/_health` not shadowed), TestGetRunMethods (markdown body / 404 / charset / inputs+outputs surfaced), TestRerunRun (started envelope / threads `execute_from_block_id` / 404 unknown run / `ValueError` → 400 / `FileNotFoundError` → 404 / 422 on non-string body). `tests/core/test_methods_export.py` (NEW, 10 tests): happy-path renderer output (Q1-Q4) + edge cases (unknown run → "Run not found" body, no blocks, no workflow_yaml, dirty marker, block without I/O). `tests/blocks/ai/test_run_dir_skeleton.py` updated for the attribute rename. - [#920] D38-2.2 — wire-up + schema for unified lineage (ADR-038 §6 Phase 1). New `src/scistudio/core/lineage/` 4-table package: `store.py` rewritten as `LineageStore` over `runs / block_executions / data_objects / block_io` (~340 LOC, ADR-038 §3.1 schema verbatim, WAL + FK ON); both normal-path and interactive-path emissions are updated. `src/scistudio/engine/runners/local.py` lifts the worker envelope's `environment` field into the returned outputs dict under a `__scistudio_env__` sentinel key that the scheduler pops before storing in `_block_outputs` (downstream blocks never see it). `src/scistudio/api/runtime.py` opens the unified store on `open_project` via new `_init_lineage_store` (closes prior store on project switch), updates `create_project` scaffold list to use `.scistudio/` (legacy `checkpoints/` and `lineage/` top-level dirs retired per ADR §3.5), closes the lineage handle before `delete_project` rmtree to avoid Windows `WinError 32`, and `start_workflow` now builds a `LineageRecorder` (via `_build_lineage_recorder` which seeds the `runs` row with full env + workflow YAML snapshot) and finalizes it via task done-callback. `src/scistudio/api/deps.py::get_lineage_store` returns the runtime-owned shared store instead of allocating a fresh `LineageStore` per request (the orphan dependency is now load-bearing). `src/scistudio/api/app.py` registers a placeholder `runs` router. `src/scistudio/api/routes/runs.py` (NEW) stubs `GET /api/runs/_health` for Phase D38-2.2 smoke testing; in-tree + drop-in blocks stamp `scistudio.__version__`; entry-point + monorepo plugins look up their distribution; no more `"unknown"` default. `src/scistudio/cli/main.py::init` scaffold list aligned with `runtime.py::create_project`. - [#985] ADR-040 production-environment agent reliability engineering — drafted ADR proposing a four-layer reliability stack for the embedded prod-env agent (claude/codex spawned by the SciStudio GUI inside user SciStudio projects). Six decisions: (1) FastMCP 3.x migration replacing the hand-rolled 251-LOC JSON-RPC server, (2) per-project dynamic context injection making the previously-unused `project_dir` argument actually shape the prompt (closes #825), (3) multi-skill split + skill tree relocation `skills/` → `src/scistudio/_skills/` for wheel-install compatibility (closes #832 + #824), (4) prod-env `<project>/CLAUDE.md` + `<project>/AGENTS.md` auto-provisioning with purpose-written content distinct from the dev-env source-repo CLAUDE.md, (5) project-scoped `.claude/settings.json` + 6 Python hook scripts deterministically blocking CLI bypass (`Bash(scistudio *)`), direct workflow YAML edits, block writes without prior `list_blocks` (session-keyed marker), and flagging generic-`DataObject` port types via AST scan (closes #875), (6) Codex parity via newly-supported project-scope `.codex/config.toml` + `scistudio install --skill` cross-install to both `~/.claude/skills/` and `~/.agents/skills/` (fixes the previously-silent prod-env Codex defect where GUI codex tabs got zero MCP tools without manual install). The ADR is scoped exclusively to the production environment — the user's SciStudio project directory — and explicitly carves the development environment (the SciStudio source repo) out of scope (§2.1). All assets auto-installed at `ApiRuntime.create_project` + `cli.main.init` and idempotently topped-up at `open_project`. Sub-deliverable of #903 (umbrella tracking issue stays open for dimensions D overlays + E empirical evaluation). Status: proposed; promotes to accepted after Phase 1 ships FastMCP migration with a green 26-tool parity test. Implementation in 4 phases (~14 working days / 18 files modified / ~370 LOC net change) tracked as separate sub-issues filed after this ADR merges. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: docs/issue-985/adr-040-agent-reliability, session: 20260515-211923-adr-040-production-environment-agent-rel)

- [#947] ADR-039 D39-2.4b frontend Phase-3 IMPL — filled the skeleton bodies from PR #945. **Branch graph (`frontend/src/components/Git/GitGraph/`)**: `laneAssign.ts` implements the ADR §3.5b lane-assignment algorithm (topo-order iteration with active-lane recycling — fresh lanes when no waiting slot is found, merge-parent fold-in into the first null slot, deterministic `color_index = lane mod PALETTE.length`); `edgeRouter.ts` computes per-edge SVG bezier paths (straight verticals when child_lane === parent_lane, S-curves with control points at midY for lane jumps, dangling stubs for parents truncated out of the visible log) and exposes `centerOf(idx, lane)` for the renderer to align dots with edge anchors; `colorPalette.ts::resolveLaneColor` applies the §3.5c filtered-grey rule; `GraphSVG.tsx` renders dots + edges + a sibling DOM column for labels (Approach B from the skeleton docstring), accepts a `visibleRange` for virtualization, and surfaces `data-testid="git-graph-svg"` + `git-graph-dot-{short_sha}` + `git-graph-label-{short_sha}` for tests / Chrome smoke; `interactions.ts::useGraphInteractions` provides scroll-driven manual virtualization (overscan = 10 rows; falls back to render-everything when no container ref is attached — the skeleton's `@tanstack/react-virtual` reference dropped because that package is not in `frontend/package.json` and cascade hygiene forbids worktree dep changes), keyboard arrow navigation, and a click handler that dispatches the caller's `onOpenDiff` callback; `integration.ts::useGraphData` pulls `logCache["<all>"]` + `historyFilter` from gitSlice, memoises `assignLanes` + `routeEdges` on the commits-array reference (`useMemo`) and applies the filter as a cheap O(C) pass that only flips `filtered_out` (does NOT recompute lanes). **Conflict resolution UI**: `ConflictMarkerDecoration.ts::registerConflictDecorations` registers Monaco line-range decorations (current section green / incoming section blue), mounts one `IContentWidget` above each region with `[Accept Current] [Accept Incoming] [Accept Both] [Manual edit]` buttons, listens to `model.onDidChangeContent` and re-applies on every edit, and returns a dispose function that unregisters listeners + clears decorations + removes widgets (no DOM leaks on tab switch); `ConflictMarkerDecoration.ts::resolveRegionText` is a pure splice helper that rewrites the conflict region per `ConflictAction.type` (`accept_current` keeps the ours section, `accept_incoming` keeps theirs, `accept_both` concatenates current+incoming, `manual_edit` leaves the markers untouched); `MergeFlow.tsx` is the full state-machine modal (`idle → in_flight → {success | conflict | error}`; `conflict → completing | aborting → success | conflict`) with kicked-off `gitMerge` on open, auto-close after a 1s success toast, blocked-close while in flight / conflict / completing / aborting (the conflicted working tree must be either Completed or Aborted before closing), `aria-modal="true"`, `data-testid="merge-flow"` + `merge-flow-in-flight` / `merge-flow-conflict` / `merge-flow-success` / `merge-flow-error`; `ConflictResolveView.tsx` renders the per-file list with Open-in-editor + Mark-Resolved buttons, per-file `Unresolved` / `Resolved` status badges with `aria-describedby` linking the Mark-Resolved button to its badge, footer Complete-Merge (`aria-disabled=true` until every file is resolved) + Abort-Merge (which invokes `window.confirm` with the literal copy from ADR §3.5a). **Editor wiring (`CodeEditor.tsx`)**: the `onAction` callback now calls `model.executeEdits("conflict-resolution", [{range, text, forceMoveMarkers: true}])` via `resolveRegionText` so the edit participates in Monaco's undo stack — Ctrl+Z reverts a misclicked Accept Both without losing the markers. **Toolbar wiring (`Toolbar.tsx`)**: `BranchPicker.onMergeRequested` now opens `<MergeFlow sourceBranch={…} isOpen={…} />` rendered outside the toolbar header (no clipping). **History list integration (`GitHistoryList.tsx`)**: added a List / Graph view toggle; the Graph view mounts `GitGraphPane` which composes `useGraphData` + `useGraphInteractions` + `GraphSVG`, scroll-virtualizes via the container ref + ROW_HEIGHT math, and routes `onCommitClick` through `setDiffOpen` so the existing GitDiffModal opens against the clicked commit's parent (or the empty-tree hash for root commits, mirroring the row-click path). **Tests**: 47 new vitest assertions across 4 files — `GitGraph/__tests__/laneAssign.test.ts` (11 tests: maxLane purity + 8 algorithm fixtures incl. linear, two-way merge, 3-parent octopus, two disconnected roots, empty, single-commit, color wrap, mutation-free purity), `GitGraph/__tests__/edgeRouter.test.ts` (11 tests: buildShaIndex + centerOf + 6 path-string fixtures with hard-coded geometry incl. dangling-stub + octopus + color-inheritance rule + self-cycle defensive warn), `Git/__tests__/MergeFlow.test.tsx` (7 tests: fast-forward / clean / conflict / complete / abort / error all via mocked `api.gitMerge*`), `Git/__tests__/ConflictResolveView.test.tsx` (18 tests: parser fixtures preserved + 4 `resolveRegionText` action assertions + 6 view-wiring assertions on Open / Mark Resolved / status badge flip / aria-disabled gating / Complete handler / Abort handler). `vitest run` reports 31 files / 301 pass / 13 skip; `npm run build` clean; `tsc --noEmit` clean. Live Chrome smoke (per dispatch's mandatory clause): not yet recorded — the merge-conflict scenario requires backend running with the bundled git binary; smoke captured + GIF linked in the PR body before merge per the checklist row update. Out of scope (will fail static review if changed): backend Python, other `Git/*` components from D39-2.3a/b (CommitDialog / GitDiffModal / BranchPicker / GitStatusBadge / StashApplyDialog / StashListPanel — touched only via existing import surface), `frontend/src/store/gitSlice.ts` (reuses existing `mergeInProgress.conflicted_files` field per the dispatch's "skeleton agent declined to add `activeConflict` field" note), `frontend/src/lib/api.ts` (existing 18 git wrappers already cover every call this PR makes), ADR-038 / Lineage files, ADR docs. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: feat/issue-947/d39-2-4b-conflict-graph-impl, session: D39-2.4b-impl)

- [#941] ADR-039 D39-2.4a frontend Phase-3 SKELETON — scaffolding for the conflict-resolution UI (Monaco decorations + inline action buttons + merge orchestrator) and the clean-room branch-graph component per ADR-039 §3.5a / §3.5b / §6 Phase 3. ### Fixed

- [#968] ADR-039 D39-3.2 — fix the 5 release-blocking findings from the D39-3.1 combined audit. **P1-A (dual git-watcher collapse)**: deleted the duplicate asyncio-poll `core.versioning.watcher.GitChangeWatcher` that emitted `git.head_changed` with a `head_sha` key, conflicting with the watchdog-based `_GitHeadHandler` in `api/routes/workflow_watcher.py` which emits with `commit_sha` (the key the frontend reads in `useWebSocket.ts`). The watchdog handler is now the single source of truth for the `.git/` watch surface; `api/app.py` no longer constructs a parallel watcher; `core/versioning/__init__.py` no longer re-exports `GitChangeWatcher`. **P1-B (H-A1 defensive guard)**: verified the `getattr` + `callable()` guard at `runtime.py:1333` stays in place so the cross-track `lineage_store.set_pending_git_commit` hook remains a no-op until D38-3.2 ships the receiver; added two regression tests (lineage_store without the method → workflow still starts; lineage_store hook raises → exception swallowed, workflow still starts). **P2-A (AIBlock `agent:` prefix docstring)**: corrected the AIBlock module docstring which claimed enforcement via a non-existent `mcp__scistudio__git_commit` MCP tool — replaced with the actual enforcement path (system-prompt + `git commit -m "agent: …"` typed by the agent in its PTY shell). The MCP-tool wrapper is documented as a future enhancement. **P2-B (project-switch watcher restart)**: resolved for free by the P1-A collapse — `workflow_watcher.WorkflowWatcher.start_for_project` is already invoked from `routes/projects.py::_restart_workflow_watcher` on `GET /api/projects/{id}` so project switch now restarts the unified watcher's `.git/` schedule against the new project. **P2-C (empty-repo commit edge case)**: `GitEngine.commit()` previously used `git diff --cached --quiet` to detect an empty tree, which returns 0 against a missing HEAD (no commits yet) even with a non-empty index — raising a false `nothing to commit` error for the repo's initial commit. Fix branches on `git rev-parse --verify HEAD` and falls back to `git ls-files --cached` when HEAD is absent. **P3 nits** (is_repository worktree handling, merge FF heuristic, log parser empty-body edge) filed as follow-up issue #969 — no current consumer affected. Tests: 5 new cases — 2 in `tests/api/test_app.py` (lifespan no longer constructs git_watcher state + GitChangeWatcher is no longer exported), 2 in `tests/api/test_workflow_run_git.py` (H-A1 defensive guard — no hook + hook-raises), 2 in `tests/core/test_git_engine.py` (P2-C — first commit on no-HEAD succeeds + truly empty index still raises). 203 backend tests pass on the ADR-039 surface (`tests/{core/test_git_engine.py, api/{test_git_endpoints,test_workflow_run_git,test_workflow_watcher_git,test_ws_git_events,test_workflow_watcher,test_app},cli}.py`). Out of scope (untouched): ANY ADR-038 owned file under `src/scistudio/core/lineage/` or `engine/scheduler.py` (D38-3.2 owns the receiver-side fix for H-A1); new feature work; ADR docs structural changes. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: fix/issue-968/d39-3-2-audit-fixes, session: n/a-fix-agent)

- [#923] Codex P2 follow-ups on merged PR #918 (D39-2.1). **P2-A**: filter `*.lock` files in `_GitHeadHandler._classify` so git's transient ref-update lockfiles (e.g. `refs/heads/main.lock`) never emit a `git.head_changed` event with a bogus ref name. **P2-B**: align the `_watched_git_dir` idempotency guard in `WorkflowWatcher.start_for_project` with the `is_dir()` schedule check so worktree projects (where `.git` is a gitlink *file* not a directory) no longer re-tear-down + recreate the observer on every project re-open. Tests: `tests/api/test_workflow_watcher_git.py` adds two cases (`refs/heads/main.lock`, `HEAD.lock`); `tests/api/test_workflow_watcher.py` adds `test_watcher_start_idempotent_when_dotgit_is_a_file_worktree`. ### Changed

- [#972] ADR-039 §3.5 — relocate the Git versioning surface from the top Toolbar into a dedicated `Git` bottom-panel tab and mount the previously orphaned `GitHistoryList`. D39-2.3b shipped `GitHistoryList.tsx` (commit history + List/Graph view toggle + GraphSVG) but never wired it into the production UI, so the entire commit history and branch graph were unreachable from the running app; D39-3.1's audit deferred its Chrome smoke and missed the orphan. The same D39-2.3b drop also mounted BranchPicker + GitStatusBadge + Commit + Stashes inline in `Toolbar.tsx`, which overflowed the viewport on narrow screens and forced a horizontal scrollbar. This PR collapses both issues by moving every Git affordance into a new `frontend/src/components/Git/GitTab.tsx` rendered inside `BottomPanel` (`activeTab === "git"`). The Git tab owns its own modal/drawer state (`commitOpen`, `stashOpen`, `mergeSource`) and mounts BranchPicker + GitStatusBadge + Commit + Stashes in a sticky top bar above `<GitHistoryList />`, then renders `CommitDialog` / `StashListPanel` / `MergeFlow` (which itself renders `ConflictResolveView`) as tab-scoped modals — switching away from the Git tab tears the modals down automatically. `frontend/src/types/ui.ts` extends `BottomTab` with `"git"`; `frontend/src/components/BottomPanel.tsx` adds the new label (`🔀 Git`), the `git` entry in `ALL_TABS`, and the render branch that mounts `<GitTab />`; `frontend/src/components/Toolbar.tsx` removes 5 Git imports (BranchPicker / CommitDialog / GitStatusBadge / MergeFlow / StashListPanel), the 2 lucide icons used only by the Git group (GitCommit / Archive), the `data-testid="git-toolbar-slot"` div + its 4 ToolbarButtons, the `useAppStore` import, the local `useState` declarations for `commitOpen` / `stashOpen` / `mergeSource`, and the 3 dialog mounts at the bottom of the component (~75 LOC removed) — the Toolbar is back to its pre-D39-2.3b non-Git shape. `frontend/src/store/index.ts::onRehydrateStorage` gains a `VALID_BOTTOM_TABS` whitelist coercion so persisted `activeBottomTab` values from old snapshots that contain retired values (e.g. `"problems"`) or unknown values fall back to `"config"` cleanly. NEW tests: `frontend/src/components/Git/__tests__/GitTab.test.tsx` (4 cases: empty-state when no project; top-bar mounts BranchPicker / GitStatusBadge / Commit / Stashes; GitHistoryList renders below the top bar — closes the orphan-mount gap; clicking Commit opens CommitDialog; clicking Stashes opens StashListPanel). All 315 existing vitest assertions remain green (33 files, 13 skips), `npm run build` clean. Out of scope (untouched): backend Python, ADR docs, ADR-038-owned files (LineageTab / lineageSlice — different tracking branch), new Git features beyond the relocation. Live Chrome smoke deferred to manager (`mcp__claude-in-chrome__list_connected_browsers` requires interactive device selection in this worktree). (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: feat/issue-972/git-bottom-panel-tab, session: n/a-impl-agent)

- [#954] ADR-039 D39-2.5 polish + ADR-038 integration — replaced the D39-2.2b TODO marker in `src/scistudio/api/runtime.py::start_workflow` with the final `workflow_git_commit` wiring: (1) the captured post-auto-commit HEAD SHA is now carried on the `WorkflowRun` dataclass via a new `workflow_git_commit: str | None` field so the ADR-038 LineageRecorder reads it when persisting the `runs` row; (2) a defensive forward-compatible hook calls `runtime.lineage_store.set_pending_git_commit(workflow_id, sha)` when the lineage store exposes that method (lands on integrated `main` / `track/adr-038/lineage-db`; no-op on `track/adr-039/git-versioning` alone) — this is the **single intentional cross-track edit before Phase 3 audits** per the dispatch. - [#925] ADR-039 D39-2.2b backend IMPL — flipped the skeleton from PR #924 to real bodies. `scistudio.core.versioning.git_engine.GitEngine` now subprocess-invokes the bundled git CLI with plumbing-only flags (`--porcelain=v2`, `--format=...`, `for-each-ref`, `rev-parse`) and structured `GitError` envelopes (returncode + stderr + git_args). `init_repository` writes the default `.gitignore` (per ADR §3.3), stages everything, and uses `-c user.name/email` injection so the initial commit succeeds on a fresh machine without global git config. `commit` accepts `prefix in {"auto","agent"}` per ADR §3.4 / §3.4a, rejects empty messages and clean trees (409). `log` returns the structured dict shape (sha, short_sha, parents, author_name/email/date, subject, body, branches). `diff`, `restore` (with auto-stash on dirty tree per §3.6), `branches`, `branch_create / switch / delete`, `status` (full porcelain v2 parser bucketing into modified/staged/untracked/conflicted), `head_state`, `merge` (FF / clean / conflict classification), `cherry_pick`, `stash_list / save / apply / drop`, `merge_stage_file / complete / abort` all real. `GitBinary.locate()` checks bundle paths (Windows MinGit at `resources/git/cmd/git.exe` + Linux/macOS `resources/git/bin/git`) with `SCISTUDIO_GIT_BUNDLE_ROOT` env override, falls back to `shutil.which("git")` for the dev CLI, raises `BundledGitMissing` with the full tried-path list otherwise. `GitChangeWatcher` (`watcher.py`) polls `.git/HEAD` + every loose `.git/refs/heads/*` mtime on a 1s tick, emits `git.head_changed` with `{project, head_sha, branches_changed[]}` via the runtime event bus. `scistudio.api.routes.git` — all 21 endpoints functional with structured GitError → HTTP code mapping (`unknown revision` → 404, `nothing to commit` / `cannot delete` / `conflicted entries remain` → 409, `still has conflict markers` → 409); `/api/git/status` returns empty defaults rather than 500 when git is unavailable; the `SCISTUDIO_ENABLE_GIT_ROUTER` opt-in gate is removed (the router is unconditionally registered now). `scistudio.api.app` lifespan installs the `GitChangeWatcher` against the active project on startup + tears it down in `finally`. `scistudio.api.runtime` — `create_project` auto-inits the git repo immediately after writing `project.yaml` + scaffolding `workflows/main.yaml`; `open_project` re-inits silently when `.git/` is absent and no `.scistudio/no_git` opt-out marker is present (per §3.2 / §3.9); `start_workflow` runs the pre-run auto-commit hook (`auto:` prefix per §3.4) and captures the resulting HEAD SHA into a `workflow_git_commit` local (lineage-row write deferred to D39-2.5 once ADR-038's schema lands on this tracking branch). `delete_project` now closes the per-project MetadataStore (ADR-032) before rmtree and uses the new `_rmtree_force` helper to chmod-and-retry past git's read-only object files on Windows. The known-projects prune logic checks both `is_dir()` AND `project.yaml.is_file()` so sqlite WAL residue can't keep stale entries alive. `scistudio.cli.main::init` calls `GitEngine.init_repository` on CLI-created projects, gracefully degrading with a `WARNING: git binary unavailable` line if `BundledGitMissing` fires (per §3.9). `desktop/scripts/fetch-git-portable.ps1` and `.sh` carry full download / SHA-256-verify / extract / smoke-test / sentinel logic; SHA-256 values are placeholders (`<PASTE-VERIFIED-SHA-256-HERE>`) and the desktop maintainer must paste verified hashes on the first version bump (or set `SCISTUDIO_SKIP_GIT_SHA_VERIFY=1` for initial bring-up). Tests: 38 new engine cases (`tests/core/test_git_engine.py`), 28 endpoint cases (`tests/api/test_git_endpoints.py`), 2 CLI cases (`tests/cli/test_init_git_init.py`); all xfail markers from D39-2.2a removed. Out of scope: D38-2.2 lineage schema integration (handled in D39-2.5), frontend Git UI (D39-2.3a/b), conflict resolution UI (D39-2.4a/b). (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: feat/issue-925/d39-2-2b-backend-impl, session: 20260515-081835-d39-2-2b-backend-engine-rest-auto-init-i)

- [#921] ADR-039 D39-2.2a backend SKELETON — scaffolding for the bundled-git-CLI engine, the ~15-endpoint REST surface, the auto-init project lifecycle hooks, and the desktop fetch-portable-git build scripts. All callables raise `NotImplementedError` with ≥20-line comment blocks describing the implementation algorithm (subprocess flags, parsing strategy, error envelopes, edge cases, test plan, ADR references) so D39-2.2b can fill bodies without re-reading ADR-039. NEW: `src/scistudio/core/versioning/{__init__.py, git_engine.py, git_binary.py, gitignore_template.py, status.py, watcher.py}`, `src/scistudio/api/routes/git.py`, `desktop/scripts/fetch-git-portable.{ps1,sh}`.
