- [#915] ADR-039 D39-2.1 refactor — remove `bump_revision` / `current_revision` / `If-Match` optimistic-concurrency layer from the workflow API and add a `git.head_changed` engine event surface to the existing `workflow_watcher`. `src/scistudio/api/runtime.py` drops the `_workflow_revisions` dict + the `current_revision` / `bump_revision` methods + the project-switch reset + the `delete_workflow` cleanup. `src/scistudio/api/routes/workflows.py` drops the `If-Match` header parsing, the 412 `Precondition Failed` branch, the `_parse_if_match` helper, and the `WorkflowConflictResponse` model usage; `_emit_workflow_changed` still fires for every successful write (cross-tab cache invalidation rides on the existing `workflow.changed` event flow) but the payload no longer carries `revision`. `src/scistudio/api/schemas.py` drops `WorkflowResponse.revision` (no frontend consumer — grep clean) and `WorkflowConflictResponse` (only reachable from the deleted 412 branch). `src/scistudio/engine/events.py` gains a `GIT_HEAD_CHANGED = "git.head_changed"` constant (single authorized addition to the EventBus contract per cascade boilerplate, ADR-039 §3.8). `src/scistudio/api/routes/workflow_watcher.py` gains a new `_GitHeadHandler` class that watches `<project>/.git/HEAD` + `<project>/.git/refs/heads/*` mtime changes, resolves symbolic refs to their tip SHA, filters out `packed-refs` / `index` / `logs/HEAD` / `ORIG_HEAD` / `MERGE_HEAD` churn, and reuses the existing 200ms per-path debounce window; `WorkflowWatcher.start_for_project` now schedules a second watch on the project's `.git/` alongside the existing `workflows/` watch when one exists (silently skipped for non-git projects — D39-2.2b auto-init populates `.git/` later). `src/scistudio/api/ws.py` adds `GIT_HEAD_CHANGED` to `_OUTBOUND_EVENTS` so connected clients receive the JSON frame. `src/scistudio/ai/agent/mcp/tools_workflow.py` refreshes the stale #732 TODO that referenced the removed `If-Match` layer. Frontend stub in `frontend/src/hooks/useWebSocket.ts` handles the `git.head_changed` frame with a `console.debug` placeholder + `TODO(D39-2.3a)` for the upcoming `gitSlice.invalidate` wiring. Tests: `tests/api/test_workflow_watcher_git.py` (10 cases: symbolic HEAD, detached HEAD, `refs/heads/<branch>` incl. nested `feature/x`, churn filter for packed-refs/index/logs/HEAD, debounce coalescing + post-window emission, unreadable-HEAD resilience), `tests/api/test_ws_git_events.py` (3 cases: allowlist membership, WS frame forwarding, null-`commit_sha` resilience). `tests/api/test_workflows.py` drops 8 revision/If-Match tests; rewrites the `workflow.changed` flow tests for the new payload shape (no `revision`); adds an explicit assertion that legacy `If-Match` clients are no longer 412'd. `frontend/src/hooks/useWebSocket.test.ts` drops a stale `revision: 7` from the `workflow.changed` fixture. ### Added

- [#934] D38-2.4b — frontend Lineage tab skeleton (ADR-038 §6 Phase 3 frontend). New `frontend/src/components/Lineage/` directory with six skeleton components — `LineageTab.tsx` (two-pane root per ADR-038 §3.8), `RunsList.tsx` (reverse-chrono left pane), `RunDetail.tsx` (right pane with Re-run + Export methods affordances), `BlockExecutionCard.tsx` (expandable per-block view with resolved params + I/O DataObject list), `MethodsExportDialog.tsx` (markdown preview + copy + download .md), `RerunDialog.tsx` (input + env validation warnings per ADR §3.6). Each file carries a ≥30-line top-of-file comment block covering props, state shape, layout markup pseudocode with `data-testid` selectors vitest will assert on, English copy strings (frozen for v1), keyboard shortcuts, ARIA / accessibility requirements, and edge cases (empty / loading / error / stale data states); function bodies throw `new Error("TODO: D38-2.4c — ...")`. New `frontend/src/store/lineageSlice.ts` declares the full state shape (`runs / runsLoading / runsError / selectedRunId / runDetails / runDetailLoading / runDetailError / expandedBlockExecutionIds / methodsDialogRunId / rerunDialogRunId`) and action signatures (`fetchRuns / fetchRunDetail / selectRun / toggleBlockExecutionExpanded / openMethodsDialog / closeMethodsDialog / openRerunDialog / closeRerunDialog / clearLineage`) with TODO-throwing bodies. New `frontend/src/types/lineage.ts` is the single source of truth for the Lineage REST wire-shape types — `LineageRunSummary / LineageBlockExecution / LineageDataObjectRef / LineageRunDetail` mirror the ADR-038 §3.1 schema, plus endpoint envelopes (`LineageGetRunsResponse / LineageMethodsResponse / LineageRerunValidation / LineageRerunResponse`); both the slice and `lib/api.ts` import from this module to keep the import graph acyclic. `frontend/src/lib/api.ts` adds an `api.lineage.*` namespace with typed function stubs (`getRuns`, `getRun`, `getRunMethods`, `validateRerun`, `rerunRun`) that throw TODO; the URL shapes target D38-2.4a's `src/scistudio/api/routes/runs.py` (parallel PR, same tracking branch `track/adr-038/lineage-db`). `frontend/src/components/BottomPanel.tsx` removes the `"jobs"` entry from `ALL_TABS` + the `TAB_LABELS["jobs"]` placeholder and mounts `<LineageTab/>` when `activeTab === "lineage"`. `frontend/src/types/ui.ts` drops `"jobs"` from the `BottomTab` discriminated union per ADR-038 §3.8 (Jobs tab subsumed by Lineage). `frontend/src/store/{index,types}.ts` register `LineageSlice` in the `AppStore` composition. Test stubs: `frontend/src/components/Lineage/__tests__/{LineageTab,RunsList,RunDetail}.test.tsx` + `frontend/src/store/__tests__/lineageSlice.test.ts` use `it.skip(...)` with detailed numbered IMPL docstrings (24 cases across the four files, plus BlockExecutionCard interactions covered via RunDetail.test.tsx); 31 new tests cleanly skip under `vitest run`. `cd frontend && npm run build` clean. D38-2.4c IMPL fills function bodies + flips it.skip to it. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: feat/issue-934/d38-2-4b-lineage-skeleton, session: 20260515-103126-d38-2-4b-frontend-lineage-tab-skeleton)
- [#897] ADR-038 + ADR-039 proposed — unified history model (run lineage + git versioning). ADR-038 collapses `metadata.db` (ADR-032, superseded) and the dormant `lineage.db` schema into a single `<project>/.scistudio/lineage.db` with four normalized tables (`runs`, `block_executions`, `data_objects`, `block_io`) and wires the existing-but-never-constructed `LineageRecorder` into the production scheduler path. Investigation confirmed the dormancy: both `DAGScheduler` construction sites (`api/runtime.py:969`, `cli/main.py:187`) omit `lineage_recorder=`, the BLOCK_DONE event data carries only `{workflow_id, outputs}` (none of the keys `LineageRecorder._on_terminal` reads), no content hashing happens anywhere in the engine, and `api/deps.py::get_lineage_store` has zero call sites. ADR-038 fixes all five by extending BLOCK_DONE event data with `config / block_version / environment / input_object_ids / output_object_ids`, force-injecting `block_version` from `importlib.metadata.version(<distribution>)` at `BlockRegistry.scan()` time (replacing the default `"unknown"`), capturing full `uv pip freeze` as `environment_snapshot` (replacing the 5-package default), lifting the worker envelope's `environment` field into the event data at `runners/local.py:229`, and constructing `LineageRecorder` in `ApiRuntime.start_workflow` with the run row already inserted. Architectural stance: no per-run data isolation directories, no content hashing, no retention policy or GC — the recipe (workflow YAML snapshot + resolved params + environment + git commit SHA) is preserved and re-runnable, which matches the Fiji / ImageJ / GraphPad scientific-software norm of "keep the recipe, not the artifacts". Re-run validates input file `size_bytes + mtime_at_write` and environment drift as advisory-only warnings. `data_objects.wire_payload` is KB-scale per object per ADR-031 reference-only contract (StorageReference + framework/meta/user); even 1000-item Collections produce ~MB of rows, no compression needed. Block author contract unchanged; AI Block (ADR-035) internal `run_id` renamed to `block_execution_id` to align with the new top-level concept. UI scope: implements the existing-but-empty Lineage tab in `BottomPanel.tsx:26` as a two-pane runs-list + run-detail surface; removes the Jobs tab at `BottomPanel.tsx:27` (also empty). `runs.execute_from_block_id` column added to capture "Run from here" provenance; partial-DAG re-execution records only executed blocks (skipped upstream blocks get no row in the new run). **ADR-012 checkpoint scope unchanged**: pause/resume + "Run from here" works against the most-recent-run checkpoint only; older historical runs are recipe-only and require full re-execution from start to reproduce (intermediate data is overwritten by subsequent runs per the no-per-run-isolation decision §3.5). ADR-039 establishes **bundled-git-CLI**-backed source version control: every SciStudio project becomes a git repository auto-init'd on first open via the bundled portable git binary (MinGit on Windows ~30 MB, static-built git on macOS / Linux ~25 MB) — chosen over `pygit2` (libgit2 binding, ~3 MB) for cross-platform reliability, 100% bug-for-bug compatibility with external git tools, and universal debugging ("paste this command in a terminal"). Default `.gitignore` excludes `data/`, `.scistudio/`, `__pycache__/`. **Pre-run auto-commit is ON by default** — when a workflow run starts against a dirty working tree, SciStudio squash-commits the changes with an `auto: pre-run @ <ts> (run=..., workflow=...)` message and the run's `lineage.db.runs.workflow_git_commit` field is set to the post-commit HEAD SHA. The GUI history panel filters `auto:` and `agent:` prefixes by default ("Manual milestones" view) so the curated commit log stays readable; "All" / "Auto only" / "Agent only" filters available. Agent commits (from ADR-034 embedded coding agent or ADR-035 AI Block) use `agent:` prefix and render with a 🤖 icon. Users can disable pre-run auto-commit in Settings; the lineage layer's `workflow_yaml_snapshot` field is the reproducibility safety net if disabled. Branch operations are **full set in v1** (driven by agent collaboration: agents work on their own branches, users merge back): commit / history (with filter) / diff (via `react-diff-viewer-continued`) / restore / branch list/switch/create/delete / **merge** (fast-forward / clean three-way / conflict path) / **cherry-pick** / **stash list+save+apply+drop** / **branch graph visualization**. Conflict resolution reuses the ADR-036 Monaco editor with conflict-marker decorations + inline action widgets (Accept Current / Accept Incoming / Accept Both / Manual edit) — no new editor component, no third-party 3-way merge library. Branch graph visualization is a **clean-room implementation** at `frontend/src/components/Git/GitGraph/` (lane assignment + edge routing + SVG rendering + interactions, ~1500 LOC) after evaluating and rejecting CommitGraph (supply-chain risk: single maintainer, 28 stars), `@gitgraph/react` (archived), `mhutchie/vscode-git-graph` (custom license forbidding derivative redistribution), and embedding VS Code's git module (not architecturally separable from the extension host). Remote push/pull and Git LFS remain explicitly out of scope; rebase / bisect / submodule UI also deferred (CLI works). The in-memory `bump_revision` / `If-Match` optimistic-concurrency flow is removed in favor of git commit SHA + working-tree dirty state. Sibling join key: `runs.workflow_git_commit` from ADR-038 records the SHA each run executed against. Documentation impact (per each ADR's §5.3): substantial rewrite of `docs/architecture/ARCHITECTURE.md` §4.4 (Data lineage), new top-level "History and versioning model" section explaining the two-layer split, `docs/architecture/PROJECT_TREE.md` add `.git/` + `.scistudio/lineage.db` and remove `metadata.db`, `docs/adr/ADR-032.md` status flip to `superseded by ADR-038`, plus alignment edits to ADR-012/018/020/027/031 and `docs/block-development/*` for the metadata→lineage terminology cleanup. Implementation phases tracked as separate post-merge issues (wire-up + schema → metadata.db collapse → frontend Lineage tab + AI Block rename → pygit2 engine + auto-init → frontend Git UI → integration). MCP server intentionally NOT extended: agents query `lineage.db` via SQL and run `git` via bash in their PTY; a `skills/scistudio/SKILL.md` update documenting the schema + git availability is a separate post-merge issue. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: docs/issue-897/adr-038-039-lineage-and-git, session: 20260515-021657-add-adr-038-run-lineage-adr-039-git-vers)
- [#894] ADR-037 proposed — Desktop Application Packaging, Plugin Distribution, and First-Run Dependency Management. New `docs/adr/ADR-037.md` (~820 lines, status `proposed`) covers the architectural decisions for shipping SciStudio as a double-click-installable desktop app targeting non-technical scientists. Three coupled subsystems plus full distribution policy: (a) packaging = Electron + `python-build-standalone` + Vite static frontend, with the SciStudio runtime decoupled from the packaging tech (no SciStudio core module imports Electron); (b) plugin distribution = PyPI piggyback (naming convention `scistudio-plugin-*` + trove classifier `Framework :: SciStudio`), `pyproject.toml` `[tool.scistudio]` manifest, three tiers (Verified / Community / Sideload), bundled-`uv` per-plugin venvs, heavy-deps fetched from plugin-author GitHub Releases, in-app plugin browser; (c) first-run UX = ClaudePrism-style per-dep cards in a non-blocking right-side drawer, with "Install all" convenience button, silent background `check_<dep>_status` returning structured version-compatibility, ANSI-stripped streaming subprocess output with synthetic step progress, `osascript` for macOS admin elevation. New §3.11 release policy: three channels (stable monthly / beta weekly / nightly per-merge), download-aside atomic-swap updates with N-1 version rollback retained 30 days, independent SemVer for core vs plugin API, forward-only schema migrations for workflow YAML + metadata.db with `.bak` snapshots, 2-minor-version deprecation windows, opt-in `<project>/scistudio-plugins.lock` for cross-machine reproducibility. Signing phased v0 unsigned (advanced users only) → v0.5 SignPath.io for Windows OSS → v1 Apple Developer Program + Windows EV Authenticode. Plugin security § with 7-row threat-model table + 7-layer defense-in-depth ordering + explicit declaration of three classes of attack not defended in v1 (Sideload risk, Verified-post-compromise without v2 enforcement, network-level attacks on PyPI). New §5 file-level impact: ~6900 new LOC across `desktop/` (Electron shell), `src/scistudio/plugins/`, `src/scistudio/paths.py`, `src/scistudio/telemetry/`, frontend `Setup/` `Settings/` `FirstRun/` components, new store slices, CI release workflows; ~700 LOC mechanical `platformdirs` migration across 25 existing files. New §7 Distribution Test Matrix: 38 validation points across Windows (W1-W10), macOS (M1-M10), Linux (L1-L8), cross-cutting (X1-X10), with explicit automation-vs-manual coverage tagging. §5.4 enumerates 8 ADRs (017/019/029/031/032/034/035/036) whose architectural surfaces this ADR explicitly does NOT touch — purely additive, zero core files deleted. Implementation phases (Bootstrap PoC → first-run UX → plugin system → signing → polish) tracked as separate issues after this ADR merges in proposed status. Reference precedents source-verified: ClaudePrism (`apps/desktop/src-tauri/src/{claude,uv,skills}.rs`), Langflow / ComfyUI / Dify / n8n plugin distribution models, sibling `zjzcpj/ihhdmodel-desktop` for the macOS quarantine-bit trap explanation. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: docs/issue-894/adr-037-desktop-packaging, session: 20260515-003654-add-adr-037-desktop-application-packagin)

### Fixed

- [#962 #909] Eliminate TOCTOU race between AI Block MCP-signal writer and `CompletionWatcher` reader. `tests/blocks/ai/conftest.py::StubAgent._emit` was writing `signals/finish_ai_block.json` (and the sibling `mark_done.json` + deliberate-error file) via `Path.write_text`, which opens the target with mode `"w"` and **truncates to 0 bytes before** writing data. The watcher polling on the main thread had a non-zero chance of reading the 0-byte file inside that window and re-raising `json.JSONDecodeError("Expecting value: line 1 column 1 (char 0)")` as `ValueError("AIBlock completion: malformed MCP signal …")`. This surfaced as ~1-in-30 flakes on Python 3.11 (occasionally 3.13) across all AIBlock skeleton tests — repeatedly hit during the ADR-038 / ADR-039 cascade (PR #926, #931, #940, #944) and cleared only by `gh run rerun --failed`. Issue #909 tracked the first-noticed symptom. Fix replaces the three non-atomic writes in `_emit` with a shared `_atomic_write_signal` helper using `tempfile.mkstemp` + `os.replace` (mirrors the existing production `scistudio.ai.agent.mcp.tools_workflow._atomic_write_text` pattern). Production `mcp__scistudio__finish_ai_block` already used the atomic helper, so no production write site changed — confirmed via `grep finish_ai_block src/`. The non-atomic `mark_done.json` write in `api/ws.py:118` was left as-is because `completion.py:218` swallows JSON errors on that path via `contextlib.suppress`. New `tests/blocks/ai/test_completion_race.py` ships two deterministic regression tests coordinated with `threading.Event`: `test_non_atomic_writer_loses_race` drives a buggy writer and asserts the watcher raises `ValueError` (documents the failure mode); `test_atomic_writer_wins_race` drives the atomic writer and asserts the watcher returns a `MCP_FINISH_TOOL` event cleanly (regression lock). Verified `pytest tests/blocks/ai/ tests/ai/` 57+ pass with no flakes. Checklist row "AI Block MCP-signal write/read race" in `docs/planning/adr-038-039-checklist.md` flipped to RESOLVED. Reader-side retry (option C in the checklist) intentionally NOT taken — it would weaken the watcher contract and mask future real writer-crash bugs. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: fix/issue-962/ai-block-atomic-signal-write, session: 20260515-160655-fix-962-atomic-write-for-aiblock-mcp-sig)
- [#898 #899] Data Preview panel — source filename in pill labels + single-slider 3-D viewer. **#898** (frontend-only): `extractRefEntries` walks `blockOutputs[block_id]` and resolves each `data_ref` to a friendly display name from `metadata.framework.source` (LoadImage) → `metadata.meta.source_file` (typed Image.Meta) → `metadata.meta.file_path` (Artifact) → truncated-ref fallback. Pill at `DataPreview.tsx:552` renders the filename (e.g. `1000nm_2800-3200-40.tif`) instead of `data-873de`. **#899**: `runtime.py::preview_data` image branch rewritten to (a) read `axes` from the wire format (set by `_serialise_extra_metadata` in `core/types/array.py`), (b) pick the (y, x) plane via axis labels or numpy convention (last two dims), (c) select the first non-(y, x) dim as the slider axis, (d) accept `?slice=N` query param (clamped to `[0, size-1]`, never 400), (e) emit `shape` as the FULL original ndim plus `axes`, `slice_axis_name`, `slice_axis_size`, `slice_index`. Frontend renders a horizontal `<input type="range">` slider in `ImageViewer` when `slice_axis_size > 1`, labeled e.g. `lambda (40)` with position `[N+1]/total`; 200 ms debounce on drag; local `sliceCacheRef: Map<refSliceKey, DataPreviewResponse>` for instant re-drag to cached positions. Zoom / pan / LUT / min-max display state persists across slice transitions because `ImageViewer` is never unmounted — the preview memo falls back to ANY cached slice for the same ref while a new slice is in flight, and the slider position is driven from parent `currentSliceByRef` state (not from `preview.slice_index`, which would snap back to a stale value). New spec at `docs/specs/data-preview-3d-viewer.md` documents the contract, the (y, x) detection precedence, and the v2 deferred items (RGB composite, multi-slider for ndim>3, lambda-click-spectrum, zarr partial reads). 5 new pytest cases in `tests/api/test_data.py` (ndim=2, (y,x,c), (z,y,x), no-axes fallback, `?slice=` clamping); 3 new vitest cases in `frontend/src/components/DataPreview.test.tsx` (filename pill resolution, slider rendered when `slice_axis_size > 1`, no slider for ndim=2). Live-verified via Chrome MCP in `microplastic-calibration`: `srs_calibrate` Done (`(40, 320, 320)` `axes=["lambda","y","x"]`) shows pills `1000nm_2800-3200-40.tif` etc., badge `40 × 320 × 320 | 100%`, slider `lambda (40) 13/40` after drag to position 12, image `src` changes between positions, zoom 156% and viridis LUT survive the drag; `max_project` Done (`(320, 320)`) shows no slider and badge `320 × 320 | 100%`. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: feat/issue-899/preview-panel-3d-viewer, session: 20260515-022426-preview-panel-source-filename-in-pills-3)
- [#879] Scaffold `workflows/main.yaml` on `POST /api/projects/` so the default "main" canvas tab has a real on-disk file from the moment a project is created. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/2026-05-15-session, session: n/a-hotfix-no-gate)
- [#878] View source on a fresh-but-unsaved workflow no longer pops a native `alert("<id> 不存在")`. The `onViewSource` handler in `frontend/src/App.tsx` now `await`s `saveWorkflow()` before calling `openFileTab(workflows/<id>.yaml, {readOnly: true})` so the YAML always exists on disk at open time. Native `alert()` was automation-hostile (blocks Chrome MCP) and a poor UX. Together with #879, the natural "new project → View source" path now works end-to-end. Live-verified via Chrome MCP: hooked `window.alert`, clicked View source on a brand-new project; `alerts: []` (no native alert fired) and the "main.yaml (source)" tab opened with content rendered. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/2026-05-15-session, session: n/a-hotfix-no-gate)
- [#871] CodeEditor lint responses now carry a request-version guard so out-of-order arrivals cannot repaint stale markers. `frontend/src/components/CodeEditor.tsx::runLint` bumps a monotonic `lintRequestIdRef` per scheduled lint, tags each in-flight request, and discards responses (both pre- and post-JSON-parse) whose tag is below the latest. Live-verified via Chrome MCP: mocked `/api/lint/python` so request #1 (3s delay, code `STALE1`) returns AFTER request #2 (0.5s delay, code `LATEST2`); Monaco model markers show only `LATEST2`. Without the guard, request #1's response would have overwritten #2. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/2026-05-15-session, session: n/a-hotfix-no-gate)
- [#870] File-tab autosave debounce timers now live in a `useRef<Map>` outside the effect closure, so editing one tab no longer cancels every other dirty tab's pending save. The previous `useEffect` had `[tabs]` as a dep and tore down all timers on every keystroke; continuously typing in tab A meant tab B's 800ms debounce never reached zero. The rewrite in `frontend/src/App.tsx` prunes only timers for tabs that are no longer dirty/present and resets a per-tab timer only when its OWN content changes. A separate unmount-only effect clears the map defensively. Live-verified via Chrome MCP: opened `blocks/foo.py` + `blocks/bar.py`; made bar dirty once; rapid-typed in foo (100ms cadence for 1.5s); `PUT /file?path=blocks/bar.py` fired at T+~0.8s (during foo-typing) and `PUT /file?path=blocks/foo.py` fired at T+~2.3s (after typing stopped). Before fix, bar.py would never have been saved during foo-typing. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/2026-05-15-session, session: n/a-hotfix-no-gate)
- [#869] `openFileTab` now refetches when an existing tab is stuck in `loading: true` (e.g. after `localStorage` rehydrate strips `content` and sets `loading: true` per ADR-036 §3.11). The previous early dedup-return left the rehydrated placeholder permanently empty. New `needsRefetch = existing && kind === "file" && loading` falls through to focus the existing slot, fire the GET, and replace the placeholder with populated content on success. Repopulation reads the current tab from store at `.then()` time so the path is identical for fresh-create and refetch. Live-verified via Chrome MCP: patched `fetch` to delay `/file` 4s, clicked View source, switched to canvas tab, clicked View source again while source tab was still loading — second click fired a second `GET /api/projects/{id}/file?path=workflows%2Fmain.yaml` (refetch path) instead of returning early. (@claude, 2026-05-15, branch: hotfix/2026-05-15-session, session: n/a-hotfix-no-gate)
- [#883 #884] ADR-035 hotfix-2 — variadic AI Block port config + MCP env propagation. (1) `src/scistudio/engine/runners/worker.py:266` now instantiates the block as `block_cls(config=config)` instead of `block_cls()`; the previous form left `self.config = BlockConfig()` empty so variadic-port blocks (ADR-029 D1) read the static class-level `result` port instead of the user-configured `metadata` port from `self.config["output_ports"]`, and the CompletionWatcher / output validator monitored the wrong file (#883). (2) Engine-initiated PTY spawn now threads `extra_env` from `open_engine_initiated_tab` → `_spawn` → `spawn_claude` / `spawn_codex` → `PtyProcess.__init__`, injecting `SCISTUDIO_AI_BLOCK_RUN_DIR=str(run_dir_path)` into the child env; the `finish_ai_block` MCP tool's `_resolve_ai_block_run_dir()` already checked this env var but it had no producer, so every call returned `not_in_ai_block_context` and ADR-035 §3.5 path (a) was dead-on-arrival (#884). Validated live in ADR-035 e2e (4-image LoadImage → AIBlock → Save): manifest declares the user-config `metadata` port, FileWatcher (path b) detects `outputs/metadata.csv`, SaveData writes `metadata_saved.csv` with the expected rows. Path a (MCP `finish_ai_block`) plumbing is correct but runtime-unverified this round — Anthropic API was 529 Overloaded throughout the test window so claude could not invoke any tools. (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: hotfix/adr-035-port-config-and-mcp-tool, session: 20260514-205138-hotfix-2-ai-block-port-config-mcp-env-pr)
- [#880] ADR-035 hotfix — three live-debug fixes for the AI Block PTY path. (1) **CLI exports `SCISTUDIO_ENGINE_API_URL`** before uvicorn forks workers (`scistudio/cli/main.py` `gui` + `serve`) — companion to the `SCISTUDIO_ENGINE_IPC_TOKEN` export from #873 audit P1-B. Before this, every AIBlock crashed at PTY spawn with `RuntimeError: AIBlock: PTY spawn failed: request_pty_tab: SCISTUDIO_ENGINE_API_URL is not set` because workers had no way to call back to the engine for tab allocation. (2) **AIBlock inline node UI reordered**: `user_prompt` (textarea) + `provider` + `permission_mode` now have `ui_priority` 1/2/3 so they render on the canvas card; `input_ports` / `output_ports` lose their `ui_priority` and fall back to the side-panel port editor (where the editor has room). Previously the canvas card showed the two `[object Object]` port-editor strings + provider — useless for actually authoring the agent's task. (3) **`_scistudio_command_for_env` switches from `shutil.which("scistudio")` to `(sys.executable, ["-m", "scistudio"])`** so `<project>/.scistudio/mcp.json` always pins the same scistudio install as the engine — previously a stale `.venv-agent-test\Scripts\scistudio.EXE` on PATH would pin the wrong scistudio in every project's mcp.json and claude's MCP bridge silently failed (visible to user as "MCP servers failed" inside the AI Block PTY, killing path (a) of ADR-035 §3.5). Live e2e in Chrome confirmed: PTY spawn no longer crashes, canvas card shows the right fields, claude TUI no longer reports MCP server failures. CLAUDE.md §11.5 also gains an "on entering hotfix mode" rule (must re-read the relevant ADR + arch docs before any code edit, to ground against hallucination — gate workflow's change-plan checkpoint is suspended in hotfix mode so this is the only ground-truth pass). Out of scope and tracked separately: #881 prompt auto-submit (claude TUI consumes `\r`s for first-run welcome banners, no clean fix today), #882 conditional-AND completion semantics (ADR-035 §3.5 amend), #883 `get_effective_output_ports` doesn't see user-config ports (Mark done validator looks at static-default port), #884 scistudio MCP `finish_ai_block` tool not surfaced to claude despite bridge starting. (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: hotfix/adr-035-pty-spawn-and-block-ui, session: 20260514-182017-hotfix-adr-035-pty-spawn-env-block-inlin)
- [#852] ADR-035 Phase 2.6 — fix audit P1 + P2 (5 P1 + 1 P2). Addresses all findings from `docs/audit/2026-05-14-1253-adr-035-implementation.md`: (P1-A) `AIBlock._build_spawn_argv` re-raises bootstrap failures so the block transitions to ERROR with "AIBlock bootstrap failed: …" instead of silently degrading argv; (P1-B) `_ensure_ipc_token()` is now invoked from the FastAPI lifespan in `api/app.py` so `SCISTUDIO_ENGINE_IPC_TOKEN` is exported BEFORE any AI Block worker subprocess inherits the env — prior every internal IPC call returned 401 and the entire AI Block path was dead-on-arrival; (P1-C) `pty_endpoint` now JOINs an engine-pre-spawned PTY (detected via the `_engine_block_run_id` sentinel set by `open_engine_initiated_tab`) instead of calling `_spawn` a second time and orphaning the original agent process; on first WS connect it replays the recorded `_engine_initial_stdin` exactly once via a stamped sentinel attribute; (P1-D) `useWebSocket.ts::block_pty_closed` reads the top-level `event` field (the actual wire shape) and maps `completed → done` / `cancelled_by_user_close → cancelled` / `error → error` — successful runs no longer render as red ✗; (P1-E) `api/ws.py` now handles `block_user_marked_done` and `block_user_cancel` inbound frames by writing `signals/mark_done.json` under the right run dir; new `_engine_run_to_run_dir` registry + `PtyTabSpec.run_dir_path` field let the WS layer resolve `block_run_id → run_dir` without leaking AI Block internals into `api/ws.py`; (P2-A) `useWebSocket.ts::block_pty_opened` reads `permission_mode` from the top level (matching the engine's emit shape) so bypass-mode tabs register as `dangerous` instead of silently downgrading to `safe`. Tests: 6 new pytest cases in `tests/api/test_ai_pty_audit_fixes.py` (P1-A through P1-E + unknown-rid robustness) + 4 new vitest cases in `frontend/src/hooks/useWebSocket.test.ts` (P1-D ×3 mappings + P2-A); `tests/engine/test_pty_control{,_skeleton}.py` dataclass-shape assertions updated to include the new `run_dir_path` field. (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: fix/adr-035-impl-audit-p1, session: 20260514-130035-f35-impl-fix-audit-p1-p2-adr-035)

- [#876] ProcessBlock output Collection no longer pinned to input item_type. `src/scistudio/blocks/process/process_block.py:166` previously forced `Collection(results, item_type=primary.item_type)`, which broke parent-typed outputs (e.g. SRSImage→Image transformations) by failing `Collection.__init__`'s strict isinstance check with `TypeError: Collection requires homogeneous types: item[0] is Image, expected SRSImage`. The bidirectional port-type fix (#601) only patched design-time `validate_connection`, not runtime Collection construction. Now infers item_type from the actual results; falls back to `primary.item_type` only when results is empty so the empty Collection still carries a meaningful type label for downstream port checks. Adds `TestProcessBlockOutputTypeInference` (2 cases: parent-type output accepted, empty input preserves input type). (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: fix/issue-876/process-block-collection-type-inference, session: 20260514-134618)
- [#851] ADR-036 Phase 2.6 — fix audit P1 findings (saveFileTab data-loss race + new-block/note silent overwrite). `saveFileTab` in `frontend/src/store/tabSlice.ts` used to snapshot the tab BEFORE the in-flight `putProjectFile` await and rebuild the FileTab from that stale reference post-await, silently overwriting any keystrokes the user made during the network round-trip. Now the post-await branch re-reads the latest tab from the store and only clears `dirty` if the content has not diverged; if the user typed mid-flight, `contentLoadedAt` advances (the older content really did land on disk) but `dirty=true` so the next debounce saves the newer content. New `frontend/src/lib/fileExistence.ts::probeProjectFileExistence` GETs the target path before PUT for `createNewCustomBlock` / `createNewNote` in `App.tsx`; 200 → alert + abort, 404 → safe to create, other errors surface to the user. P2 #6 (createNewNote silently falls back to project root on any error) also fixed in-PR — `getProjectTree("notes")` failures now branch on `ApiError.status === 404` only. P2 #3 (rehydrated tab stuck loading), #4 (multi-tab autosave debounce cancel), #5 (lint stale-response paint) deferred to backlog issues. Tests: 2 new vitest cases in `tabState.test.ts` exercise the race with a stalled `putProjectFile` mock + interleaved `updateFileTabContent`; 4 new cases in `fileExistence.test.ts` cover the existence probe (exists / missing / non-404 ApiError / network Error). (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: fix/adr-036-impl-audit-p1, session: 20260514-131100-f36-impl-phase-2-6-fix-audit-p1-p2)
- [#840] Live-test hotfix bundle for PR #834. (a) Canvas blank on workflow modify — `workflow_watcher` now suppresses transient `kind=deleted` events when the path still exists at emit time (atomic-replace artefact). (b) MCP `get_run_status.errors` was always `[]`; engine already emits full Python tracebacks on `block_error`, the MCP layer just wasn't surfacing them — now lazy-installs a `block_error` subscriber on the runtime's `event_bus` (exposed via 3-line `_RuntimeAdapter.event_bus` addition in `api/app.py`) and returns the captured records, with a `task.exception()` + `format_exception` fallback for scheduler-level failures. (c) Logs tab "N unread but panel empty" — `unreadLogsCount` was bumped for every `block_*`/`workflow_*` event but only `block_error` produced a Logs row; the badge is now coupled to the actual `appendLog`/`consumeEvent` row append in `executionSlice`. (d) Refactor: Problems tab collapsed into Logs (`LogViewer` already shipped a level selector). Drops `ProblemsPanel`, `unreadProblemsCount`, `bumpUnreadProblems`; keeps the `blockErrors` store field for the inline BlockNode error badge. (e) `write_workflow` MCP tool now pre-validates against `WorkflowFileModel` before writing so malformed YAML (e.g. agent-written 4-field edges) never lands on disk; the GET route surfaces 422 with the pydantic error list for any pre-existing bad files instead of 500. Engine + schema intentionally untouched per project policy. (@claude, 2026-05-14, branch: fix/adr-034/bugs-abc-canvas-traceback-logs, session: 20260514-005000-pr834-hotfix-bundle)
- [#810][#811] Restore mcp-bridge run() impl + MCP-spec content blocks. `cli/mcp_bridge.py::run()` now implements both attached-mode (proxy stdin↔backend socket) and standalone-mode (spawn in-process MCPServer via `runtime.make_mcp_runtime`); `mcp/server.py:233` returns spec-compliant `{"type": "text", "text": json.dumps(...)}` instead of non-spec `{"type": "json", ...}`. Both regressions were introduced by PR #808's rollback over-correction. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-810-811/mcp-bridge-and-content-block, session: 20260513-200156-fix-810-811-mcp-bridge-run-mcp-content-b)

(@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: chore/issue-809/post-rollback-cleanup-v2, session: 20260513-193032-phase-0-post-rollback-cleanup-re-dispatc)

### Added

- [#817] ADR-034 Phase 1.3 — Frontend xterm.js terminal. New `frontend/src/components/AIChat/` package: `SetupScreen` (provider + permission-mode picker reading `/api/ai/status`), `TerminalView` (xterm.js wrapper with fit/search/web-links addons), `TerminalTab` (setup→running→closed state machine), `TerminalTabs` (multi-tab strip with Ctrl+T / Ctrl+W / Ctrl+1..9 shortcuts, capture-phase listener so Ctrl+W beats Chrome's default), and `hooks/usePtyWebSocket` (locked JSON-frame protocol — `stdin` / `resize` outbound, `stdout` / `exit` / `error` inbound, no auto-reconnect). New Zustand `terminalTabsSlice` persists tab metadata across reloads; on rehydrate any `running` tab is downgraded to `closed` with synthetic `exitCode -1` since the PTY did not survive page unload. `BottomPanel` now mounts `<TerminalTabs/>` for the AI bottom tab; `App.tsx` drops the legacy chat plumbing (`chatMessages`, `aiLoading`, `aiError`, `onSendChat`, `onApplyWorkflow`). Legacy `AIChat.tsx` is left in place per Phase 1.3 scope — Phase 2 deletes it. 29 new vitest cases (`__tests__/SetupScreen.test.tsx`, `TerminalView.test.tsx`, `TerminalTabs.test.tsx`, `usePtyWebSocket.test.ts`) cover URL encoding, frame dispatch, disabled-Launch logic, "(not logged in)" hint, keyboard shortcuts, and rehydration downgrade. Backend Phase 1.2 lands in parallel; WS contract is locked identically in both. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: feat/issue-817/phase-1-3-frontend-terminal, session: 20260513-204242-adr-034-phase-1-3-frontend-xterm-js-term)
- [#813] ADR-035 draft — AI Block as PTY-tab variant of AppBlock. Rewrites AIBlock from a one-shot Messages-API call into a workflow-graph node that spawns a claude/codex agent inside an ADR-034 PTY tab. Three completion signals (MCP `finish_ai_block` + FileWatcher on declared `expected_path` + user "Mark done" button), input manifest at `.scistudio/ai-block-runs/{run_id}/manifest.json` (coordination dir, not a sandbox), outputs validated via existing IOBlock loader registry. Agent has full filesystem reach matching ADR-034 — no sandboxing per explicit user directive. Variadic ports reuse ADR-029; block UI mirrors ADR-034 Setup screen; tab survives DONE/ERROR and remains interactive. Implementation cascade (Phases 1-4) deferred to a separate ADR-035 ticket batch. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: docs/issue-813/adr-035-ai-block-draft, session: 20260513-200454-draft-adr-035-ai-block-as-pty-tab-appblo)
- [#788] Generic fallback renderer for AIChat — display_class taxonomy. Backend (`scistudio.ai.agent.stream_json.classify_for_display`) tags every `OtherEvent` with one of five stable classes (`hidden`, `meta`, `text-like`, `tool-like`, `raw`); frontend `EventRenderer` dispatches on the class instead of the legacy "Unrecognised event: <json>" fallback. New `genericRows/` folder with 4 small row components plus a reusable `<CondensedToolRow>` that #784 will also consume for native `tool_use` events. Adding a new claude stream-json kind now usually requires zero frontend changes — the structural heuristics (`text` / `content` / `tool_name+input`) handle it automatically. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: feat/issue-788/generic-fallback-renderer, session: 20260513-154519-implement-788-generic-fallback-renderer)
- [#787] Developer CLI integration — standalone `scistudio mcp-bridge` (auto-spins up an in-process MCP server when no backend is running, scoped to `$SCISTUDIO_PROJECT_DIR`/cwd, tear-down on stdin EOF); new `scistudio install` Typer subcommand wiring the MCP entry into Claude (`~/.claude.json` user / `<cwd>/.mcp.json` project) and Codex (`~/.codex/config.toml` `[mcp_servers.scistudio]`) plus a `--skill` install that copies `skills/scistudio/` into `~/.claude/skills/scistudio/`; new `skills/scistudio/SKILL.md` as the single source of truth for the embedded GUI agent's system prompt (`compose_system_prompt` now reads it, falling back to inline sections + warning on missing file, with the tool catalog always re-synthesised from the live registry); new `docs/cli-integration.md` linked from README. Verified live with the real `claude` CLI in a fresh project — claude called `mcp__scistudio__list_blocks` + `mcp__scistudio__get_project_info` via the standalone bridge and returned real data. Codex MCP entry verified via `codex mcp list` (status enabled). (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: feat/issue-787/dev-cli, session: 20260513-154325-implement-787-dev-cli-integration)

### Fixed

- [#793] Stop bottom panel from forcibly switching to the Logs tab on every engine event — `useWebSocket` no longer calls `setActiveBottomTab("logs")` when `block_*` / `workflow_*` arrive, and all `setActiveBottomTab` calls in `App.tsx` user-action callbacks (`runWorkflow`, `startFromSelected`, `handleRunBlock`, `handleRestartBlock` + their catch branches) were removed per user directive ("永远不要自动跳"). The two remaining switches are explicit user interactions: node-select goes to Config, error-badge click goes to Problems. To preserve "draw attention" UX, `uiSlice` gains `unreadLogsCount` / `unreadProblemsCount` counters that bump when events arrive while their tab is hidden; `BottomPanel` renders them as small badges next to the tab labels and clears them on activation. New tests in `useWebSocket.test.ts`, `BottomPanel.test.tsx`, `tabSlice.test.ts`. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-793-796/tab-routing, session: 20260513-161943-bundle-793-796-stop-auto-tab-switch-and)
- [#796] Restore workflow tab label and top-left title when YAML omits the `id:` field — `WorkflowModel.id` has an empty-string default in the backend schema, so a hand-edited or older workflow YAML missing `id:` round-tripped as `id: ""` and rendered a blank tab + blank top-left title (mostly hit on macOS where users edit YAML externally). `ProjectTree.handleDoubleClick` now passes the filename stem as a displayName fallback through `loadWorkflowById` to `openTab`; `tabSlice.openTab` accepts an optional displayName and prefers the workflow id, then displayName, then "Untitled"; `workflowSlice.setWorkflow` falls back to "Untitled" when id is empty. Macos live verification deferred to user; regression test `tabSlice.test.ts` reproduces the broken state-derivation path. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-793-796/tab-routing, session: 20260513-161943-bundle-793-796-stop-auto-tab-switch-and)
- [#790] MCP tool path resolution — `write_workflow`, `get_workflow`, `validate_workflow`, `update_block_config`, `get_block_config`, and `run_workflow` now resolve user-supplied path arguments against `ctx.project_dir` via the new `_resolve_project_path` helper in `src/scistudio/ai/agent/mcp/_context.py`. Previously these tools called `Path(<user_arg>)` raw, which resolved relative paths against the backend process's CWD and accepted absolute paths anywhere on disk — so workflows landed in random locations and `run_workflow` couldn't find what `write_workflow` had just written, and a malicious or buggy agent could escape the project with `../../etc/passwd`. Response envelopes now carry the absolute resolved path so the agent has unambiguous evidence of where its artifact landed. The resolution chain uses `os.path.realpath` via `Path.resolve` to handle macOS `/tmp → /private/tmp` symlinks and NFD/NFC Unicode normalisation. New `tests/ai/test_mcp_tools_disk_integration.py` adds 13 disk-state regression cases. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-790-791/mcp-paths-and-permission-mode, session: 20260513-155611-fix-790-791-mcp-path-permission-mode)
- [#791] AIChat permission_mode plumbing — the Settings panel Strict/Bypass dropdown was purely cosmetic: `useAgentWebSocket` never sent the value to the backend, and `_start_default_session` hardcoded `PermissionMode.BYPASS` regardless of the frontend setting (a Phase 5 e2e shortcut that was never reverted). STRICT mode was unreachable from the GUI; every tool call silently auto-approved. The fix adds a `?permission_mode=strict|bypass` query parameter to `WS /api/ai/chat/{chat_id}` (default STRICT), plumbs it through `_start_default_session` into `SessionMetadata.bypass_mode`, and has the frontend append the store-backed `permissionMode` to the WS URL. The Settings panel now shows a confirm dialog when changing mode mid-session (changing the store causes `useAgentWebSocket`'s effect to re-open the WS with the new mode). New `tests/api/test_strict_mode_write_workflow_e2e.py` pins the WS-to-metadata mode plumbing and the strict-mode `permission_request` emission. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-790-791/mcp-paths-and-permission-mode, session: 20260513-155611-fix-790-791-mcp-path-permission-mode)
- [#782] AIChat thinking + input UX — three related Phase 5 e2e bugs: (1) `thinking` events no longer fall through to the "Unrecognised event" branch — renderer now also catches wire frames with `raw.type === "thinking"` and shows an animated indicator (✻ Thinking…) even for empty-text / signature-only thinking frames; (2) new in-flight Thinking… indicator visible from user send until first real agent event (`assistant_text_delta` / `tool_use` / `tool_result` / `thinking` / `done` / `error`), so the chat no longer looks frozen while the agent is reasoning; (3) input textarea now bounded with `max-h-[200px] overflow-y-auto` so long messages scroll inside the textarea instead of pushing the Send button off-screen. Frontend-only fix; backend serialization already correct. Verified live in Chrome with claude-opus-4-7. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-782/aichat-thinking-and-input, session: 20260513-151107-fix-782-aichat-thinking-input-ux)
- [#775] Fix Claude subprocess launch — three coordinated bugs that prevented the agent from responding at all: stdin envelope schema (now `{type:user, message:{role,content}}` per Anthropic shape), missing `--input-format stream-json`, and bogus `@path` prefix on `--append-system-prompt` and `--mcp-config` (claude doesn't support `@file` indirection on those flags). Verified live in Chrome: agent now emits system/init → assistant → result. (@claude, 2026-05-13, branch: fix/issue-775/claude-launch, session: 20260513-001646-fix-775-claude-subprocess-launch-envelop)

Replace the live `selectionRef` with a one-shot `pendingSelectionRef` that is cleared at the end of every layout effect, so unrelated re-renders no longer snap the caret back to the stale post-edit position. Applied to both `BlockNode.InlineConfigField` and `BottomPanel.CaretPreservingTextInput`; new regression test in `BlockNode.test.tsx` (@claude, 2026-05-12, branch: fix/issue-710/inline-input-caret-jump, session: 20260512-190539-fix-inlineconfigfield-caret-jump-on-mid)

- [#331] T-TRK-012: `FilterCollection` block accepts a new `expression: str` config param parsed through an AST-whitelisted evaluator (new module `src/scistudio/blocks/process/builtins/expression_evaluator.py`). Expressions run against a per-item scope of `item`, `index`, `meta`, `framework`, `user`, plus a single whitelisted `len` call — no `eval()`, no trusted-mode bypass, no DSL. Forbidden constructs (arbitrary calls, imports, lambdas, dunder attribute/name access, non-literal subscripts, `BinOp`, `NamedExpr`) raise `ValueError("Expression contains forbidden construct: ...")` at parse time so workflow validation catches the error before the block runs. Legacy `predicate_key` / `predicate_value` equality match is preserved for backward compatibility and is mutually exclusive with `expression`. Tests: 18 unit tests for the evaluator (8 positive, 10 rejection) + 12 integration tests through `FilterCollection` including empty-Collection pass-through, dunder rejection, legacy path, and mutually-exclusive mode enforcement. Spec: `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` §T-TRK-012 lines 1800-1889. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: feat/issue-331/filter-collection-expression, session: 20260407-200431-t-trk-012-filtercollection-ast-whitelist)
- [#326] Frontend `BlockNode.tsx` consumes the ADR-028 Addendum 1 dynamic-port mechanism: replaced the three pre-ADR-028 hardcoded `blockType === "io_block"` checks with property-based discriminators (`data.category === "io"` for the Browse button on `path` config fields per Addendum 1 §C11; `data.category === "io"` for hiding the `direction` config field per Addendum 1 §B fix #2; `data.schema?.direction` instead of `data.config?.direction` for the file-vs-directory branch per Addendum 1 §C8). Added `frontend/src/utils/computeEffectivePorts.ts` — a pure-function helper that consumes the new `BlockSchemaResponse.dynamic_ports` descriptor + the current driving config value and returns per-instance effective ports so port colours auto-update via `resolveTypeColor()` as the user changes the dropdown (no backend round-trip; static blocks pay zero allocation cost via reference identity). Wired the helper into the input/output Handle render paths in `BlockNode.tsx` per spec §d step 4. Extended `frontend/src/types/api.ts` `BlockSchemaResponse` interface with `dynamic_ports?: DynamicPortsConfig | null` and `direction?: string | null` (mirroring the backend Pydantic fields T-TRK-006 added in PR #321) and defined the `DynamicPortsConfig` interface with strict types (`Record<string, Record<string, string[]>>`, no `any`). - [#323] Add `SaveData` block at `src/scistudio/blocks/io/savers/save_data.py` — the canonical core IO **output** block per ADR-028 Addendum 1 §C5/§C9. `SaveData(IOBlock)` carries `direction="output"`, `type_name="save_data"`, `category="io"`, a single `data` input port whose `accepted_types` is narrowed per-instance via `get_effective_input_ports()` against the `core_type` config enum, and a `dynamic_ports` descriptor that uses `input_port_mapping` (the symmetric mirror of LoadData's `output_port_mapping`). `SaveData.save()` dispatches to one of six private module-level functions per ADR-028 Addendum 1 §C9 (`_save_array`, `_save_dataframe`, `_save_series`, `_save_text`, `_save_artifact`, `_save_composite_data`) which absorb the write logic from the T-TRK-004-deleted `csv_adapter` / `parquet_adapter` / `zarr_adapter` / `generic_adapter`. Supported extensions: Array → `.npy` / `.npz` / `.zarr` / `.parquet` (1-D); DataFrame → `.csv` / `.tsv` / `.parquet` / `.json`; Series → `.csv` / `.tsv` / `.parquet` / `.json` (single-column); Text → `.txt` / `.md` / `.html` / `.xml` / `.log` / `.yaml` / `.toml` / `.json`; Artifact → raw bytes plus a `.meta.json` sidecar; CompositeData → JSON manifest plus per-slot sidecar files in a `<stem>_slots/` subdirectory. `allow_pickle=True` opt-in enables `.pkl` / `.pickle` writes for Array / DataFrame / Series with an explicit WARNING-level security log via `logging`. `SaveData.load()` raises `NotImplementedError` (output-only). Mixed-type Collections, multi-item Collections, empty Collections, and wrong-type-for-core-type inputs all raise `ValueError` per spec §j out-of-scope rule. The new `src/scistudio/blocks/io/savers/__init__.py` re-exports `SaveData` and `src/scistudio/blocks/io/__init__.py` adds it to `__all__`. Registered as `save_data = "scistudio.blocks.io.savers.save_data:SaveData"` under `[project.entry-points."scistudio.blocks"]` so it surfaces in the block palette. Test coverage: 53 new tests in `tests/blocks/io/test_save_data.py` covering class-shape invariants, parametrized `get_effective_input_ports`, end-to-end round-trip per core type via the underlying lib (pyarrow / numpy / json / pickle / zarr — independent of T-TRK-007 LoadData merge order), allow_pickle gate (default-rejects + opt-in writes + WARNING log), mixed-type Collection rejection, and the `SaveData.load() → NotImplementedError` contract. Per `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` T-TRK-008 (Sprint A Level B PR 4 of 5, parallel with T-TRK-007). (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: feat/issue-323/T-TRK-008-save-data-class, session: 20260407-185152-t-trk-008-savedata-class-6-private-save)
- [#323] Extend `BlockRegistry._validate_dynamic_ports` (`src/scistudio/blocks/registry.py`) to accept either `output_port_mapping` (LoadData / input-direction blocks) **or** `input_port_mapping` (SaveData / output-direction blocks). Exactly one of the two keys must be present per ADR-028 Addendum 1 §C5; declaring both raises `ValueError`. T-TRK-006 (PR #321) only declared the `output_port_mapping` branch because LoadData was the first dynamic-ports consumer; SaveData is the symmetric output-direction counterpart and must use `input_port_mapping` per spec line 1497 and the T-TRK-008 prompt's locked autonomy limit. Error-message paths now interpolate the actual mapping key so diagnostics still pinpoint the offending field. The 22 existing dynamic-ports tests in `tests/blocks/test_dynamic_ports.py` continue to pass without modification. Per `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` T-TRK-008. - [#322] Add `LoadData` class (`src/scistudio/blocks/io/loaders/load_data.py`) plus six private module-level dispatch functions (`_load_array`, `_load_dataframe`, `_load_series`, `_load_text`, `_load_artifact`, `_load_composite_data`). `LoadData` is the canonical core IO loader: a single dynamic-port block whose `data` `OutputPort` accepted-types are computed per-instance from the `core_type` enum config field via `get_effective_output_ports()`. Pickle is gated via `allow_pickle=False` default — `.pkl` / `.pickle` paths raise `ValueError` with a security message unless explicitly opted in, in which case a WARNING is logged before loading. - [#320] Add `Block.get_effective_input_ports()` and `Block.get_effective_output_ports()` instance methods on the `Block` ABC plus a new `dynamic_ports: ClassVar[dict[str, Any] | None]` declarative descriptor (default `None`). The two effective-ports methods default to a defensive copy of the class-level `input_ports` / `output_ports` ClassVars; dynamic blocks (e.g. the upcoming `LoadData` / `SaveData` from T-TRK-007 / T-TRK-008) override them to return per-instance ports computed from `self.config`. Per ADR-028 Addendum 1 D1, D2 and `docs/specs/phase11-implementation-standards.md` T-TRK-006 (Sprint A Level B PR 2 of 5, bundled with the framework read-path migration per master plan §4.3 Q3). The ClassVar carries a contract docstring describing the enum-only `{source_config_key, output_port_mapping: {port_name: {enum_value: [type_names]}}}` shape. - [#320] Extend `BlockSpec` (`src/scistudio/blocks/registry.py`) with two new dataclass fields: `direction: str = ""` (populated from the class-level `direction` ClassVar — `"input"` / `"output"` for IO blocks, empty string otherwise) and `dynamic_ports: dict[str, Any] | None = None` (the enum-driven dynamic-port descriptor copied verbatim from the class). `_spec_from_class` populates both fields via `getattr(cls, ...)`. Per ADR-028 Addendum 1 D3 and T-TRK-006. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: feat/issue-320/T-TRK-006-block-abc-dynamic-port-hooks, session: 20260407-182146-t-trk-006-block-abc-dynamic-port-hooks-f)
- [#320] Add `BlockRegistry._validate_dynamic_ports(cls)` static method that rejects malformed `dynamic_ports` dicts at scan time with descriptive `ValueError` messages. Validates: top-level dict shape, required `source_config_key` (non-empty string), required `output_port_mapping` (dict whose keys are non-empty port names, whose values are enum-value dicts mapping non-empty enum strings to non-empty lists of non-empty type-name strings). - [#323] `IOBlock.run()` output direction now wraps the path receipt in a single-item `Collection` of `Text` (`Collection(items=[Text(content=str(path))], item_type=Text)`) instead of returning a literal `dict[str, str]` under a `dict[str, Collection]` signature, removing the pre-existing `# type: ignore[dict-item]` suppression on `src/scistudio/blocks/io/io_block.py`. Verified zero production consumers of the old shape via grep: no `src/scistudio` code reads `result["path"]` from `IOBlock.run()` (the key has always been a write receipt for downstream observers, not a load-bearing data path). Master task-decomposition document for the Phase 11 plugin cascade — single source of truth for the skeleton agent and the 88 implementation agents that follow. Closes #305 (the v1 task-decomposition agent died silently after posting a change plan; v2 succeeds via aggressive context budgeting and chunked commit-as-you-go protocol). Defines 89 tickets across 4 tracks: Track 1 (15 T-TRK-* core block cleanup + ADR-028 implementation tickets, full per-ticket format with 13 subsections each), Track 2 (38 T-IMG-* imaging tickets, compact reference pointers to `phase11-imaging-block-spec.md`), Track 3 (15 T-SRS-* SRS tickets, compact reference pointers to `phase11-srs-block-spec.md`), Track 4 (21 T-LCMS-* LC-MS tickets, compact reference pointers to `phase11-lcms-block-spec.md`). Walks the full Phase 10-style standards document structure: §1 Purpose, §2 Scope (in-scope tracks + explicit out-of-scope ADR-029 freeze, plugin packages beyond imaging/SRS/LCMS, ARCHITECTURE.md scope cap, frontend refactor cap), §3 Cross-reference table, §4 Dependency graph (ASCII DAG of Sprint A0-A5/B/C0-C3/D0-D2/E0-E3 with parallel/sequential edges), §5 Recommended chained PR order, §6 Universal rules (workflow gate mandatory, branch naming `feat/issue-N/T-XXX-NNN-short`, stacked PR base, scope discipline, all-checks-green requirement, CHANGELOG attribution, PR body cross-references, **8 scope-violation red flags verbatim from master plan §5** as the audit-agent checklist, doc-external-changes restriction, branch base from origin/main, one-ticket-per-PR rule), §7 Universal acceptance criteria (10-item checklist), §8 Open questions resolved (12 implementation-phase decisions: Q1 branch+ticket numbering scheme, Q2 sub-1c parallelism, **Q3 PR-B coupling resolution that bundles original PR-B-1 and PR-B-2 into T-TRK-006** because splitting them leaves the codebase broken intermediate, Q4 single skeleton PR strategy, Q5 cross-plugin import pattern via `pytest.importorskip` + `imaging_types` session fixture, Q6 E2E test image constants in `tests/fixtures/test_images.py`, Q7 nine new pytest markers `requires_cellpose/napari/fiji/cellprofiler/qupath/r/elmaven/graphpad/lcms`, Q8 marker registration locations split between root and per-plugin pyproject.toml, **Q9 ADR-028 §D3 supersession anti-drift flag** for any imaging-spec reference to the now-removed six-loader structure, Q10 SRS canonical block count is 11 not 8, **Q11 ImageCalculator 2-port-fixed in 0.1.0** with variadic deferred to ADR-029, Q12 monorepo `testpaths` discovery in root pyproject.toml), §9 Per-ticket sections (Track 1 full format ~1430 lines, Tracks 2/3/4 compact ~1000 lines combined), §10 Summary table (one row per ticket with track/sprint/diff/deps/coupling), §11 E2E test plan (Phase 1 post-Sprint-D imaging+SRS pipeline using 4 K562 test images per master plan §8, Phase 2 post-Sprint-E full plugin set, Chrome GUI E2E via `mcp__Claude_in_Chrome__*`), §12 References. Five coupled ticket bundles documented: T-TRK-004 (delete adapters + rewrite io_block.py — must be atomic), T-TRK-006 (Block ABC dynamic-port hooks + framework migration — bundles PR-B-1+PR-B-2 per Q3), T-IMG-008/010/022/030/031/033 (geometry/axis/cleanup/projection/scalar/visualization 5-block bundles per imaging spec author's coupling judgment), T-LCMS-006 (LoadSampleMetadata + SaveTable), T-LCMS-007 (ElMAVENBlock + AccuCorR — shared marker registration). Three flagged inconsistencies between source docs: (1) the master plan §2.4 "~8 SRS blocks" estimate vs the SRS spec's actual 11 implementation blocks (resolved Q10 — spec is canonical), (2) potential imaging-spec residual references to the original ADR-028 §D3 six-loader structure (resolved Q9 — addendum supersedes), (3) ImageCalculator variadic ambition vs the ADR-029 freeze (resolved Q11 — fixed 2-port in 0.1.0). Ticket ID T-TRK-005 deliberately reserved-no-implement so that ticket numbering remains stable across this document, the master plan, and future PR descriptions. Document was written in 7 chunked commits with `git push` after each chunk per the v2 commit-as-you-go protocol (lessons from v1 silent death) — chunk 1 placeholder, chunk 2 §1-§8, chunk 3 §9.1 Track 1, chunk 4 §9.2 Track 2, chunk 5 §9.3 Track 3, chunk 6 §9.4 Track 4, chunk 7 §10-§12, plus this CHANGELOG entry. No source/test/frontend changes — docs-only. Enables the Phase 11 skeleton agent + the 88 per-ticket implementation agents. - [#301] Phase 11 LC-MS plugin block specification (`docs/specs/phase11-lcms-block-spec.md`, 3753 lines). Documentation-only spec authored per master plan §2.4 LC-MS PLUGIN lock. Defines the `scistudio-blocks-lcms` plugin package: 4 plain-DataFrame/Artifact types (`MSRawFile(Artifact)`, `PeakTable(DataFrame)`, `MIDTable(DataFrame)`, `SampleMetadata(DataFrame)` — **NO `MSSpectrum(Series)` or `MSRun(Array)`** per user), 19 blocks across 21 T-LCMS tickets: IO (5) `LoadMSRawFiles` / `LoadPeakTable` / `LoadMIDTable` / `LoadSampleMetadata` / `SaveTable`; external tools (2) `ElMAVENBlock` (AppBlock wrapping the user's ElMAVEN interactive desktop workflow per §8 Q-2 — no UI scripting, 30-min watch_timeout, FileWatcher picks up user exports) and `AccuCorR` (CodeBlock `language="r"` wrapping the AccuCor R package v0.3.1 via a bundled `accucor_default.R` driver script resolved via `importlib.resources` per §8 Q-1); isotope tracing USP cluster (5) `Calculate13CEnrichment` / `FractionalLabeling` / `CompareGroupMID` / `FluxEstimate` (simple `labeling_rate × pool_size` — explicitly NOT 13C-MFA per §8 Q-9) / `PoolSizeNormalize`; metabolomics analysis (6) `MetaboliteMatrix` / `MatrixPreprocess` / `UnivariateStats` / `MultivariateAnalysis` / `PathwayEnrichment` (Python-native KEGG REST default per §8 Q-6, MetaboAnalystR R wrapper deferred) / `ConsumptionSecretionAnalysis` (NEW per user, spent-vs-fresh media flux with optional cell count normalization per §8 Q-7); external plotting (1) `GraphPadBlock` (AppBlock wrapping GraphPad Prism, no default path per §8 Q-8, Windows-primary with non-Windows warning). Spec explicitly forbids adding scan-level data types, `EnumerateIsotopologues` / `MatchIsotopologues` / `ComputeMID` / `AtomPercentExcess` / `TimeCourseFit` / `TracerFateMap` (AccuCor does all of this externally), QC blocks, `ManualReview` blocks, MZmine / XCMS (user: "先实现 ElMAVEN"), and full 13C-MFA. MID long-format locked per §8 Q-3 (matches AccuCor output and the user's verbatim cytosine example). Sample-column detection heuristic per §8 Q-4 (`_KNOWN_IDENTITY_COLUMNS` ∪ `_KNOWN_ATOM_COLUMNS` exclusion with regex override). Multi-tracer support (`C13 + H2`) per §8 Q-5. Per §8 Q-11, no LC-MS block uses `dynamic_ports` — all four plugin types render via the existing `resolveTypeColor` walk with no frontend changes. 12 resolved open questions (§8 Q-1 through Q-12) capture every decision the spec agent owned beyond the master plan lock. 21 T-LCMS tickets each with the 12-subsection pattern matching `phase10-implementation-standards.md`: T-LCMS-001 scaffold, T-LCMS-002 types, T-LCMS-003..006 IO, T-LCMS-007 ElMAVEN+AccuCor, T-LCMS-008..012 isotope tracing (most-detailed cluster as the plugin USP — T-LCMS-008 `Calculate13CEnrichment` includes the Antoniewicz 2018 formula `E[c,s] = sum(n * M+n[c,s]) / n_max[c]` with the user's verbatim cytosine worked example), T-LCMS-013..018 metabolomics analysis, T-LCMS-019 GraphPad, T-LCMS-020 entry-point registration + smoke test, T-LCMS-021 isotope tracing integration test with synthetic fixtures (per master plan §8, LC-MS does NOT use the 4 imaging test images at Example/images/ — those are imaging/SRS only). Section §11 contains the full end-to-end integration test body chaining `LoadPeakTable` → `LoadMIDTable` → `LoadSampleMetadata` → `Calculate13CEnrichment` → `CompareGroupMID` → `MetaboliteMatrix` → `MatrixPreprocess` → `UnivariateStats` → `SaveTable` with no external-tool dependencies and no network calls. Package layout: `packages/scistudio-blocks-lcms/` with `pyproject.toml` declaring `scistudio.blocks` + `scistudio.types` entry-points, `scripts/accucor_default.R` as package data via `[tool.setuptools.package-data]`, and `requires_elmaven` / `requires_r` / `requires_graphpad` pytest markers for external-tool integration tests. Estimated total implementation size ~9,680 LOC across 21 stacked PRs. No ADR changes, no source/test changes — docs-only. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: docs/issue-301/phase11-lcms-spec, session: 20260407-011856-phase-11-lc-ms-plugin-block-specificatio)
- [#298] Phase 11 imaging plugin specification (`docs/specs/phase11-imaging-block-spec.md`, ~6200 lines). Documentation-only spec that codifies the contract for the `scistudio-blocks-imaging` plugin package and its 38 implementation tickets (T-IMG-001 through T-IMG-038), mirroring the structure of `docs/specs/phase10-implementation-standards.md`. Defines the four imaging types (`Image(Array)` 2D-to-6D with the t/z/c/lambda/y/x alphabet, `Mask(Image)` strict bool-dtype, `Label(CompositeData)` with raster+polygon slots, `Transform(Array)` for affine matrices), the unified `LoadImage`/`SaveImage` IO blocks (TIFF/PNG/JPG/NPY/Zarr first-class plus optional CZI/ND2/LIF extras, lazy loading at 128 MiB threshold, `SCISTUDIO:`-prefixed JSON-in-ImageDescription metadata protocol moved verbatim from OptEasy `tiff_adapter.py`), the flagship `CellposeSegment` block using `ProcessBlock.setup`/`teardown` to load the cellpose model ONCE per run (Q-IMG-2 CPU default, GPU auto-fallback, `torch.cuda.empty_cache()` in teardown), 12 preprocessing blocks (`Denoise`/`BackgroundSubtract`/`Normalize`/`FlatFieldCorrect`/`Rotate`/`Flip`/`Crop`/`Pad`/`Resize`/`ConvertDType`/`AxisSplit`/`AxisMerge` plus `Deconvolve` Phase 12 placeholder), 5 morphology blocks (`MorphologyOp`/`EdgeDetect`/`RidgeFilter`/`Sharpen`/`FFTFilter`), 8 segmentation blocks (`Threshold` with 8 methods, `Watershed`, `BlobDetect`, `ConnectedComponents`, the 5-block cleanup bundle), `TrackObjects` Phase 12 placeholder, 3 measurement blocks (`RegionProps` with multi-select properties param, `PairwiseDistance` for tumour-microenvironment analyses, `Colocalization`), 3 registration blocks (`ComputeRegistration`/`ApplyTransform`/`RegisterSeries`), `AxisProjection`+`SelectSlice`, 4 scalar math blocks plus `ImageCalculator` (with AST-whitelisted expression mode for FRET ratios; variadic deferred to ADR-029 per Q-IMG-5), 5 visualization blocks producing `Artifact` outputs, and 4 interactive AppBlocks (`FijiBlock` with the user's locked Windows Fiji path, `NapariBlock`, `CellProfilerBlock`, `QuPathBlock`). Twelve resolved open questions cover the TIFF metadata protocol location (Q-IMG-1), Cellpose CPU fallback (Q-IMG-2), metadata propagation under shape-changing transforms with `Resize` updating `pixel_size` (Q-IMG-3), `AxisSplit` filename derivation rule (Q-IMG-4), `ImageCalculator` 0.1.0 fixed-port subset (Q-IMG-5), `Mask` strict dtype enforcement via `_validate_extra` (Q-IMG-6), `Label` requires-at-least-one-slot rule (Q-IMG-7), `LoadImage` unsupported-extension behaviour with no fallback (Q-IMG-8), the `iterate_over_axes`-vs-direct-indexing rule (Q-IMG-9), the 128 MiB lazy threshold (Q-IMG-10), `SaveImage` length-1-vs-N path semantics (Q-IMG-11), and `RegionProps` Collection-input concatenation pattern (Q-IMG-12). Each ticket section follows the Phase 10 12-subsection contract: source ADR sections, files to create, files to modify, new tests (each ticket lists 5-15 specific test names), implementation details with code sketches, acceptance criteria checklist, out-of-scope notes, dependencies, diff size estimate, suggested workflow gate ticket title. Cross-reference table maps every ticket to ADR-027 / ADR-028 / Addendum 1 sections; dependency graph identifies the critical path (T-IMG-001 → T-IMG-002 → T-IMG-019); recommended chained PR order shows where parallel work is permitted. Universal rules section mirrors Phase 10 standards §4 with two added imaging-specific rules: optional dependencies declared in extras with `requires_<extra>` pytest markers, and metadata propagation per ADR-027 D5 mandatory. Universal acceptance criteria add a worker subprocess round-trip smoke test for every block. E2E test sketch in §11 covers the imaging-only sub-workflow against the four `K562_*_2845`/`K562_*_spectra` test images at `C:\Users\jiazh\Desktop\workspace\Example\images\` (with parens and spaces in filenames preserved verbatim per master plan §8) and acknowledges the cross-plugin extension where `ExtractSpectrum` (specified in `docs/specs/phase11-srs-block-spec.md`) consumes the masks plus the spectra branch. Block list, type definitions, package layout, entry-point registration, and all locked decisions per Phase 11 master plan §2.4 are documented verbatim — this spec makes ZERO architectural decisions, only records them. Enables the Phase 11 implementation cascade for the `scistudio-blocks-imaging` 0.1.0 release.
