- [#299] Phase 11 SRS plugin block specification — `docs/specs/phase11-srs-block-spec.md` (~1900 lines). Documentation-only spec defining the implementation contract for `scistudio-blocks-srs` per master plan §2.4 SRS PLUGIN. Locks one type (`SRSImage` subclassing imaging's `Image` with `required_axes = frozenset({"y","x","lambda"})` and a `Meta` model carrying `wavenumbers_cm1`, `laser_power`, `integration_time`, four digitizer parameters, and pump/Stokes wavelengths) and 11 blocks across three categories: 4 preprocessing (`SRSCalibrate` digitizer inversion + `Image→SRSImage` type conversion, `SRSBaseline` polynomial/rubber_band/rolling_ball_spectral, `SRSDenoise` PCA/SVD/wavelet/BM4D, `SRSNormalize` SNV/MSC/vector/area/peak_area), 5 component analysis (`SRSVCA` Vertex Component Analysis, `SRSUnmix` NNLS with auto-VCA fallback, `SRSPCA`, `SRSICA` FastICA, `SRSKMeansCluster`), 2 spectral extraction (`ExtractSpectrum` long-format DataFrame from Mask/Label ROIs, `BandRatio` two-band intensity ratio → 2D `Image`). No `RamanSpectrum` / `Spectrum` class — spectra are returned as plain `DataFrame`. No separate `LoadSRS` block — SRS ingress reuses imaging plugin's `LoadImage` then chains `SRSCalibrate`. Explicitly removed per user feedback: `SRSDespike` (no cosmic rays in SRS), `SRSWavenumberCalibrate` (systems pre-calibrated), `SRSMCR_ALS`, `SRSNMF`, `PeakFind`, `PeakFit`, all SRS-specific measurement blocks (`LipidDropletQuantify`, `ProteinLipidRatio`, `WaterContentMap`, `CellDryMassMap`), and any ALS-flavoured baseline correction. The spec walks the full Phase 10-style 12-subsection per-ticket pattern across 15 T-SRS tickets (T-SRS-000 package skeleton, T-SRS-001 type, T-SRS-002 through T-SRS-012 blocks, T-SRS-013 entry-point wiring, T-SRS-014 cross-plugin E2E test). Six open questions resolved: re-calibration detection via type+meta guards, lambda/c coexistence via `np.moveaxis` broadcast, `ExtractSpectrum` long format with `(region_id, wavenumber_cm1, intensity)` columns, `SRSUnmix` auto-VCA fallback when references absent, `SRSKMeansCluster` spectral feature shape, `SRSBaseline` default `polynomial` order=3. Cross-plugin dependency on `scistudio-blocks-imaging` declared one-way (srs imports imaging types; reverse forbidden). E2E integration test (T-SRS-014) consumes the four real test images at `Example/images/{K562_L_2845,K562_UL_2845,K562_L_spectra,K562_UL_spectra} (uV).tif` and exercises the full pipeline `LoadImage → Denoise → CellposeSegment → SRSCalibrate → ExtractSpectrum → SaveData`, gated behind `pytest.mark.requires_imaging`. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: docs/issue-299/phase11-srs-spec, session: 20260407-011711-phase-11-srs-plugin-spec-docs-specs-phas)
- [#297] ADR-029 preliminary: variadic port count and per-instance port editor (scope pending discussion). Reserves the ADR-029 namespace and documents the problem space for the count dimension of dynamic-port behaviour that ADR-028 Addendum 1 explicitly deferred. **Contains no architectural decisions** — every section that would normally hold a "Decision" reads "Pending discussion". The body documents the current state of `AIBlock` (30-line stub whose `run()` raises `NotImplementedError`, no port lists declared) and `CodeBlock` (163 lines, single static `data` input port and `result` output port both typed `DataObject`), explains why variadic ports are needed (concrete use cases: AI block taking N images and producing M tables, R-script ensemble averaging with variable fan-in, Python preprocessing fork with multiple typed outputs, future ensemble blocks), distinguishes the count dimension from Addendum 1's type dimension (fixed-count enum-driven types vs. variable-count user-declared types per port), and explains why the design discussion is being deferred until after the Phase 11 plugin cascade lands. Lists ten open questions Q1–Q10 each with 2–4 candidate answer directions A/B/C/D none of which are endorsed: Q1 where the variadic port list is stored (inline in `self.config`, new `self.port_config`, sidecar JSON, per-instance `BlockSpec`), Q2 how the GUI renders add/remove port controls (generic `variadic_port_list` widget, per-block React component, side panel, text-declared in script body), Q3 how validation handles variadic ports (treat user-declared like class-declared, fall back to `Any`, defer to runtime, hybrid structural-plus-runtime), Q4 how the scheduler routes through variadic ports (no change, per-dispatch effective-port read, special variadic dispatch path), Q5 how `_reconstruct_one` (worker subprocess) handles variadic ports given ADR-027 Addendum 1's typed reconstruction contract (per-port `type_chain` in payload, sidecar pre-resolved mapping, restrict to scan-time-resolvable types), Q6 whether AIBlock needs a `port_template` for the palette preview (zero ports, declared template, sentinel "+" badge, tooltip-only), Q7 whether CodeBlock auto-infers ports from script AST or user declares explicitly (manual editor only, Python AST auto-infer only, hybrid by language, side-load `block.yaml`), Q8 how `BlockSpec` represents a variadic block at scan time (single bool flag, separate input/output bools, capability enum, absence of port lists), Q9 whether variadic mode mixes with Addendum 1's enum `dynamic_ports` mapping (compose freely, mutually exclusive, compose with restrictions, defer), Q10 wire format for variadic ports in engine→worker payload (sidecar field, self-describing per-port metadata, CompositeData envelope). Scope statement enumerates what would be in scope (extensions to `get_effective_*_ports()`, frontend port editor widget, backend per-instance port storage, `BlockSpec` capability flag, validator updates, worker round-trip updates) once promoted plus what is explicitly out of scope (per-port auth, lazy port instantiation, runtime type inference, migration tooling, AI port suggestion). Adds `TODO(ADR-029)` paragraphs to `AIBlock` and `CodeBlock` class docstrings as forward pointers. Decision / Alternatives considered / Consequences sections all read "Pending discussion". Status `draft — scope pending discussion`. Hard freeze: any implementation PR that touches variadic AIBlock, variadic CodeBlock, or "add port" / "remove port" GUI controls must reference ADR-029 explicitly until it is promoted to `proposed`. ~739 lines appended to `docs/adr/ADR.md`. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: docs/issue-297/adr-029-preliminary, session: 20260407-011117-adr-029-preliminary-variadic-port-count)
- [#295] ADR-028 Addendum 1: Dynamic port override mechanism and GUI consequences. Documentation-only Addendum that introduces a minimal dynamic-port mechanism on the `Block` ABC (two override methods `get_effective_input_ports()` / `get_effective_output_ports()` + an enum-only declarative `dynamic_ports: ClassVar[dict | None]` mapping), locks the `BlockNode.tsx` GUI hardcoding removal (three `blockType === "io_block"` checks generalised to `category === "io"` plus Browse button generalisation), and **supersedes ADR-028 §D3** ("Seven core loader/saver pairs"): the six concrete loader/saver classes become two dynamic blocks `LoadData` and `SaveData` with twelve private module-level dispatch functions (`_load_array`, `_load_dataframe`, `_load_series`, `_load_text`, `_load_artifact`, `_load_composite_data`, and the symmetric `_save_*` set) in `load_data.py` / `save_data.py`. The user explicitly chose private functions over helper classes (Q-B) and enum-only mapping over a mini-DSL (Q-A). AI variadic port count and CodeBlock variadic port count are explicitly out of scope and deferred to ADR-029 (preliminary). Nine discussion-point decisions D1'–D9' (with prime marks to distinguish from ADR-028's D1–D14), four rejected alternatives (no dynamic mechanism, hidden classes with meta-palette, Pydantic discriminated union, combined variadic in same addendum). Detailed impact scope enumerates 7 backend files to modify, 4 backend files to create, 2 frontend files to modify, 5 test files to create, and an explicit "not affected" list covering Phase 10 core types / engine / other block bases / ADR-027 Addendum 1 worker reconstruction contract. Framework read-path migration: `Block.validate()`, `ProcessBlock.run()`, `workflow/validator.py`, `api/routes/blocks.py` all switch from `type(block).input_ports` to `block.get_effective_*_ports()`. Plugin IO blocks (`LoadImage`, `LoadMSRawFile`, etc.) remain static and get port colours via the existing `resolveTypeColor()` type-hierarchy walk — no per-plugin frontend work. 591 lines appended to docs/adr/ADR.md. (@claude, 2026-04-07, branch: docs/issue-295/adr-028-addendum-1-dynamic-ports, session: 20260407-005014-adr-028-addendum-1-dynamic-ports-overrid)
- [#293] ADR-028: IOBlock architectural refactor — plugin-owned IO pattern. Documentation-only ADR that records the Phase 11 decision to delete the central adapter registry and refactor `IOBlock` into an abstract base class whose concrete subclasses are per-type loaders/savers. The eight bundled adapters are redistributed: `csv`/`parquet`/`zarr`/`generic` merge into core `LoadDataFrame`/`LoadArray`/`LoadArtifact` implementations; `tiff`/`mzxml`/`h5ad`/`fcs` move verbatim to their target plugin packages (`scistudio-blocks-imaging`, `scistudio-blocks-lcms`, future `scistudio-blocks-singlecell`, future `scistudio-blocks-flow`). Core ships seven concrete loader/saver pairs (Array/DataFrame/Series/Text/Artifact/CompositeData; bare DataObject has no loader). The `scistudio.adapters` entry-point group is deleted (ADR-025 §6 superseded); plugins register IO blocks via the existing `scistudio.blocks` entry-point group. Pickle support is first-class but opt-in via `allow_pickle: bool = False` on LoadDataFrame/LoadSeries/LoadArray with an explicit security warning. Additional first-class format paths added: `.tsv`, `.pkl`, `.pickle`, `.npy`, `.npz`, `.parquet` for single-column Series. 14 discussion-point decisions D1–D14 plus four rejected alternatives (retrofit adapter with type_chain, subclass_of ClassVar, gradual deprecation, unified TypeRegistry-reader graph). Detailed impact scope enumerates 13 files to delete, 3 files to rewrite, 14 files to create, 9 documentation files to update in follow-up PRs, and explicit "not affected" list covering core types / engine / other block bases. Migration guide for workflow YAML files (`IOBlock(format=...)` → specific loader blocks). Enables Phase 11 Track 2 (scistudio-blocks-imaging), Track 3 (scistudio-blocks-srs), Track 4 (scistudio-blocks-lcms). 752 lines appended to docs/adr/ADR.md. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: docs/issue-293/adr-028-ioblock-refactor, session: 20260406-233129-adr-028-ioblock-architectural-refactor-a)
- [#251] Stage 10.1 Part 1: Palette research, skeleton, and design doc — adds category ClassVar on Block, source/package_name fields on BlockSummary (with safe defaults), optional source?/package_name? on TS type, TODO markers in _infer_category/_summary/BlockPalette.tsx, and 13 skipped test stubs for Agent B to implement in Part 2; includes docs/design/stage-10-1-palette.md (661 lines) with current state analysis, proposed changes, test plan, and migration notes (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-251/stage-10-1-skeleton, session: 20260406-015803-stage-10-1-part-1-research-skeleton-and)
- [#290] T-014: worker subprocess typed reconstruction per ADR-027 D11 + Addendum 1 §1. Replaces the T-013 stub in `scistudio.core.types.serialization` with full `_reconstruct_one` and `_serialise_one` implementations: each delegates to the resolved class's `_reconstruct_extra_kwargs` / `_serialise_extra_metadata` classmethod hooks (T-013) for base-class-specific fields, populates the framework/meta/user three-slot model (T-005), and uses `TypeRegistry.resolve(type_chain)` (T-012) to look up the most specific registered class. `worker.reconstruct_inputs` and `worker.serialise_outputs` are refactored to delegate per-item to the new helpers, returning TYPED `DataObject` instances (not `ViewProxy`) so block authors can use `item.meta`, `item.with_meta()`, and `isinstance` checks naturally inside their subprocesses. Lazy loading is preserved at the method level: reconstructed instances have `storage_ref` set but do not read payload data until `to_memory()` / `view()` / `sel()` / `iter_over()` is called. `worker.main()` warms a module-level lazy `TypeRegistry` singleton (`_get_type_registry` in `serialization.py`) on startup that scans core built-ins via `scan_builtins()` and attempts plugin entry-points via `_scan_entrypoint_types()` inside a `contextlib.suppress(Exception)` so a broken plugin never takes down core reconstruction. The `ViewProxy` import is removed from `worker.py`; `ViewProxy` remains as the return type of `Array.view()` for blocks that need explicit chunk-by-chunk reading. Construction failures inside `_reconstruct_one` are wrapped with the offending class name (`"Failed to reconstruct {cls.__name__} from payload: {original_error}"`) so operators can locate broken payloads quickly. 38 new tests in `tests/engine/test_worker_typed_reconstruction.py` covering `_reconstruct_one` class resolution (type_chain fallback, Meta validation, framework round-trip, user dict preservation), `_serialise_one` metadata sidecar shape, round-trip equivalence for all six base classes (Array / Series / DataFrame / Text / Artifact / CompositeData), `reconstruct_inputs` dispatcher cases (single typed item, Collection, scalar pass-through), `serialise_outputs` round-trip, reconstructed-instance behaviour (with_meta, isinstance, lazy payload), the TypeRegistry singleton helper, and construction-failure error wrapping. `tests/core/test_base_class_reconstruction_hooks.py` deletes the four T-013 stub-raises tests (`test_composite_reconstruct_raises_until_t014`, `test_composite_serialise_raises_until_t014`, `test_serialization_stub_reconstruct_raises`, `test_serialization_stub_serialise_raises`) and replaces them with positive composite round-trip tests plus smoke tests for the real `_reconstruct_one` / `_serialise_one` bodies on bare `DataObject`. `tests/engine/test_worker.py` and `tests/engine/test_local_runner.py` are updated where they asserted `ViewProxy` return types to assert the typed class instead (`Array` for the imaging-shaped payload, `DataObject` for the bare fallback). Capstone of Phase 10 — every previous ticket (T-001..T-013) was preparing for this moment. Stacked on PR #289. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-290/T-014-worker-typed-reconstruction, session: 20260406-201435-t-014-worker-subprocess-typed-reconstruc)
- [#288] T-013: six base-class reconstruction hook pairs per ADR-027 Addendum 1 §2. Each of DataObject, Array, Series, DataFrame, Text, Artifact, CompositeData gains a `_reconstruct_extra_kwargs(metadata: dict) -> dict` classmethod (returns the constructor kwargs to extract from the wire-format metadata sidecar) and a `_serialise_extra_metadata(obj) -> dict` classmethod (the symmetric counterpart that writes into the sidecar). DataObject returns empty dicts by default; Array extracts `axes`/`shape`/`dtype`/`chunk_shape` (tuples↔lists, dtype stringified); Series extracts `index_name`/`value_name`/`length`; DataFrame extracts `columns`/`row_count`/`schema`; Text extracts `content`/`format`/`encoding`; Artifact extracts `file_path` (Path↔str)/`mime_type`/`description`; CompositeData recursively delegates to `_reconstruct_one` / `_serialise_one` from a new `scistudio.core.types.serialization` module via lazy import inside the classmethod body to break the load-time cycle. The `serialization` module is a T-013 stub whose `_reconstruct_one` / `_serialise_one` raise NotImplementedError with a pointer to T-014; T-014 lands the full worker reconstruction logic, replacing the stub bodies while keeping the signatures locked. Composite empty-slots paths short-circuit before touching the stub, so T-013 ships without breaking plugin tests that construct an empty composite. Subclass overrides type their `obj` parameter as `DataObject` (not the narrower subclass) to respect Liskov with the base classmethod and assert-narrow inside the body. 39 new tests in `tests/core/test_base_class_reconstruction_hooks.py` covering per-class kwargs extraction, per-class metadata emission, round-trip equivalence on the five flat base classes, composite stub-raises delegation, serialization module importability, parametrized hook discovery on all seven classes, and the plugin-subclass `super()` override chaining pattern. Stacked on PR #287. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-288/T-013-base-class-reconstruction-hooks, session: 20260406-195928-t-013-base-class-reconstruction-hooks-pe)
- [#286] T-012: TypeRegistry.resolve(type_chain) and Meta-class validation per ADR-027 D11 + Addendum 1 §3. resolve() is overloaded on argument type: passing a list[str] walks the chain rightmost-to-leftmost and returns the most specific registered class (or None) — used by worker subprocess reconstruction (T-014) to look up typed DataObject classes from serialised metadata; the legacy resolve(name: str) -> TypeSpec path is preserved for backward compatibility with existing callers (load_class, tests/core/test_types.py, tests/architecture/test_registries.py). _validate_meta_class() runs at registration time inside scan_builtins and _scan_entrypoint_types and rejects any subclass whose Meta is not a pydantic.BaseModel subclass, declares PrivateAttr fields, or fails JSON round-trip through model_dump(mode='json') / model_validate, with clear error messages pointing at the offending class. Meta classes whose required fields have no defaults skip the round-trip smoke test per the ADR (plugin authors are expected to write their own regression test). Broken plugin Meta is logged-and-skipped inside _scan_entrypoint_types so one bad plugin does not take down the whole registry; broken core-builtin Meta raises loudly inside scan_builtins. A new register_class(cls) convenience helper validates + builds a TypeSpec + registers in one call. All six core base classes (Meta=None per T-005) pass validation via a canary test that guards against future refactors. 19 new tests in tests/core/test_type_registry_resolve_and_meta.py. Stacked on PR #285. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-286/T-012-type-registry-resolve, session: 20260406-194916-t-012-typeregistry-resolve-meta-validati)
- [#284] T-011: scistudio.utils.axis_iter.iterate_over_axes(source, operates_on, func) utility per ADR-027 D3. Iterates user-provided func over all axes NOT in operates_on, calls func(slice_data, coord_dict) for each combination, stacks results back into a new Array of source's concrete class. Memory: O(one input slice + one output slice). Serial by design (no threads, no subprocesses) per ADR-027 D8. Metadata propagation: framework derived (with `derived_from=source.framework.object_id`), meta shared by reference, user shallow copy, axes preserved. Raises `BroadcastError` when operates_on is not a subset of source.axes, when source.shape is None, when slice outputs have inconsistent shapes, or when func returns arrays with a different number of dimensions than len(operates_on); user-raised errors propagate unchanged. Imports `BroadcastError` from the sibling `scistudio.utils.broadcast` module (ADR-027 D3 referenced `scistudio.core.exceptions` which does not yet exist in the repo) so one `except BroadcastError:` clause covers both utilities. Sibling of `broadcast_apply` for the "single Array, iterate extra dims" pattern. Replaces the T-011 `NotImplementedError` skeleton from PR #262; removes the corresponding smoke tests from `tests/core/test_phase10_skeleton.py`; adds 16 per-feature tests in `tests/utils/test_axis_iter.py` covering the ADR-027 D3 acceptance criteria plus edge cases (empty extra axes, func reducing dim count, subclass preservation, metadata propagation, user-func error propagation). Stacked on PR #283. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-284/T-011-axis-iter, session: 20260406-193821-t-011-scistudio-utils-axis-iter-iterate-ov)
- [#282] T-010: scistudio.utils.constraints port helper factories per ADR-027 D4 companion. Adds `has_axes(*required)` (superset check), `has_exact_axes(*axes)` (set equality), `has_shape(ndim)` (exact rank), `has_min_shape(ndim)` (minimum rank), `has_dtype(*dtypes)` (string-normalised dtype match), and `is_2d()` / `is_3d()` convenience aliases. Each factory returns a `Callable[[Collection], bool]` suitable for `InputPort(constraint=...)` — pure Python predicates that read instance attributes only, with no I/O, no `to_memory()` calls, and no storage-backend coupling (consistent with Phase 10 Level 1 laziness). Every returned callable iterates the collection once, short-circuits on first failure, treats missing attributes as a graceful `False` (not `AttributeError`), treats empty iterables as vacuously true, and carries a descriptive `__name__` / `__doc__` for `validate_port_constraint` breadcrumbs. Replaces the T-010 `NotImplementedError` skeleton from PR #262; removes the corresponding smoke tests from `tests/core/test_phase10_skeleton.py`; adds 31 per-feature tests in `tests/utils/test_constraints.py` including end-to-end integration through `InputPort` + `validate_port_constraint`. Stacked on PR #281. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-282/T-010-utils-constraints, session: 20260406-192835-t-010-scistudio-utils-constraints-per-adr)
- [#280] T-009: ProcessBlock setup/teardown lifecycle hooks per ADR-027 D7. New `setup(config)` method runs once per `run()` before iterating the input Collection and returns opaque state. New `teardown(state)` method runs in a finally block even on exception so blocks can release resources (close DB handles, free GPU memory). `process_item` signature gains an optional third parameter `state` (default `None`) that is threaded from `setup` through every per-item call to `teardown`. The default `run()` calls setup once, iterates with `state`, and calls teardown via try/finally. Backward-compat: pre-T-009 `process_item(self, item, config)` overrides continue to work because `run()` uses `inspect.signature` (`_process_item_takes_state`) to detect the override's arity and calls with 2 or 3 args accordingly. Built-in `TransformBlock` (the only built-in that overrides `process_item`) is updated to the new 3-arg form; other built-ins override `run()` directly and are unaffected. Cellpose-style heavy blocks can now load their model once per run instead of per item. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-280/T-009-process-block-lifecycle, session: 20260406-191910-t-009-processblock-setup-teardown-hooks)
- [#269] T-004: FrameworkMeta + scistudio.core.meta module per ADR-027 D5. FrameworkMeta is a frozen Pydantic v2 BaseModel populated at DataObject construction with `created_at` (UTC), `object_id` (UUIDv4 hex), `source`, `lineage_id`, and `derived_from`; its `derive(**changes)` method implements the ADR-027 D5 propagation rule. ChannelInfo is a frozen Pydantic BaseModel for plugin Meta classes describing acquisition channels (`name`, `dye`, `excitation_nm`, `emission_nm`); lives in core so plugins compose it without forcing plugin->plugin imports. `with_meta_changes(meta, **changes)` is the free-function helper backing `DataObject.with_meta()`, which lands in T-005. The Phase 10 skeleton's NotImplementedError placeholders in `src/scistudio/core/meta/` are replaced with the real implementation; the corresponding T-004 smoke tests in `tests/core/test_phase10_skeleton.py` are removed and superseded by 22 unit tests in the new `tests/core/test_framework_meta.py`. Stacked on PR #262 (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-269/T-004-framework-meta, session: 20260406-174408-t-004-frameworkmeta-scistudio-core-meta-mo)
- [#267] T-003: PhysicalQuantity dataclass with Pydantic v2 integration per ADR-027 D6 + Addendum 1 §4. Frozen dataclass holding (value, unit) with kind-aware `to()` conversion, ordering, and equality. Pydantic BaseModel fields can declare `pixel_size: PhysicalQuantity` directly; round-trips through `model_dump_json` / `model_validate_json` as `{"value": ..., "unit": ...}`. Covers length, time, frequency, wavenumber kinds. - [#273] T-006: Array now uses instance-level axes per ADR-027 D1 — `axes` is a required keyword-only constructor argument carrying the axis labels (e.g., `["t", "z", "c", "lambda", "y", "x"]` for 6D fluorescence/spectral imaging). Class-level schema fields `required_axes` (frozenset), `allowed_axes` (frozenset | None), and `canonical_order` (tuple) let subclasses constrain the accepted axis sets without subclassing per dimensional combination. Adds `Array.sel(**kwargs)` and `Array.iter_over(axis)` per ADR-027 D4 with Level 1 laziness (one slice per iteration step, metadata preserved per ADR-027 D5). Overrides `DataObject.with_meta()` to propagate Array-specific constructor kwargs (axes/shape/dtype/chunk_shape). `TypeSignature.from_type()` now captures `required_axes` for Array subclasses with a non-empty schema so port-level compatibility checks can enforce axis requirements (ADR-027 D1). REMOVES `Image`, `MSImage`, `SRSImage`, `FluorImage` from core per ADR-027 D2 — these now live in the `scistudio-blocks-imaging` plugin. Internal call sites in `tiff_adapter.py` and `api/runtime.py` migrated to use `Array(axes=...)` directly; `TypeRegistry.scan_builtins` no longer registers the removed subtypes. Non-core test files that imported `Image` carry a T-008 shim (`from scistudio.core.types.array import Array as Image`) so collection stays green until T-008 lands the proper migration; `tests/core/` is fully migrated in this PR. (@claude, 2026-04-06, branch: feat/issue-273/T-006-array-6d-axes, session: 20260406-181626-t-006-array-6d-instance-level-axes-per-a)
- [#271] T-005: DataObject metadata is now stratified into three slots per ADR-027 D5: `framework` (FrameworkMeta, immutable framework-managed), `meta` (typed Pydantic BaseModel, None on the base class, overridden by plugin subtypes via the new `Meta` ClassVar), and `user` (free-form JSON-serialisable dict). Adds `with_meta(**changes)` instance method that returns a new instance with updated meta and a freshly-derived FrameworkMeta (`derived_from = self.framework.object_id`). Backward-compat: `DataObject.metadata` property and `DataObject(metadata=...)` constructor kwarg both still work and emit DeprecationWarning; both removed in Phase 11. Subclasses with extra `__init__` parameters (Array, CompositeData) must override `with_meta` themselves — T-006/T-007 own those overrides. - Phase 4 — Block system implementation:
  - Port system: type matching (isinstance-based, inheritance-aware), constraint validation, connection validation (source→target compatibility)
  - Block lifecycle: validate() with port type/constraint checking, postprocess() pass-through, state machine with transition()
  - IOBlock: read/write via AdapterRegistry with direction config
  - ProcessBlock: base with algorithm ClassVar; MergeBlock (Arrow concat), SplitBlock (head/ratio/filter)
  - CodeBlock: inline and script modes with MEMORY/PROXY/CHUNKED delivery
  - PythonRunner: exec() for inline, importlib for script with mtime-based hot-reload safety
  - introspect_script(): AST-based run() signature and configure() schema extraction
  - R/Julia runners: helpful NotImplementedError stubs
  - AppBlock: full lifecycle with RUNNING→PAUSED→RUNNING→DONE state transitions
  - FileExchangeBridge: prepare (JSON manifest), launch (subprocess), watch, collect
  - FileWatcher: polling-based output detection with timeout and glob patterns
  - SubWorkflowBlock: input/output mapping with sequential executor stub (real DAG scheduler in Phase 5)
  - BlockRegistry: Tier 1 (drop-in .py scan) + Tier 2 (entry_points) discovery, instantiate(), hot_reload()
  - AdapterRegistry: extension→adapter mapping with register_defaults() and entry_point scan
  - RunnerRegistry: language→runner mapping with register_defaults()
  - Format adapters: CSV (PyArrow), Parquet (PyArrow), TIFF (tifffile), generic binary (Artifact)
  - Stub adapters: mzXML, H5AD, FCS with NotImplementedError
  - 69 new tests across 7 test files covering ports, IO, process, code, app, registry, and subworkflow blocks
- CI: test coverage enforcement at 65% minimum via pytest-cov (will increase to 85% as test suite grows)
- CI: PR gate check requiring tests/ updates when src/ changes

- Phase 3 — Core data layer implementation:
  - DataObject metadata handling, TypeSignature auto-generation from class MRO
  - TypeSignature.matches() for inheritance-aware type compatibility
  - CompositeData slot management with type validation (get, set, slot_types)
  - TypeRegistry with register, resolve, scan_builtins, load_class, is_instance
  - ZarrBackend — write/read numpy arrays via Zarr, chunk-aware slicing
  - ArrowBackend — write/read PyArrow Tables via Parquet, column selection
  - FilesystemBackend — text and binary file storage with byte-range slicing
  - CompositeStore — directory-of-slots with manifest.json
  - ViewProxy — lazy loading with shape/axes metadata, size warnings (>2 GB)
  - LineageStore — SQLite-backed lineage records with ancestor tracing
  - EnvironmentSnapshot.capture() — Python version and key package versions
  - ProvenanceGraph — in-memory ancestry, descendant, diff, and audit queries
  - broadcast_apply() — named-axis-aware broadcasting utility
  - iter_axis_slices() — axis-aware slice generator for Array types
  - content_hash() — xxhash-based content hashing for lineage
  - 102 tests covering types, composites, storage round-trips, proxy lazy loading, lineage, and broadcast
- [#9] Scaffold repository structure and implement interface skeleton (Phases 0-2)
- [#7] Add mandatory branch and PR commit rules to CLAUDE.md
- Workflow gate system (`.workflow/gate.py`) for enforced development pipeline
- SpecKit integration (`.specify/`) for feature-level design pipeline
- GitHub Actions CI: lint, typecheck, test matrix, import contracts
- GitHub Actions workflow gate check for PR compliance
- Issue templates (feature, bug, refactor, architecture)
